# math.QA [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Defects in skein theory and TQFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07432)
*Patrick Kinnear,Ingo Runkel*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文将纽结流形（skein module）的定义推广至边界含有线缺陷和点缺陷网络的3维流形，并证明在半单数据标记下，该缺陷纽结流形与Carqueville-Runkel-Schaumann构造的缺陷Reshetikhin-Turaev拓扑量子场论（TQFT）中边界态空间同构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典纽结流形仅考虑边界点缺陷情形，缺乏对更一般缺陷结构（线缺陷+点缺陷网络）的统一定义；同时，缺陷拓扑量子场论（defect TQFT）中的缺陷数据仅限于半单情形，其与纽结流形之间的对应关系尚未被系统建立。

Method: 通过全局化模范畴（module categories）及其函子的图形演算（graphical calculus），将经典纽结流形定义自然推广至含边界线缺陷和点缺陷网络的3维流形，从而得到缺陷纽结流形（defect skein module）。

Result: 当所有缺陷由半单数据标记时，缺陷纽结流形与Carqueville-Runkel-Schaumann构造的缺陷Reshetikhin-Turaev TQFT中边界态空间同构；该构造还能涵盖缺陷TQFT中超出半单情形的一般缺陷数据。

Conclusion: 缺陷纽结流形为连接经典纽结理论（knot theory）与缺陷拓扑量子场论提供了统一框架，并自然扩展到非半单缺陷数据，拓展了现有缺陷TQFT的理论适用范围。

Abstract: Given a 3-manifold $M$ with a network of line and point defects in its boundary, we define the skein module of this configuration, generalizing the well-studied case of 3-manifolds which only admit point defects in the boundary. We prove that when all defects are labelled by semisimple data, our skein module is isomorphic to the state space of $\partial M$ in the defect version of the Reshetikhin-Turaev TQFT constructed by Carqueville-Runkel-Schaumann. Our defect skein modules follow naturally by globalizing the graphical calculus of module categories and functors thereof, and generalize the possible defect data considered in the defect TQFT beyond the semisimple case.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.HE'></div>

# astro-ph.HE [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Trapped fireshell (halo) of photons and pairs around black-hole horizon: source for ultra-high-energy particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03702)
*She-Sheng Xue*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文研究了强辐射力在温度超过电子质量且空间不均匀的致密光子和电子-正电子对火壳（fireshell）中加速电子的康普顿-火箭效应（Compton-rocket effect），发现带电粒子加速与雪崩逃逸过程可产生超高能（UHE）电子和质子，进而产生甚高能（VHE）光子和中微子。通过一维简化模型，以伽马射线暴中心引擎为例展示了该动力学过程，计算了随时间变化的UHE粒子光度，并讨论了其与数值模拟、观测及实验的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在具有空间不均匀温度分布的高密度光子-电子-正电子对火壳中，强辐射力（康普顿-火箭效应）能否有效加速带电粒子并引发雪崩逃逸过程，从而解释超高能粒子与甚高能辐射的产生机制。

Method: 采用简化的一维模型（one-dimensional model），以伽马射线暴（Gamma-Ray Burst, GRB）中心引擎为具体背景，定性分析火球（fireball）内部物质内流并在黑洞视界（horizon）附近形成引力束缚的火壳结构，进而考察该火壳通过超高能粒子发射和黑体辐射（blackbody radiation）进行冷却的动力学过程。

Result: 发现了带电粒子加速与雪崩逃逸过程的可行性，可产生超高能电子和质子，并随后产生甚高能光子和中微子。计算了随时间变化的超高能粒子光度（luminosity），并指出该火壳处于亚稳态（metastable）。

Conclusion: 从理论上论证了康普顿-火箭效应在极端天体物理环境中产生超高能粒子的可能性，强调了该机制与相关数值模拟、天文观测及地面实验之间进行交叉验证的潜在价值。

Abstract: We study the Compton-rocket effect of strong radiation force accelerating electrons in an opaque fireshell (or fire spot) of dense photons and electron-positron pairs, whose temperature is spatially inhomogeneous and exceeds the electron mass. We find the possibility of the charged-particle acceleration and the avalanche runaway process, leading to a non-trivial probability of ultra-high-energy (UHE) electrons and protons, which subsequently produce very-high-energy (VHE) photons and neutrinos. In a simplified one-dimensional model, we qualitatively show such peculiar dynamics using the fireball, Gamma-Ray Burst central engine, whose inner part inflows and forms a gravitationally trapped fireshell (halo) around the horizon of a black hole. The fireshell is metastable, cooling via UHE particle emissions and blackbody radiation. We calculate the UHE particle luminosity varying in time, and discuss the peculiar features of such produced UHE particles, which lead to VHE particles, in connection with possible numerical simulations, observations and experiments.

</details>


### [3] [Tidal Disruption of Blanets in Kerr Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06884)
*Shreesham Pandey,Sunita Singh*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文研究了活动星系核（AGN）环核盘中围绕超大质量黑洞（SMBH）运行的类行星天体（blanet）的潮汐瓦解事件（TDE），推导了其瓦解判据、潮汐半径和Hills质量，并分析了其吸积回落率、轨道稳定性、相对论修正以及引力波辐射探测前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的潮汐瓦解事件（tidal disruption event, TDE）研究主要针对恒星，对于活动星系核（AGN）环核盘中可能存在的类行星质量天体（blanet）的潮汐瓦解行为尚缺乏系统分析。

Method: 利用测地偏离方程（geodesic deviation equation）与Kerr潮汐张量（Kerr tidal tensor），从试验粒子极限到大质量行星体，在Kerr时空中推导了类行星天体的瓦解判据、潮汐半径（tidal radius）和Hills质量（Hills mass），并分析了其轨道稳定性，包括开普勒进动、Lense–Thirring节点进动、环核盘迁移及Kozai–Lidov共振。

Result: Blanet潮汐瓦解事件对于质量高达约10^10倍太阳质量（M⊙）的SMBH仍然可观测，显著高于恒星Hills质量（约10^8 M⊙）；其回落率（fallback rate）仍遵循t^{-5/3}形式，但峰值时标更短（数小时至数月），峰值吸积率更低，且多波段特征与恒星TDE不同；同时给出了潮汐半径的相对论修正、自旋相关的瓦解阈值以及Kerr自旋对瓦解几何的影响。

Conclusion: Blanet TDE为解释AGN环境中异常TDE-like暂现源提供了新途径，且其碎屑极端质量比旋进（EMRI）产生的引力波有望被LISA探测到。

Abstract: Blanets are planetary-mass bodies ($20$--$3000\,\Me$) that may orbit supermassive black holes (SMBHs) in the circumnuclear disks of active galactic nuclei (AGN). We examine tidal disruption events produced by blanet--SMBH encounters, from the test-particle limit to massive planetary bodies in Kerr spacetime. Using the geodesic deviation equation and the Kerr tidal tensor, we derive disruption criteria, tidal radii, and Hills masses for planetary-mass objects, and show that blanet TDEs can remain observable for SMBHs up to $\sim10^{10}\,\Msun$, well above the stellar Hills mass of $\sim10^8\,\Msun$. The fallback rate retains the usual $t^{-5/3}$ form, but the peak timescales are shorter -- from hours to months -- with lower peak accretion rates and multi-wavelength signatures that differ from those of stellar TDEs. We also examine orbital stability, including Keplerian precession, Lense--Thirring nodal precession, migration in the circumnuclear disk, and the Kozai--Lidov resonance, and identify the region where blanets can survive before disruption. We derive relativistic corrections to the tidal radius, spin-dependent disruption thresholds, and the effect of Kerr spin on the disruption geometry. We also discuss gravitational-wave emission from blanet debris EMRIs and the prospects for LISA detection, which may help in interpreting unusual TDE-like transients in AGN environments.

</details>


### [4] [Plasticity of Neutron Star Crusts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06706)
*Matthew E Caplan,Nevin T Smith,Ashley J Bransgrove,Charles J Horowitz*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理分子动力学模拟，研究中子星地壳（neutron star crusts）的变形与断裂。发现在比以往工作慢数个数量级的应变率（strain rate）下，超过断裂点后存在一个与初始晶体结构无关的稳态塑性流动（steady plastic flow）新机制。多晶（polycrystals）在剪切应变 ε=0.05 时从线性弹性（linear elasticity）转变为完美塑性流动（perfect plastic flow），而单晶（monocrystals）在 ε=0.11 处断裂后也进入塑性流动。这种普遍的后断裂塑性可能源于晶体自洽地形成缺陷密度以适应施加的应变率。若断裂后的地壳能重新退火（re-anneal）至大晶粒尺寸，则地壳断裂可能重复发生，对磁星爆发与耀发（magnetar bursts and flares）具有重要启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解中子星地壳在极端条件下的变形与断裂行为，特别是超越断裂点后的塑性流动机制，这对于解释磁星爆发等天体物理现象至关重要。

Method: 采用第一性原理分子动力学（first-principles molecular dynamics）模拟，使用比以往工作慢数个数量级的应变率进行模拟，对比多晶与单晶的力学响应。

Result: 发现了与初始晶体结构无关的稳态塑性流动新机制；多晶在 ε=0.05 处从线性弹性转变为完美塑性流动；单晶在 ε=0.11 处断裂后也进入塑性流动。

Conclusion: 晶体可通过自洽地形成缺陷密度以适应施加的应变率，从而产生普遍的后断裂塑性。若断裂地壳能重新退火至大晶粒尺寸，断裂可能重复发生，这对磁星爆发和耀发具有重要启示。

Abstract: We use first-principles molecular dynamics simulations to study the deformation and breaking of neutron star crusts. When simulating with strain rates several orders of magnitude slower than prior work, we find a new regime of steady plastic flow beyond the breaking point that is independent of the initial crystal structure. Polycrystals exhibit a robust transition from linear elasticity to perfect plastic flow at shear strains of $ε= 0.05$, while monocrystals break at $ε= 0.11$ and then flow plastically. The universal post-break plasticity may arise because the crystal self-consistently assumes a defect density to accommodate the imposed strain rate. If broken crusts can re-anneal to large crystal sizes, crust breaking may repeat with implications for magnetar bursts and flares.

</details>

### [5] [Hyperon-Nucleon Spectrometer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06553)
*Xiaozhi Bai,Xu Cao,Zhe Cao,Jinhui Chen,Kai Chen,Qibo Chen,Shi Chen,Xin Chen,Yuquan Chen,Zhenyu Chen,Jianping Dai,Heng-Tong Ding,Dongshuo Du,Shuxian Du,Limin Duan,Zhe Duan,Anhui Feng,Jie Feng,Yicheng Feng,Jinlin Fu,Xiaofeng Fu,Chaosong Gao,Liang Ge,Wenwen Ge,Lisheng Geng,Boxing Gou,An Gu,Yinghui Guan,Yutian Guan,Aiqiang Guo,Fengkun Guo,Lu Guo,Hao Han,Weijia Han,Yunxiang Hao,Wanbing He,Xionghong He,Zhixuan He,Defu Hou,Tingting Hou,Jinniu Hu,Shouyang Hu,Zhen Hu,Fei Huang,Kaixuan Huang,Linqin Huang,Mei Huang,Xuguang Huang,Yuanjing Ji,Xincai Kang,Jie Kong,Cheng Li,Demin Li,Haibo Li,Jibo Li,Lixuan Li,Min Li,Peilian Li,Peiyu Li,Ronghua Li,Suxian Li,Weilong Li,Wuyuan Li,Xin Li,Xiaomei Li,Xiaqing Li,Yang Li,Yangu Li,Yutie Liang,Zheng Liang,Zuotang Liang,Chuangxin Lin,Dexu Lin,Shoulong Lin,Ting Lin,Bo Liu,Bo-Chao Liu,Feng Liu,Hang Liu,Hongna Liu,Hui Liu,Kai Liu,Liuming Liu,Qian Liu,Tianbo Liu,Tong Liu,Xiang Liu,Yanwen Liu,Pengzhong Lu,Weijian Lu,Xiaofeng Luo,Xiao-Rui Lyu,Bo-Qiang Ma,Jianping Ma,Kuo Ma,Weihu Ma,Yugang Ma,Lijun Mao,Ruishi Mao,Yu Meng,Norihito Muramatsu,Maowu Nie,Xiaoyang Niu,Hua Pei,Ronggang Ping,Shi Pu,Tianlei Pu,Cheng Qian,Wenbin Qian,Yi Qian,Guangyou Qin,Jiajun Qin,Cong-Feng Qiao,Zan Ren,Dingyu Shao,Qianshun She,Diyu Shen,Guodong Shen,Wenhan Shen,Xiaomin Shen,Lina Sheng,Shusu Shi,Jinxing Song,Qintao Song,Yuan Song,Zihe Su,Baohua Sun,Hao Sun,Kai-Jia Sun,Liangting Sun,Peng Sun,Pengfei Sun,Xiangming Sun,Xu Sun,Yelei Sun,Zhipeng Sun,Zhiyu Sun,Shuwen Tang,Zebo Tang,Jing Tian,Ye Tian,Yu Tian,Yapeng Wan,Boqun Wang,Changxin Wang,En Wang,Enke Wang,Haozhen Wang,Hulin Wang,Jiansong Wang,Ling Wang,Qun Wang,Tianao Wang,Xiangang Wang,Xiang-Peng Wang,Xiaoyu Wang,Xinyu Wang,Xiongfei Wang,Xiuhua Wang,Yaping Wang,Shuyi Wei,Xianglun Wei,Xiangjie Wen,Fengjun Wu,Jia-jun Wu,Xin Wu,Bowen Xiao,Le Xiao,Zhigang Xiao,Guannan Xie,Yaping Xie,Hongxi Xing,Weizhi Xiong,Ji Xu,Lailin Xu,Nu Xu,Qinghua Xu,Xiaowei Xu,Junwei Yan,Wenbiao Yan,Wencheng Yan,Xiaoyu Yan,Bo Yang,Chi Yang,Haibo Yang,Herun Yang,Jiancheng Yang,Qian Yang,Shuai Yang,Tongjun Yang,Yadong Yang,Yuansheng Yang,Yuna Yang,Zaochen Ye,Zhihong Ye,Li Yi,Hang Yin,Junhao Yin,Yi Yin,Kejie You,Zhengyun You,Chunxu Yu,Yuhong Yu,Zhaoyang Yuan,Wangmei Zha,Honglin Zhang,Jianyu Zhang,Jin Zhang,Jinlong Zhang,Jinqun Zhang,Shisheng Zhang,Weibin Zhang,Xiang Zhang,Xueheng Zhang,Yapeng Zhang,Yateng Zhang,Yifei Zhang,Yumei Zhang,Yuqiao Zhang,Zhe Zhang,He Zhao,Hongyun Zhao,Lei Zhao,Yuxiang Zhao,Zhengguo Zhao,Yajun Zheng,Yangheng Zheng,Zhiyang Zheng,Daicui Zhou,Jian Zhou,Jiangpeng Zhou,Jing Zhou,Kai Zhou,Xianrong Zhou,Xiaorong Zhou,Yiyu Zhou,Sitao Zhu,Xiao Zhuang,Xinyu Zong,Bingsong Zou*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出了在 HIAF 上建造超子-核子谱仪（H-NS）的构想，旨在通过质子-质子（$pp$）、质子-核（$pA$）和核-核（$AA$）固定靶碰撞实验，系统研究 $\Lambda$ 超子极化之谜及其机制，并探索冷热核物质效应对自旋极化的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低能量子色动力学（QCD）中的手征对称性及其自发破缺是理解强子质量和强相互作用动力学的核心，而 $\Lambda$ 超子在非极化强子碰撞中产生的显著横向极化现象（$\Lambda$ 极化之谜）至今在理论上无法解释，亟需系统的实验研究。

Method: H-NS 实验将利用 HIAF 高能高强度的质子与重离子束流，在固定靶模式下开展 $pp$、$pA$、$AA$ 碰撞实验；通过束流能量扫描（质子束能量 3–9.3 GeV 及升级后最高 32 GeV）研究极化对碰撞能量的依赖；采用专用探测器实现末态重子极化的高精度重建。

Result: 该实验将同时测量超子和质子的自旋可观测量，以探究强子相互作用中的极化机制及重子自旋结构；利用 $pA$ 和 $AA$ 碰撞详细研究冷核物质和热核物质效应对自旋极化的影响。

Conclusion: H-NS 的物理计划与探测器研制工作将对中国未来的电子-离子对撞机（Electron-ion Collider in China）产生重要推动作用，有望为手征动力学和自发手征对称性破缺相关核心问题提供实验答案。

Abstract: Chirality lies at the heart of low-energy QCD, governing the symmetry structure that shapes hadron masses and strong interaction dynamics. Among the most compelling open questions tied to chiral dynamics and spontaneous chiral symmetry breaking is the longstanding $Λ$ polarization puzzle, in which $Λ$ hyperons produced in unpolarized hadronic collisions exhibit a surprisingly large transverse polarization that remains theoretically unexplained. This whitepaper presents the proposal for the Hyperon-Nucleon Spectrometer (H-NS) at the High-Intensity heavy-ion Accelerator Facility (HIAF). Leveraging the high energy and high intensity of HIAF's proton and heavy-ion beams, the H-NS experiment will perform systematic studies of hyperon polarization phenomena and their underlying mechanisms in proton-proton ($pp$), proton-nucleus ($pA$), and nucleus-nucleus ($AA$) collisions in the fixed target mode. A wide-range beam energy scan, including proton beams from 3 GeV up to 9.3 GeV (HIAF) and up to 32 GeV (upgraded HIAF), will be conducted to examine the dependence of polarization on collision energy. The spectrometer is designed with specialized detectors capable of high-precision reconstruction of final-state baryon polarizations. Among its many interesting and important measurements, H-NS will simultaneously measure hyperon and proton spin observables to explore the polarization mechanism in hadronic interactions and the spin structure of baryons. Furthermore, the use of $pA$ and $AA$ collisions will enable detailed investigations of cold and hot nuclear matter effects on spin polarization. Its physics program and detector development will significantly benefit the future Electron-ion Collider in China.

</details>


### [6] [Sensor Quality Control and Annealing Studies of HGCAL Silicon Sensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07278)
*Gizem Gul Dincer*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文总结了CMS HGCAL探测器非辐照硅传感器的质量控制（SQC）结果，并首次报告了针对晶圆级120 µm外延（epitaxial）传感器在60°C条件下、退火时间从10到5000分钟的等温退火（isothermal annealing）行为研究，提取了Hamburg模型参数，同时分析了辐照前漏电流热区及存在堆垛层错（stacking faults）的外延传感器在辐照后的性能变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为CMS HGCAL探测器的高粒度硅传感器建立全面的质量控制（QC）工作流，并系统研究辐照后传感器的退火行为，以理解有效掺杂浓度（effective doping concentration）随时间的变化规律，从而评估探测器长期运行中的性能退化。

Method: 采用非辐照硅传感器的质量控制流程，包括供应商数据自动处理、电学测量验证及晶圆级特性交叉校验；针对暴露于 \(2\times10^{15}\) n_eq/cm² 中子等效通量的120 µm外延传感器，在60°C条件下进行10至5000分钟的等温退火实验，利用Hamburg模型拟合有效掺杂浓度随退火时间的变化。

Result: 首次获得了60°C等温退火条件下退火时间10–5000分钟范围内的完整数据，提取了Hamburg模型参数；揭示了辐照前存在热区（hot regions）的传感器及含有堆垛层错的外延传感器在辐照后的不同行为特征。

Conclusion: 研究工作为非辐照硅传感器的质量控制流程提供了系统方案，并为HGCAL探测器中硅传感器在辐照后退火行为提供了重要的实验数据与模型参数，有助于评估探测器的长期稳定性和性能预期。

Abstract: We summarise Sensor Quality Control (SQC) results of non-irradiated silicon sensors for the CMS HGCAL detector, as well as the first detailed annealing campaign with a wafer-scale 120\,\textmu m (Epitaxial) sensor exposed to \(2\times10^{15}\)\,\si{n_{eq}/cm^2} at the Rhode Island Nuclear Science Center (RINSC). For the non-irradiated sensors, we present an overview of the QC workflow developed for HGCAL, including automated handling of vendor data, validation of electrical measurements, and cross-checking of wafer-level characteristics. The study investigates, for the first time, the isothermal annealing behaviour at 60\,\si{\celsius} after annealing periods ranging from 10 to 5000 minutes. Hamburg-model parameters for effective doping concentration changes with annealing time, extracted from full-sensor data, are presented. The post-irradiation behaviour of sensors with hot regions in the pre-irradiation leakage current measurements, as well as epitaxial sensors with stacking faults in individual cells, is also investigated.

</details>

# cond-mat.soft [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Beyond Snap-Fit: Optimizing the Lifting Capabilities of a Partial Cylindrical Shell](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06710)
*Grace K. Curtis,Ian M. Griffiths,Dominic Vella*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了圆柱卡扣（cylindrical snap-fit）作为弹性薄壳在刚性圆柱上的力学行为，根据举升能力（lifting capacity）将接触状态分为“抓扣（grip-fit）”和“无举升能力”两类，并进一步在抓扣内区分了“卡扣（snap-fit）”与“粘扣（stick-fit）”两种机制，最终给出了基于几何与摩擦系数的完整分类及设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圆柱卡扣虽广泛用于制造与装配，但其力学机制尚未被充分理解。本文旨在基于前人工作，将圆柱卡扣建模为置于刚性圆柱上的自然弯曲薄弹性壳，系统分类其接触状态并揭示举升性能的权衡关系，为安全举升、易拆卸及易碎品操作提供设计依据。

Method: 将圆柱卡扣视为置于刚性圆柱上的自然弯曲薄弹性壳（thin elastic shell），施加点力将其推向或拉离圆柱，分析壳体的力学响应。根据壳体是否具有非零举升能力（lifting capacity）划分接触状态，并引入“抓扣”（grip-fit）作为有举升能力的总称，其中包含“卡扣”（snap-fit）和“粘扣”（stick-fit）两种子类。所有状态完全由壳/圆柱几何参数（geometry）与摩擦系数（coefficient of friction）表征。

Result: 成功将接触状态分为有举升能力（抓扣）与无举升能力两大类，且抓扣内部可区分出具有典型“咔嗒”特性的卡扣与无此特性但仍可举升的粘扣。不同状态完全由几何与摩擦系数决定。分析了装配力（assembly force）、拆卸力（disassembly force）、举升力（lifting force）与夹紧力（clamping force）之间的权衡关系。

Conclusion: 圆柱卡扣的力学行为可由几何与摩擦系数完整分类；抓扣（包括卡扣与粘扣）的设计需要在装配力、拆卸力、举升力与夹紧力之间进行权衡，为实际工程中实现安全举升、便捷拆卸及保护易碎物体提供了明确的设计原则。

Abstract: The cylindrical snap-fit is a ubiquitous fastening method that is both simple to manufacture and assemble, and yet secure. It consists of a partial cylindrical shell that `snaps' onto a cylindrical object. We build on previous work to describe the mechanics of the cylindrical snap-fit as a naturally curved thin elastic shell placed atop a rigid cylinder; we investigate the shell's behaviour when subject to a point force pushing it onto or pulling it off the cylinder. We classify the possible contact regimes according to whether the shell has a nonzero lifting capacity. We term situations with lifting capacity `grip-fits' and show that this includes both the snap-fit and a `stick-fit' regime, which allows lifting despite not having the characteristic `snap'. Regimes without lifting capacity are also characterized for completeness. We show that the different regimes may be characterized entirely by the shell/cylinder geometry and the coefficient of friction. We then consider different metrics for the lifting performance in the grip-fit regime. Our analysis reveals the trade-offs between assembly force, disassembly force, lifting force, and clamping force, providing design principles for secure lifting, easy detachment, and safe handling of fragile objects.

</details>


### [8] [Enhanced viscous adhesion using deformable structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07133)
*Mary Williams,Thomas Desmedt,Fabian Brau,Pascal Damman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和理论研究了柔性薄弹性结构在粘性流体中受控回缩时的粘附动力学，发现结构柔性会引入强非线性力学响应，从而显著改变粘附力的大小和演化行为。相比刚性系统，柔性结构能够实现增强且可调的粘附力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然界中许多粘附机制涉及柔性结构与粘性流体的耦合，但其力学原理尚未完全理解。本文旨在揭示结构柔性如何影响粘附力的产生和调控。

Method: 采用专门的实验测量柔性薄弹性结构在粘性流体中受控回缩时的粘附力响应，同时发展了一个耦合弹性（elasticity）与粘度（viscosity）的理论框架来捕捉流固耦合行为。

Result: 实验表明结构柔性会引入强非线性（strongly nonlinear）力学响应，显著改变粘附力的大小及其随回缩速度的演化规律。与刚性系统相比，柔性结构的可变形性能够实现增强且可调的粘附（enhanced and tunable adhesion）。

Conclusion: 结构柔性是调控粘附力大小与演化的重要机制，所提出的弹性-粘度耦合理论框架为理解柔性结构如何实现粘附控制提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We investigate the adhesion dynamics of a thin elastic structure in contact with a viscous fluid and retracted at a controlled speed, mimicking natural adhesion mechanisms. During detachment, the viscous fluid confined between the deformable structure and a rigid substrate generates an adhesive force due to a pressure drop within the thin film. We show from dedicated experiments that the structural flexibility introduces a strongly nonlinear mechanical response, which significantly alters both the magnitude and the evolution of the adhesion force with retraction velocity. In contrast to rigid systems, the deformability of the structure enables enhanced and tunable adhesion. To capture this interplay, we develop a theoretical framework that couples elasticity and viscosity, providing new insights into how flexible structures enable adhesion control.

</details>


### [9] [Microswimmers create bicontinuous emulsions in binary fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07292)
*Harinadha Gidituri,Sotiris Samatas,Juho S. Lintuvuori*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本论文通过流体动力学模拟，研究了中性润湿微泳体（microswimmers）在两相分离对称流体混合物中的行为，发现其自发乳化形成双连续泡沫状结构，并揭示了两类活性成分（源偶极与力偶极）的双重稳定机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索中性润湿活性粒子（active particles）在相分离流体混合物中如何影响乳化行为及结构稳定性，旨在理解活性物质（active matter）与流体界面的耦合机制。

Method: 采用流体动力学模拟（hydrodynamic simulations），研究中性润湿微泳体（neutrally wetting microswimmers）在两种相分离流体的对称混合物中的动力学行为。

Result: 微泳体自发将两种流体乳化为双连续泡沫状（bicontinuous foam-like）结构。源偶极（source dipole，即自推进）过强时，微泳体会快速穿越界面，导致流体重新相分离；低于该阈值时，力偶极（force dipole）产生的活性应力（active stresses）可稳定动态的双连续泡沫态。关闭活性后，系统弛豫至动力学捕获的双连续态（kinetically trapped bicontinuous state），粒子永久困于界面。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了通过调节活性微泳体的自推进与活性应力，可实现对活性乳液（active emulsions）的微观调控，对理解细菌悬浮液（bacterial suspensions）及合成活性物质（synthetic active matter）具有启示意义。

Abstract: We consider a generic case of neutrally wetting microswimmers in symmetric mixtures of two phase separating fluids, using hydrodynamic simulations. The swimmers spontaneously emulsify the two fluids into bicontinuous foam-like state. The two principal activity components: source dipole (self-propulsion) and force dipole (active mixing), create a twofold mechanism to stabilise the structures. When the self-propulsion is too strong, the swimmers cross the interfaces rapidly and the two fluids will phase separate. Below this threshold, the active stresses from the force dipoles, stabilise a dynamic and bicontinuous foam-like state. When the activity is turned off, the system relaxes into a kinetically trapped bicontinuous state, with particles permanently trapped at the interfaces. Our results provide a microscopic route to tunable active emulsions, with implications for bacterial suspensions and synthetic active matter.

</details>


### [10] [Resolving Light-Induced Structural Rearrangements in Responsive Microgels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07371)
*Fabrizio Camerin,Megha Emerse,Gianpaolo Gallo,Najet Mahmoudi,Gregory Smith,Emanuela Zaccarelli,Lucio Isa,Marco Laurati,Jacopo Vialetto*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究结合动态光散射、小角中子散射与分子动力学模拟，揭示了含香豆素（coumarin）的光响应微凝胶在紫外光照射后，其内部结构从星形致密核-伸展臂构型转变为更紧凑的网络，且该光诱导变化无法等同于合成中提高交联密度，表明光照是调控微凝胶结构与多功能响应的有效手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光响应微凝胶（optically-responsive microgels）能够实现光与热响应的耦合，交联度不仅调控粒径还调控刚度。然而，连接分子光响应机制与介观性质（mesoscopic properties）的内部结构变化尚不清晰。

Method: 研究采用动态光散射（dynamic light scattering, DLS）、小角中子散射（small-angle neutron scattering, SANS）以及分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）相结合的方法，分析含有共价嵌入香豆素（coumarin）基团的光响应微凝胶。

Result: 光照不仅改变微凝胶的粒径，还改变内部聚合物密度分布及后续热响应。照射前微凝胶呈现星形结构（star-like architecture），即致密核与伸展的聚合物臂；照射后网络演变为显著更紧凑的结构。

Conclusion: 光诱导的结构转变不能简单地等同于合成过程中提升交联密度（crosslinking density）所导致的效果；光照可作为一种调控微凝胶结构与多功能响应的有力工具。

Abstract: Optically-responsive microgels offer a versatile platform for designing adaptive soft materials with coupled light and thermal responsiveness. Control over the crosslinking degree is particularly appealing as it can regulate not only particle size but also stiffness, thereby enabling remote tuning of key material functionalities. However, the internal structural changes that couple molecular photoresponsive mechanisms to mesoscopic properties remain poorly resolved. Here, we investigate different light-responsive microgels containing covalently incorporated coumarin moieties, which impart optical sensitivity through UV-induced cycloaddition, by combining dynamic light scattering, small-angle neutron scattering, and molecular dynamics simulations. We show that light irradiation alters not only particle size but also the internal polymer density distribution and subsequent thermal response. Before irradiation, the microgels exhibit a star-like architecture with a dense core and extended polymeric arms. After irradiation, the network evolves toward a markedly more compact structure. This transformation cannot be rationalized simply as an equivalent to an increase in crosslinking density during synthesis, as observed in the thermal response, revealing light as a powerful tool to regulate microgel architecture and multifunctional responsiveness.

</details>


### [11] [Hydrogel mechanics below swelling equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07384)
*A. Chao Correas,Y. Feng,R. W. Style,D. S. Kammer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验与理论相结合，发现当水凝胶（hydrogels）未完全溶胀时，其力学行为显著简化：聚合物-水亲和力（polymer-water affinity）主导局部水化，而弹性网络（polymer network elasticity）仅决定弹性形状，从而建立了能精确预测应力与变形的简化模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水凝胶因其柔软性和含水量变化能力而用途广泛，但其力学行为涉及流体流动与弹性变形之间的强耦合，十分复杂。本文旨在揭示该耦合在非完全溶胀条件下的简化机制。

Method: 采用实验与理论相结合的方法，分析非完全溶胀水凝胶（hydrogels）中聚合物-水亲和力与聚合物网络弹性（polymer network elasticity）的相互作用关系。

Result: 发现非完全溶胀状态下，聚合物-水亲和力控制局部水化（local hydration），而弹性网络仅起次要作用，决定弹性形状（elastic shape）。基于此观测，建立了简化模型，能够准确预测应力（stresses）与变形（deformations）。

Conclusion: 非完全溶胀水凝胶的力学耦合可以简化，为准确预测其应力与变形提供了实用的理论模型。

Abstract: Hydrogels are versatile materials due to their softness and ability to undergo large changes in water content. Their mechanics, however, are complex, being a tight coupling between fluid flow and elastic deformations. We use experiments and theory to show that this coupling simplifies when hydrogels are not fully swollen. In this regime, polymer-water affinity controls local hydration, while the much weaker polymer network elasticity plays a secondary role, setting the resulting elastic shape. This observation enables a simplified model that accurately predicts stresses and deformations.

</details>


### [12] [Flow of deformable droplets: self-pinned glasses and string-like flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07438)
*Achille Quarante,Michael Chiang,Davide Marenduzzo,Giuseppe Negro*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过数值模拟研究了可变形液滴干悬浮液在压力驱动流下的流变学，发现了两种力驱动的动力学相变：屈服（yielding）导致的间歇性粘滑态（stick-slip regime），以及进一步驱动下的类弦流动态（string-like flowing state）。研究表明重叠网络（overlap network）的重构是控制可变形颗粒悬浮液流动的通用机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解可变形液滴悬浮液在压力驱动流下的流变行为，特别是颗粒可变形性如何影响系统的屈服行为、动力学态以及流动机制。

Method: 采用数值模拟（numerical simulations）方法，研究干悬浮液（dry suspension）中可变形液滴（deformable droplets）在压力驱动流（pressure-driven flow）下的流变学（rheology）。

Result: 发现了两种力驱动的动力学转变（force-driven dynamical transitions）：低力下表现为屈服应力材料（yield-stress material）；屈服后进入间歇性粘滑态（stick-slip regime），呈现长寿命笼闭（caging）与非高斯速度涨落（non-Gaussian velocity fluctuations），可解释为“自钉扎玻璃”（self-pinned glass）；更大驱动力下转变为类弦流动态（string-like flowing state）。屈服临界力强烈依赖于液滴的可变形性（deformability）。

Conclusion: 重叠网络（overlap network）的重构是可变形颗粒悬浮液在驱动下流动控制的通用机制（generic mechanism），为理解可变形颗粒体系的流变学提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate, through numerical simulations, the rheology of a dry suspension of deformable droplets under pressure-driven flow. The system exhibits two force-driven dynamical transitions. At low forcing, the suspension behaves as a yield-stress material: below a critical force, droplets remain arrested in an amorphous solid-like state. Our simulations suggest that yielding is controlled by droplet contacts and predict that the critical force strongly depends on deformability. Above yielding, the suspension does not flow steadily but rather enters an intermittent, stick-slip regime characterised by long-lived caging and non-Gaussian velocity fluctuations. This state can be interpreted as a "self-pinned'' glass, in which slowly evolving droplet overlaps generate an effective rugged energy landscape that dynamically traps droplets and produces intermittent rearrangements reminiscent of near-critical dynamics in depinning models. At larger forcing, droplets deform sufficiently to continuously exchange neighbours, progressively annealing the overlap structure and driving a dynamic transition to a string-like, flowing state. Our results identify the restructuring of overlap networks as a generic mechanism which controls flow in driven suspensions of deformable particles.

</details>

### [13] [NNLO+PS Higgs-pair production in MiNNLOPS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05300)
*Francesco Garosi,Marius Wiesemann,Giulia Zanderighi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在MiNNLO$_{PS}$框架下实现了双希格斯玻色子（Higgs-boson pair）在胶子融合（gluon fusion）产生过程中的次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD修正与部分子簇射（parton shower）的匹配，并通过基于精确NLO QCD结果的近似方法纳入有限顶夸克质量（top-quark mass）效应，最后给出了不同希格斯衰变道和三线性希格斯耦合（trilinear Higgs coupling）变化的唯象学结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双希格斯玻色子产生是检验希格斯势能形状和电弱对称性破缺机制的关键过程，需要高精度的理论预测以匹配实验精度。目前完整的顶夸克质量依赖在NNLO阶尚不可得，因此需要发展可靠的近似方案来纳入有限质量效应，并将NNLO修正与部分子簇射匹配以生成可用于实验模拟的蒙特卡洛事件。

Method: 在MiNNLO$_{PS}$框架内，将NNLO QCD修正与部分子簇射匹配。由于完整的两圈幅（two-loop amplitude）仅在全理论中已知，有限顶夸克质量效应通过基于精确NLO QCD结果的近似方案纳入：Born项、单虚修正、单实修正和双实修正确切包含，而实-虚修正和双虚修正采用近似处理，并对后者采用不同近似方案以评估相关不确定性。

Result: 预测结果经固定阶NNLO QCD结果验证，并与GENEVA框架中已有的NNLO+部分子簇射匹配结果进行了比较；在某些情况下发现了显著差异。给出了不同希格斯衰变道和三线性希格斯耦合变化下的唯象学结果。

Conclusion: 基于MiNNLO$_{PS}$的双希格斯玻色子产生发生器已在POWHEG-BOX-RES框架中发布，可供实验研究使用。

Abstract: We consider Higgs-boson pair production in gluon fusion at hadron colliders and match next-to-next-to-leading-order (NNLO) QCD corrections to parton showers within the MiNNLO$_{PS}$ framework. Since the full top-quark mass dependence at this order is not available, finite top-quark mass effects are incorporated through approximations based on the exact NLO QCD result, using the available two-loop amplitude in the full theory. Specifically, the Born, single-virtual, single-real and double-real contributions are included exactly, while the real--virtual and double-virtual corrections are approximated. We consider different approximations for the latter to assess the associated uncertainties. We validate our predictions against fixed-order NNLO QCD results and compare with existing NNLO calculations matched to parton shower from GENEVA, where in some cases we find noticeable differences. Finally, we present phenomenological results for different Higgs-decay channels and variations of the trilinear Higgs coupling. Our MiNNLO$_{PS}$ generator for Higgs-boson pair production is available within the POWHEG-BOX-RES framework.

</details>


### [14] [Method to study $CP$ violation in $B_s^0\to K_S K^\pm π^\mp$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06446)
*Chen Chen,Tim Gershon,Thomas Latham*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次提出了一种对 $B_s^0\to K_S K^\pm π^\mp$ 衰变进行标记的时间依赖达利兹图（tagged decay-time-dependent Dalitz-plot）联合分析方法，通过伪实验（pseudoexperiments）验证了其可行性，并展示了在未来LHCb数据集上对弱相位差 $φ_s^{\rm eff}$ 的良好测量精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $B_s^0\to K_S K^\pm π^\mp$ 衰变可用于检验标准模型（Standard Model）并寻找 $CP$ 破坏的新来源，但此前从未完成过对两个末态同时进行标记的时间依赖达利兹图全分析，因此需要建立新的分析方法。

Method: 建立了一种将两个末态中衰变到共振态（resonances）的振幅相互关联的方法，并在 Laura++ 达利兹图分析软件包中实现；通过伪实验（pseudoexperiments）验证了该方法的可行性。

Result: 研究表明，使用 LHCb Run 1–3 的数据集即可对 $φ_s^{\rm eff}$ 实现良好的测量精度，且未来收集的更大数据集有望进一步改善精度。

Conclusion: 该方法不仅适用于 $B_s^0\to K_S K^\pm π^\mp$ 衰变，还可推广至其他具有多个末态的多体衰变（multibody decays）。

Abstract: The $B_s^0\to K_S K^\pm π^\mp$ decays are of interest to test the Standard Model and search for new sources of $CP$ violation. A full study of these decays requires a tagged decay-time-dependent Dalitz-plot analysis performed simultaneously in the two final states. Such an analysis has never previously been performed. The method to carry out such an analysis, relating the amplitudes for decays to resonances in the two final-states to each other, is set out and its feasibility is demonstrated using pseudoexperiments. The sensitivity to the weak phase difference, $φ_s^{\rm eff}$, between $B_s^0 \to K_S K^*(892)^0$ decays with and without $B_s^0$-$\bar{B}_s^0$ mixing is studied. Good precision on $φ_s^{\rm eff}$ is found to be achievable with a dataset corresponding to LHCb Runs 1-3, with further improvement expected with datasets to be collected in future. The method is implemented in the Laura++ Dalitz-plot analysis package, and can be applied to other multibody decays with multiple final states.

</details>


### [15] [Reweighting Adversarial Networks for Unbinned Unfolding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06603)
*Umar Sohail Qureshi,Krish Desai,Jesse Thaler,Benjamin Nachman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为重加权对抗网络（Reweighting Adversarial Network, RAN）的新型无分箱展开技术，用于解决粒子与核物理中微分截面的高维展开问题。RAN通过粒子层面的重加权函数与探测器层面的Wasserstein判别器协作，无需重叠支持域和多次迭代训练，在精度和计算效率上均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子与核物理中，微分截面（differential cross sections）是科学交流的基本量。传统展开方法面临双层优化（bi-level optimization）挑战：约束条件在探测器层面，而目标在粒子层面，二者通过随机探测器响应（stochastic detector response）关联。当粒子层面与探测器层面的分布支持域不重叠或仅部分重叠时，训练不稳定且展开性能下降。

Method: RAN将无分箱展开（unbinned unfolding）视为一种双层优化问题，通过粒子层面的重加权函数（reweighting function）与探测器层面的Wasserstein判别器（Wasserstein critic）协同工作。该方法可视为矩展开协议（Moment Unfolding protocol）在完整相空间展开（full phase-space unfolding）上的推广，无需探测器层面的支持域重叠，也无需多次迭代训练。

Result: 在高斯数据和喷注子结构（jet substructure）研究中，包括专门设计用于测试支持域消失重叠（vanishing support overlap）的极端情形下，RAN在精度上超越了现有最先进方法，且计算开销更低。

Conclusion: RAN作为一种通用的无分箱展开技术，有效解决了双层优化及支持域不匹配问题，在准确性和计算效率方面均优于现有方法，为高能物理中的微分截面测量提供了一种高效新方案。

Abstract: Differential cross sections are the currency of scientific exchange in particle and nuclear physics. Recently, machine learning methods have enabled unbinned and high-dimensional cross section measurements through new approaches to unfolding. A key challenge with unfolding is that it is a bi-level optimization problem where constraints are available at the detector level while the target is at the particle level, linked by a stochastic detector response. Further complications arise when the particle-level and detector-level distributions have non-overlapping or only partially overlapping support, which can destabilize training and degrade unfolding performance. In this paper, we introduce a new unbinned unfolding technique called the Reweighting Adversarial Network (RAN), which can be viewed as a generalization of the Moment Unfolding protocol to accommodate full phase-space unfolding. RANs address the bi-level optimization problem through a particle-level reweighting function steered by a Wasserstein critic at the detector level. RANs do not require overlapping support at the detector level, nor multiple iterations of training. We evaluate the performance of RANs with Gaussian data and jet substructure studies, including cases specifically designed to stress test the method under vanishing support overlap. We demonstrate that RANs outperform state-of-the-art methods in accuracy and have a lower computational overhead.

</details>


### [16] [Lepton interactions from GeV to EeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06773)
*Reinaldo Francener*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了中微子（neutrino）和缪子（muon）与物质相互作用的唯象学后果，重点针对FASER/FASER2和IceCube两个实验进行了预测分析，涵盖tau极化效应、缪子引发事件中的核效应与内禀粲夸克（intrinsic charm）、中微子/缪子三叉线过程（trident process）以及超出标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了深入理解中微子和缪子与物质相互作用的唯象学后果，并利用FASER/FASER2和IceCube这两个互补的实验平台，探索标准模型内的核子结构（nucleon structure）及超越标准模型的新物理信号。

Method: 基于FASER/FASER2和IceCube实验的预期事件率，分析了tau中微子带电电流相互作用（charged current interaction）中产生的tau轻子的极化效应，以及缪子引发事件中的核效应和内禀粲夸克。同时，研究了高统计量下中微子三叉线过程（neutrino trident）和缪子三叉线过程（muon trident）的可能性。

Result: FASER2中产生的tau轻子不会完全极化；缪子引发的事件可以揭示核效应和内禀粲夸克的存在；中微子三叉线过程有望在FASER2中被观测到；缪子三叉线过程中的tau对产生可能首次被观测到；IceCube观测到的中微子事件有助于研究靶标强子结构及中微子传播中的新物理效应。

Conclusion: FASER/FASER2和IceCube实验能为中微子物理和缪子物理提供丰富的唯象学信息，包括核子结构、稀有过程（如三叉线过程）以及超出标准模型的新物理探索。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the phenomenological consequences of neutrino and muon interactions with matter. In our studies, we focused in phenomenological predictions for two experiments: FASER and IceCube. FASER is a detector located at the LHC that measures neutrinos produced in proton-proton collisions. A new version of FASER, FASER2, has been proposed to operate in the Forward Physics Facility during the high-luminosity regime of the LHC. The intense flux of tau neutrinos expected at FASER2 motivated us to study the polarization effects of the tau produced in charged current interactions. Our results show that the produced taus will not be completely polarized. Among the Standard Model particles, only neutrinos and muons produced in proton-proton collisions at the LHC can reach FASER. In our study, we show that muon-initiated events can reveal interesting nucleon properties, such as nuclear effects and the existence of an intrinsic charm. The high number of events induced by neutrinos at FASER motivated us to study rare processes in neutrino interaction, such as the neutrino trident. Our results indicate that the neutrino trident process can be observed at FASER2. We have also studied muon trident at the LHC, and we showed that tau pair production can be observed for the first time in this reaction. In contrast to neutrinos detected at the LHC, the neutrinos observed at IceCube come from natural sources, being mainly atmospheric and astrophysical neutrinos. IceCube is capable of observing neutrinos across a wide energy spectrum, ranging from a few GeV to beyond PeV. We show that the study of these events can contribute to our understanding of the structure of target hadrons, as well as the search for physics effects beyond the Standard Model in the propagation of these neutrinos in the universe until they reach the Earth.

</details>


### [17] [Macroscopic Quantum Interference in Dark Matter Wave Scattering with MICROSCOPE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07008)
*Cheng-Tao Fu,Peng-Shun Luo,Rui Luo,Jie Sheng,Chuan-Yang Xing*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文将MICROSCOPE实验的两个同心圆柱嵌套测试质量视为一种暗物质波散射的“干涉仪”，针对暗物质波与双靶体散射的振幅叠加与干涉效应建立理论框架，并应用于分析MICROSCOPE的实际数据。

Result: 该理论预测暗物质波散射振幅在两圆柱间发生干涉并重新分配感应力（induced force），产生由靶体几何结构决定的、受旋转调制的独特信号。对MICROSCOPE数据的分析给出了$10^{-3}$--$10^{-2}\,$eV质量区间内二次暗物质-核子耦合的领先约束，散射截面达$10^{-52}$ cm$^2$量级。

Conclusion: 超轻暗物质的量子干涉效应在嵌套测试质量结构中可产生可观测的调制信号，利用已有实验数据即可获得对暗物质-核子耦合的新强约束，表明该干涉机制为暗物质探测提供了有效的新途径。

Abstract: Ultralight dark matter behaves as a coherent wave, yet its quantum interference effects of elastic scattering with multiple targets have remained unexplored. We show that the nested test masses of MICROSCOPE realize such an ``interferometer'' for dark-matter wave scattering. Amplitudes from the two concentric cylinders interfere and redistribute the induced force between them. This effect produces unique and rotation-modulated signals set by the target geometry. Developing the theoretical framework and applying it to MICROSCOPE data, we obtain leading constraints on quadratic dark-matter--nucleon coupling for masses $10^{-3}$--$10^{-2}\,$eV, reaching cross sections of order $10^{-52}$ cm$^2$.

Method: 首先在单圈阶更新了τ弱磁偶极矩的标准模型预言，并评估了电弱（electroweak）方案依赖性带来的理论不确定性。接着在标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）框架下，联合τ弱偶极矩、电磁偶极矩、LHC上高质量Drell-Yan过程、Z玻色子部分衰变宽度以及电子电偶极矩等多种观测量，推导了当前对τ偶极算符的综合约束。

Result: τ弱偶极矩已经成为探测τ偶极算符的领先观测量之一。在未来的FCC-ee Tera-Z运行和HL-LHC上，τ弱偶极矩的探测优势将更加显著。

Conclusion: τ弱偶极矩在当前精度下已是约束τ偶极算符的重要探针，在未来对撞机实验中其主导地位将进一步增强。

Abstract: We study the weak magnetic and electric dipole moments of the $τ$ lepton as precision tests of the Standard Model (SM) and probes of heavy New Physics (NP). We present an updated SM prediction for the $τ$ weak magnetic dipole moment at one loop, including a careful assessment of theoretical uncertainties from electroweak scheme dependence. Working within the SM Effective Field Theory, we derive comprehensive current constraints on the $τ$ dipole operators from a combination of observables: the $τ$ weak and electromagnetic dipole moments, high-mass Drell-Yan tails at the LHC, $Z$ partial decay widths, and the electron electric dipole moment. Finally, we assess the prospects of measuring the SM value of the $τ$ weak magnetic moment at the FCC-$ee$ Tera-$Z$ run, and project the sensitivities of the leading observables to heavy NP at FCC-$ee$ and HL-LHC, paying particular attention to systematic uncertainties. We find that the $τ$ weak dipole moments are already among the leading probes of the $τ$ dipole operators, and will become increasingly dominant at future colliders.

### [19] [Correlating lepton flavor violating $b \to s$ and leptonic decay modes in a minimal abelian extension of the Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07398)
*Davide Milillo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于ABCD模型（标准模型的极小阿贝尔扩展），研究了$b \to s \ell_1^- \ell_2^+$跃迁（包括轻子味守恒与味破坏情形）与纯轻子味破坏衰变之间的关联。模型引入的$Z'$玻色子具有代依赖的味非普适耦合，参数$\varepsilon_{1,2,3}$确保规范反常抵消。轻子味守恒过程仅偏离标准模型预测很小，而轻子味破坏过程则受当前实验上限的强烈约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索ABCD模型框架下$b \to s$跃迁（包含轻子味守恒与轻子味破坏情形）与纯轻子味破坏衰变之间的可能关联，以理解该模型对味物理现象的预测能力。

Method: 采用ABCD模型，即标准模型（Standard Model, SM）的极小阿贝尔扩展，引入一个新的$\text{U}(1)'$对称性及相应的中性$Z'$玻色子。$Z'$与SM费米子的耦合是代依赖且味非普适的，由三个有理参数$\varepsilon_{1,2,3}$控制，其和为零以确保规范反常（gauge anomaly）抵消。每个$\varepsilon_i$对同一代的所有费米子通用，从而在夸克与轻子观测量之间产生关联。

Result: 对于轻子味守恒（lepton flavor conserving, LFC）过程，模型预测仅出现相对于标准模型的小偏差，反映夸克与轻子扇区之间的相互约束。对于轻子味破坏（lepton flavor violating, LFV）过程，模型允许树图级衰变，从而在LFV $b\to s$跃迁与带电轻子衰变之间产生关联。当前实验上限（如$\tau^- \to \mu^-\mu^+\mu^-$、$\mu^- \to e^-\gamma$、$\mu^- \to e^- e^+ e^-$及原子核内$\mu^- \to e^-$转化过程）对LFV $B_{(s)}$介子衰变的分支比施加了层级性约束。

Conclusion: 在ABCD模型中，轻子味守恒的$b \to s$跃迁受夸克-轻子扇区相互约束而仅允许微小偏离；轻子味破坏过程则被现有轻子味破坏实验数据强烈约束，为LFV $B_{(s)}$衰变的分支比提供了层级化的上限。

Abstract: We examine possible correlations between $b \to s \ell_1^- \ell_2^+$ transitions -- both in the lepton flavor conserving ($\ell_1=\ell_2$) and violating case ($\ell_1 \neq \ell_2$) -- and purely leptonic flavor violating decays within the ABCD model [1], a minimal abelian extension of the Standard Model (SM) introducing a new $\text{U}(1)'$ symmetry. The associated neutral $Z'$ boson has generation-dependent, flavor non-universal couplings to SM fermions, governed by three rational parameters $ε_{1,2,3}$, which sum to zero to ensure gauge anomaly cancellation. Each $ε_i$ is common to all fermions of a given generation, thus inducing correlations among quark and lepton observables. For lepton flavor conserving (LFC) processes, only small deviations from SM predictions were found [2], reflecting the mutual constraints between the quark and lepton sectors, which preclude large discrepancies. On the other hand, the model allows tree-level lepton flavor violating (LFV) decays, yielding correlations between LFV $b\to s$ transitions and charged lepton decays. The analysis of such correlations shows that the current experimental upper bounds for the rates of $τ^- \to μ^-μ^+μ^-$, \ $μ^-\to e^- γ$, \ $μ^- \to e^- e^+e^-$ and $μ^- \to e^-$ conversion in nuclei constrain branching ratios of LFV $B_{(s)}$ decays in hierarchical order [2].

### [20] [Photons, jets and missing momentum from a two-vector dark sector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06607)
*Yara do Amaral Coutinho,Benjamin Fuks,Mark D. Goodsell,Bertrand Laforge,José Ocariz,Farinaldo S. Queiroz,Yoxara Villamizar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究一种包含两个中性重矢量粒子的暗区有效场论（dark-sector effective theory），其中较轻的粒子是暗物质候选者，较重的粒子通过辐射衰变产生 γ+喷注+丢失横动量（γ+jets+E_T^miss）信号。通过基于截断（cut-based）的强子对撞机（LHC）分析，发现采用三-bin分箱策略相较于包容性丢失横动量选择能显著提升探测灵敏度，并覆盖与标准冻结（freeze-out）机制下观测遗迹丰度（relic abundance）兼容的参数空间，同时探讨了冻结（freeze-in）解释及高质量下有效场论（EFT）描述的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对于暗区（dark sector）中矢量媒介子（vector mediator）的LHC唯象研究尚不充分，特别是涉及两个质量不同的中性矢量态及其辐射衰变信号。本文旨在通过有效场论（effective field theory）框架，研究这类暗矢量对的产生与探测可行性，以探索与暗物质遗迹丰度（relic abundance）兼容的参数区域。

Method: 采用一个矢量暗区有效理论（vector dark-sector effective theory），包含两个在暗宇称（dark-parity）下为奇的中性重矢量态。较轻的态稳定，为暗物质候选；与标准模型的相互作用由涉及超规范场强（hypercharge field strength）的维度六算符（dimension-six operators）描述。较重的态在瞬衰（prompt-decay）条件下辐射衰变，结合量子色动力学（QCD）辐射产生γ+jets+E_T^miss的末态信号。通过基于截断分析（cut-based analysis）比较包容性丢失横动量选择（inclusive missing-transverse-momentum selection）与保留粗粒形状信息的三-bin分箱策略（three-bin strategy）。

Result: 三-bin分箱分析相较包容性选择显著提升了预期探测灵敏度（expected reach），成功覆盖与标准冻结（freeze-out）情景中观测遗迹丰度（observed relic abundance）兼容的参数空间。同时讨论了冻结（freeze-in）解释的可能性，并指出在高质量区域有效场论（EFT）描述存在局限性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了在LHC上通过分箱分析策略可以有效搜索由暗矢量对产生的γ+jets+E_T^miss信号，并确认该信号拓扑能探测与标准热冻出（freeze-out）暗物质遗迹丰度一致的参数区域。研究同时提示了冻结（freeze-in）机制的可能及EFT框架在高质量下的适用性边界。

Abstract: We investigate the LHC phenomenology of a vector dark-sector effective theory containing two neutral massive vector states, both odd under a dark-parity symmetry. The lightest state is stable and provides a dark-matter candidate, while the leading interactions with the Standard Model arise from dimension-six operators involving the hypercharge field strength. In the prompt-decay regime considered in this work, the heavier state can decay radiatively, leading to a $γ+\text{jets}+E_T^{\text{miss}}$ signature when the two dark vectors are produced in association with QCD radiation. We study this topology at the LHC through a cut-based analysis, comparing an inclusive missing-transverse-momentum selection with a three-bin strategy that retains coarse shape information. The binned analysis is found to substantially improve the expected reach and probes regions of the parameter space compatible with the observed relic abundance in the standard freeze-out scenario. We also discuss the freeze-in interpretation and the limitations associated with the EFT description at high masses.

### [21] [A more effective QCD string at colliders: Decay of excited strings and the worldsheet axion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06668)
*Ethan Carragher,John March-Russell*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过路径积分计算，研究了存在激发态的QCD弦断裂（Schwinger-like过程）的修正机制。结果表明，世界面轴子（worldsheet axion）激发导致弦的有效张力发生变化，从而指数级地增强或抑制弦断裂速率。计算采用Schwinger-Keldysh复时间轮廓方法与密度矩阵指定的初态数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Lund弦模型假设QCD通量管为恒定张力的基态弦，但高能碰撞中产生的通量管很可能同时激发世界面上的Nambu-Goldstone模和轴子模。因此，需要理论框架来描述激发态弦的断裂过程，以改进强子化（hadronisation）模型。

Method: 采用路径积分（path-integral）方法计算修正的Schwinger-like弦断裂过程，引入Schwinger-Keldysh复时间轮廓（complex time contour）处理非平衡演化，初态由密度矩阵（density matrix）指定。在激发背景下，欧几里得鞍点（Euclidean saddle point）一般为复数，但其解析延拓可给出衰变后演化的实初始数据。

Result: 世界面轴子激发是主导弦断裂率变化的因素。轴子激发导致弦的有效张力发生动态变化，根据激发局域相位的不同，断裂率可被指数级增强或抑制。

Conclusion: 该研究的结果对包含激发态QCD弦的强子化模型具有直接参考意义，有助于修正和完善现有Lund弦模型在高能对撞机现象学中的适用性。

Abstract: The confining flux tube of $(3+1)$d QCD is described by an effective string theory with $(1+1)$d worldsheet action that extends the Nambu-Goto form by the addition of a massive pseudoscalar worldsheet ``axion". As argued in companion papers concerning the modified phenomenology of the Lund string model at colliders, QCD flux tubes produced by high-energy collisions are likely to involve excitation of both worldsheet Nambu-Goldstone and axion modes, although the standard Lund model assumes a constant tension ground-state string. Here we detail the path-integral computation of the modified Schwinger-like process of string breaking via nucleation of quark-antiquark pairs in the presence of excitations above the string ground state. We find that the worldsheet axion leads to the dominant change in the string breaking process, the axion excitations producing, among other effects, a varying effective tension of the string, which can exponentially enhance or suppress the string breaking rate depending on the local phase of the excitation. Our computation employs a version of the Schwinger-Keldysh complex time contour method with initial state data specified by a density matrix. In an excited background the Euclidean saddle point is generically complex, but its continuation gives real initial data for post-decay evolution. Our results are of relevance for hadronisation models with excited QCD strings.

</details>

### [22] [Riemann Rarefaction Waves in a Strongly Interacting Fermi Gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06659)
*Eric A. Wolf,Martin Zwierlein*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了“激波管”（shock tube）几何中释放到真空的均匀强相互作用费米气体（Fermi gas）的膨胀。在幺正性（unitarity）下，稀薄波动力学呈现自相似（self-similar）行为，与欧拉方程（Euler equation）的黎曼解（Riemann's solution）高度吻合；在BEC-BCS渡越区（BEC-BCS crossover）中偏离增大，但自相似性仍近似保持。工作展示了强相互作用费米气体在非线性流体力学研究中的可控性优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索强相互作用费米气体在激波管几何中的膨胀动力学，并验证其是否具有自相似性；同时检验在幺正性附近及BEC-BCS渡越区中，真实流体行为与理想欧拉流体及纳维-斯托克斯（Navier-Stokes）流体理论预测的吻合程度。

Method: 采用激波管几何，将均匀强相互作用费米气体释放到真空中，测量膨胀过程中的密度分布；通过改变温度及相互作用强度（从幺正性到BEC-BCS渡越区），对比观测结果与欧拉方程的黎曼解以及纳维-斯托克斯理论预测。

Result: 在幺正性下，稀薄波动力学对所有测试温度都表现出自相似性，且与欧拉方程的黎曼解高度一致。远离幺正性时，随黏度增加，与黎曼解的偏差增大；但在BCS侧，即使声扩散率（sound diffusivity）提高二十倍，自相似性仍近似保持。

Conclusion: 强相互作用费米气体是研究非线性流体力学（nonlinear hydrodynamics）的高可控实验平台；幺正性下的自相似行为支持其标度不变性（scale invariance）与近无黏性；BEC-BCS渡越区中自相似性的近似保持可能与一维纳维-斯托克斯稀薄波在长时间下趋近欧拉自相似解有关。

Abstract: We investigate the expansion of a homogeneous, strongly interacting Fermi gas released into vacuum in a ``shock tube'' geometry. At unitarity, where the gas is scale invariant and nearly inviscid, we find that the resulting rarefaction wave dynamics are self-similar and in excellent agreement with Riemann's solution of the Euler equation for all temperatures probed. Probing interactions away from unitarity within the BEC-BCS crossover, we observe increasing deviations from the Riemann solution as viscosity increases. However, even on the BCS side, where the sound diffusivity is increased twenty-fold, self-similarity is still approximately preserved. This may reflect how 1D Navier-Stokes rarefaction flows approach Euler self-similar solutions at long times. Our work demonstrates the utility of strongly interacting Fermi gases for the study of nonlinear hydrodynamics in a highly controllable setting.

</details>


### [23] [Failure of the Quench Action Formalism for Mott Insulator Initial States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07111)
*Garry Goldstein*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过反例证明，淬火作用形式（quench action formalism）的核心假设——即初始态与本征态的重叠（overlap）是准粒子密度（quasiparticle density）的光滑函数——并不普遍成立。在Mott绝缘体与Lieb-Liniger气体之间的淬火中，重叠展现出高度奇异行为，无法用指数形式表达。该结论在Tonks-Girardeau极限以及1/c展开的领头阶下得到验证，并在附录中推广至XXZ模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 淬火作用形式依赖于一个关键假设：一般初始态与可积模型（integrable model）本征态的重叠可以写为准粒子密度的光滑指数函数。本文旨在检验这一假设的普适性，并寻找其失效的反例。

Method: 选取Mott绝缘体的基态与Lieb-Liniger气体的任意本征态之间的重叠作为研究对象。在Lieb-Liniger气体的Tonks-Girardeau极限下，以及针对该重叠的1/c展开（c为耦合常数）的领头阶，进行显式解析计算。附录中进一步对XXZ模型中的晶格态（crystal states）进行了类似分析。

Result: Mott绝缘体基态与Lieb-Liniger气体任意本征态之间的重叠展现出高度奇异的行为，无法满足淬火作用形式所假定的光滑指数形式。这一结果在Tonks-Girardeau极限及1/c展开领头阶下均成立。

Conclusion: 淬火作用形式关于重叠光滑性的核心假设并非普遍有效，至少在Mott绝缘体到Lieb-Liniger气体的淬火场景中不成立。这提示该形式在更广泛的可积模型淬火问题中的应用需谨慎评估。

Abstract: The quench action formalism relies on the assumption that the overlap between a generic initial state $\left|Ψ_{0}\right\rangle $ and an eigenstate of an integrable model - defined through the rapidities $\left|k_{1},...k_{N}\right\rangle $ - can be written as: \begin{equation} \left\langle k_{1},...k_{N}\midΨ_{0}\right\rangle =\exp\left(-S_{Ψ_{0}}\left(ρ\left(k\right)\right)\right),\label{eq:Exponential} \end{equation} where $ρ\left(k\right)$ is the quasiparticle density of the state $\left|k_{1},...k_{N}\right\rangle $ and $S_{Ψ_{0}}$ is some smooth function of $ρ\left(k\right)$ that depends on $Ψ_{0}$. In particular the quench action formalism assumes the overlap depends smoothly on the quasiparticle density $ρ\left(k\right)$. In this work, by explicit counter example, we show that this is not the case. We consider the quench between a Mott insulator and a Lieb Liniger gas. We show that the overlap between the ground state of the Mott insulator and arbitrary eigenstates of the Lieb Liniger gas has a highly singular behavior and no expression like Eq. (1) applies. We do so within the Tonks Girardeau limit of the Lieb Liniger gas and to leading order in the $1/c$ expansion for the overlap (with $c$ being the coupling constant of the Lieb Liniger gas). In the Appendix we show similar results for overlaps in the XXZ model with crystal states.

</details>


### [24] [Vortex dynamics in rotating dipolar supersolids across Josephson and self-trapping regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07266)
*Aitor Alaña,Michele Modugno,Pablo Capuzzi*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过将旋转偶极超固体（rotating dipolar supersolid）中的三角液滴晶格（triangular droplet lattice）描述为弱耦合凝聚体阵列，利用约瑟夫森（Josephson）和宏观自陷（self-trapping）动力学，建立了一个基于液滴间局域相位差的紧凑框架，用于研究涡旋成核与输运，揭示了六边形顶点附近的涡旋运动及涡旋-反涡旋对的产生与湮灭机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在旋转偶极超固体的三角液滴晶格中，涡旋的成核与输运机制尚不清楚，亟需一个能够描述液滴间局域相位动力学的高效理论框架来揭示微观拓扑过程。

Method: 采用约瑟夫森动力学和宏观自陷动力学描述弱耦合凝聚体阵列的相位演化，通过液滴间的局域相位差建立预测模型，并与基于扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程（extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation）的数值模拟进行对比验证。

Result: 约瑟夫森振荡可在液滴间的低密度六边形晶格顶点附近诱导涡旋成核与运动；自陷动力学产生运行相位（running phases），实现定向涡旋输运，伴随有限时间尺度内涡旋-反涡旋对的产生与湮灭；三液滴描述对捕获六边形顶点附近的涡旋运动至关重要。

Conclusion: 约瑟夫森与自陷动力学共同提供了一种可调谐的方案，用于触发和追踪涡旋成核、输运及涡旋-反涡旋对湮灭，揭示了旋转偶极超固体中相位滑移（phase slips）的微观拓扑机制。

Abstract: We investigate vortex nucleation and transport in a rotating dipolar supersolid arranged in a triangular droplet lattice, exploiting its description as an array of weakly linked condensates. By considering both Josephson and macroscopic self-trapping dynamics, we show that local phase differences between droplets provide a compact and highly predictive framework to explore a wide range of vortex behaviors. In particular, Josephson oscillations can be devised to induce vortex nucleation and motion near the vertices of the low-density hexagonal lattice (between droplets), while self-trapping dynamics induce running phases that enable directed vortex transport, which may be accompanied by vortex-antivortex pair creation and annihilation over finite time scales. Comparison with simulations based on the extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation demonstrates that a three-droplet description is essential to capture vortex motion near hexagon vertices. Together, Josephson and self-trapping dynamics provide a tunable protocol to trigger and track vortex nucleation, transport, and vortex-antivortex pair annihilation, revealing the microscopic topological mechanisms underlying phase slips in rotating dipolar supersolids.

</details>

### [25] [Near Extremal RN-AdS Control of Holographic Josephson Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06558)
*Ali Övgün,Reggie C. Pantig*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个全息弱连接（holographic weak-link）模型，通过Reissner–Nordström-AdS黑洞（RN-AdS黑膜）的电荷扇区控制约瑟夫森输运（Josephson transport）。在SNS结（超导-正常-超导结）框架下，识别了电流-相位关系、临界电流等核心可观测量，并揭示了近极端RN-AdS喉区（near-extremal throat）对约瑟夫森耦合（Josephson coupling）的径向重整化效应，其标度行为受AdS₂中带电标量场的红外维数（infrared dimension）支配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全息SNS结模型通常依赖黑膜电荷直接定义约瑟夫森相位差，限制了其在带电AdS背景（charged AdS backgrounds）下的适用性。本文旨在构建一个基于规范不变边界数据（gauge-invariant boundary data）的弱连接构型，并引入近极端RN-AdS喉区这一新自由度，以分离普通邻近效应（proximity suppression）、有限密度修正与极端喉区控制这三种不同的物理机制。

Method: 采用渐近AdS₄中的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-带电标量理论（Einstein-Maxwell-charged-scalar theory），施加空间非均匀的边界化学势（spatially inhomogeneous boundary chemical potential），从而在边界上生成两个超导“库区”（superconducting banks），中间被正常或弱超导势垒隔开。约瑟夫森相位差从带电凝聚体（charged condensate）的规范不变边界数据提取，而非黑膜电荷本身。模型通过近极端RN-AdS几何中的AdS₂×ℝ²区域，实现耦合的径向重整化。

Result: 在SNS区，临界电流与中间点凝聚体（midpoint condensate）探测相同的邻近标度；电流-相位关系中的高次谐波可诊断势垒透明度。当系统趋近极端RN-AdS时，AdS₂区域对约瑟夫森耦合产生径向重整化，导致临界电流和相位刚度（phase stiffness）在扣除空间抑制后，呈现出由AdS₂中带电标量红外维数决定的标度行为。

Conclusion: 该模型建立了普通邻近抑制、光滑有限密度修正与近极端喉区控制的三层分离框架，为带电全息物质中的相位敏感输运（phase-sensitive transport）提供了可扩展的理论工具。

Abstract: We formulate a holographic weak-link construction in which Josephson transport is controlled by the charge sector of a Reissner--Nordstrom-AdS black brane. The model is an Einstein-Maxwell-charged-scalar theory in asymptotically AdS$_4$, with a spatially inhomogeneous boundary chemical potential that creates two superconducting banks separated by a normal or weakly superconducting barrier. The Josephson phase difference is defined from gauge-invariant boundary data of the charged condensate, rather than from the black-hole charge itself, allowing a controlled extension of the standard holographic SNS junction to charged AdS backgrounds. We identify the current-phase relation, critical current, coherence length, and small-phase stiffness as the main observables. In the SNS regime, the critical current and midpoint condensate probe the same proximity scale, while higher harmonics in the current-phase relation diagnose enhanced transparency or departure from the opaque weak-link limit. The new ingredient is the near-extremal RN-AdS throat: as extremality is approached, the emergent AdS$_2\times\mathbb{R}^2$ region can radially dress the Josephson coupling before it reaches the ultraviolet boundary. After removing the ordinary spatial suppression due to the junction width, the residual critical current and phase stiffness are expected to exhibit scaling governed by the infrared dimension of the charged scalar in AdS$_2$. This separates ordinary proximity suppression, smooth finite-density corrections, and genuinely near-extremal throat control, providing a framework for phase-sensitive transport in charged holographic matter.

</details>

### [27] [Closing the loop on $Φ^4$ in AdS$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06589)
*Dean Carmi,Riccardo Ciccone,Shimon Sukholuski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在AdS₃时空中的Φ⁴理论框架下，计算了所有双迹算符（double-trace operators）[φφ]_{n,ℓ}的单圈修正CFT数据（CFT data），得到了用高阶超几何函数（higher hypergeometric functions）表示的有限闭式反常维数（anomalous dimensions），并讨论了其大自旋和高能行为以及完全单调性（completely monotonic）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在计算AdS₃中Φ⁴理论下双迹算符[φφ]_{n,ℓ}的CFT数据单圈修正，特别是对于任意主量子数n、自旋ℓ和标度维度（scaling dimension）Δ_φ>1的情形，以填补此前研究中参数范围的空白。

Method: 采用谱表示（spectral representation）方法，将t-通道单圈泡泡图（t-channel one-loop bubble diagram）简化为谱积分（spectral integrals）与共形6j符号（conformal 6j symbol）的乘积。谱积分及其后的留数求和均通过解析方法完成，最终得到用高阶超几何函数表达的有限闭式结果。

Result: 得到了双迹算符[φφ]_{n,ℓ}的单圈反常维数的解析闭式表达式，讨论了结果的结构，包括大自旋（large-spin）和高能（high-energy）行为，并证明反常维数在自旋上具有完全单调性（completely monotonic）。

Conclusion: 本文的解析计算结果为AdS/CFT对应（AdS/CFT correspondence）中双迹算符的量子修正提供了完整的描述，完全单调性等结构性结果有助于理解共形场论（conformal field theory）中算符乘积展开（operator product expansion, OPE）的收敛性质。

Abstract: We compute the one-loop correction to the CFT data of all double-trace operators $[φφ]_{n,\ell}$ for a $Φ^4$ theory in AdS$_3$, for arbitrary values of $n$, $\ell$, and of the scaling dimension $Δ_φ>1$. Working in the spectral representation, the $t$-channel one-loop bubble diagram is reduced to a product of spectral integrals dressed by the conformal $6j$ symbol. Both the spectral integrals and the subsequent sums over residues are performed analytically, yielding finite closed-form expressions for the anomalous dimensions in terms of higher hypergeometric functions. We discuss the structure of the results, including their large-spin and high-energy behaviors, and show that the anomalous dimensions are completely monotonic in spin.

### [28] [Instanton-Induced Closed-String Amplitudes in Minimal Superstring Theory at Subleading Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06596)
*Jyotirmoy Barman,Rishabh Kaushik,Raghu Mahajan,Chitraang Murdia,Ashoke Sen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究极小超弦理论中宇宙学常数算符的关联函数，并验证其是否满足DDK-KPZ标度律的预期；同时为十维类型IIB超弦中涉及玻色和费米集体坐标的次领头阶处理提供技术基础。

Method: 采用(1,1) ZZ瞬子边界条件，计算盘一点函数、盘两点函数和环面一点函数；利用开-闭弦场论对模空间积分中出现的开弦道退化发散进行规范；详细指定弦场论相互作用顶点中图像变更算符的位置，并通过垂直积分（vertical integration）贡献来完整确定所有项。

Result: 在仔细考虑所有贡献（包括垂直积分贡献）后，计算结果精确匹配DDK-KPZ标度律的预期结果。

Conclusion: 本文关于相互作用顶点详细构造的技术结果为理解十维类型IIB超弦中的类似量迈出了第一步，后者还需进一步理解如何在次领头阶处理玻色和费米集体坐标。

Abstract: We compute the disk one-point function, the disk two-point function, and the annulus one-point function of the cosmological constant operator in the type 0A and type 0B minimal superstring theories with (1,1) ZZ instanton boundary conditions. The moduli-space integrals appearing in the disk two-point function and the annulus one-point function have divergences associated with open-string-channel degenerations, which must be regulated using open-closed string field theory. The definition of the string field theory interaction vertices requires a choice of locations for the picture-changing operators, which we specify in detail. After carefully taking into account all contributions, including those from vertical integration, we find that the results precisely match the expectations from DDK-KPZ scaling. Our technical results on the detailed construction of interaction vertices are a first step toward understanding the analogous quantities in the ten-dimensional type IIB superstring, where one also needs to understand how to treat the bosonic and fermionic collective coordinates at subleading order.

### [29] [Boundary Layers and One-point Functions in the Presence of Monodromy Defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06602)
*Hugo Calvo Castro,Ignacio Carreño Bolla,Diego Rodriguez-Gomez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统地研究了U(1)整体对称性单值性缺陷（monodromy defect）背景下带电算符复合体的一点函数（one-point functions），涵盖自由质量理论、无质量理论以及全息对偶框架，发现了不同场景下sin²(eπβ)的依赖行为，并通过WKB分析和热核方法解析了鞍点结构和边界层效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解在存在单值性缺陷（monodromy defect）时，U(1)整体对称性下带电算符复合体一点函数的行为，从而填补自由理论、质量理论与全息理论之间关于单值性依赖的认知空白。

Method: 首先在自由无质量和质量理论中解析计算一点函数；然后在全息对偶（holography）框架下，针对su(N) N=4 SYM理论中U(1)∈SO(6)_R单值性缺陷下的算符O（荷J=Δ）计算一点函数，并利用大Δ下的WKB分析（WKB analysis）研究标准鞍点（standard saddles）和锚定鞍点（anchored saddles）结构；最后采用热核方法（heat kernel methods）确定复合算符O†O的诱导一点函数的单值性依赖。

Result: 在自由无质量理论中恢复了已知的sin(eπβ)依赖关系，在质量理论中得到了sin²(eπβ)依赖；在全息分析中，大Δ下的WKB分析验证了文献中标准鞍点和锚定鞍点的结构，并发现锚定区域（anchored regime）在1/Δ次领头阶下由边界层效应（boundary layer effect）所解析；复合算符O†O的诱导一点函数呈现光滑的sin²(Jπβ)行为。

Conclusion: 不同理论框架下单值性缺陷对一点函数的影响展现出不同的正弦函数依赖形式，其中全息框架下的边界层效应为锚定鞍点的亚领头阶修正提供了新的解析机制。

Abstract: We study one-point functions of composites of charge $e$ operators in the presence of a monodromy defect for a $U(1)$ global symmetry with monodromy $β$. We first compute these in free massless and massive theories, recovering in the former case the known $\sin(eπβ)$ dependence and obtaining in the latter a $\sin^2(eπβ)$ dependence. We then turn to holography and compute 1-point functions for operators $O$ of charge $J=Δ$ in $\mathfrak{su}(N)$ $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM in the presence of a monodromy defect for a $U(1)\in SO(6)_R$. From a WKB analysis in large $Δ$ we recover the structure of standard and anchored saddles previously found in the literature, finding that, to subleading order in $1/Δ$, the anchored regime is resolved by a boundary layer effect. Finally, using heat kernel methods, we determine the monodromy dependence of the induced 1-point function for the composite $O^{\dagger}O$, finding a smooth $\sin^2(Jπβ)$ behavior.

</details>


### [30] [Finite N Black Holes through the Brick Wall](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06613)
*Seiji Terashima*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过砖墙模型（brick-wall model）重新审视有限 N 下 AdS/CFT 中黑洞的微观描述，指出半经典体有效场论中近视界连续区在有限 N 下被离散量子系统取代，并分析了由此产生的吸收受限、残余反射与回声等效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限 N（finite N）的 AdS/CFT 中，黑洞由具有有限熵（finite entropy）和离散谱（discrete spectra）的普通量子系统描述，而半经典体有效场论（semiclassical bulk effective field theory）则将近视界区域视为理想连续体（ideal continuum）。这种矛盾需要一种有效的中间描述来捕捉有限 N 对半经典图像的修正。

Method: 作者重新采用砖墙模型，将其视为从半经典近视界连续体到有限 N 离散系统的简单有效过渡描述。模型中引入 Dirichlet 壁（Dirichlet wall），并通过将受调节的近壁模替换为相互作用的拉伸视界自由度（stretched-horizon degrees of freedom），使外部简单扇区呈现吸收性且类似黑洞的行为。

Result: 当拉伸视界自由度处于热布居而外部入射模处于真空态时，该模型可辐射出霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）。有限 N 阻止了近视界扇区成为理想连续吸收体，此局限性表现为残余反射（residual reflection）或回声（echoes）；这些回波效应的幅度不会被 e^{-S_{\rm BH}} 所压制，但其具体幅度依赖于具体模型。

Conclusion: 砖墙模型能有效刻画有限 N 下 AdS/CFT 中黑洞的量子修正特征，并自然导出霍金辐射与吸收受限导致的回波现象。此外，存在一类砖墙类模型，其有效内边界可由规则物质芯（regular matter core）动态产生，而非人为施加边界条件。

Abstract: In AdS/CFT at finite N, black holes are described by ordinary quantum systems with finite entropy and discrete spectra, while semiclassical bulk effective field theory treats the near-horizon region as an ideal continuum. We reconsider the brick-wall model as a simple effective description of the finite N departure from the semiclassical near-horizon continuum in AdS/CFT. A Dirichlet wall is reflecting; however, once the regulated near-wall modes are replaced by interacting stretched-horizon degrees of freedom, the exterior simple sector can look absorptive and black-hole-like. If these degrees of freedom are thermally populated while the exterior incoming modes are in their vacuum, they radiate as an ordinary hot object, and this gives Hawking radiation. Furthermore, we show that finite N prevents the near-horizon sector from being an ideal continuum absorber; the brick-wall model is a simple effective representation of this limitation, where the failure of perfect absorption appears as residual reflection or echoes. Such return effects will not be suppressed as $e^{-S_{\rm BH}}$, although their detailed amplitude is model-dependent. We also discuss brick-wall-like models in which the effective inner boundary arises dynamically from a regular matter core rather than from an imposed boundary condition.

</details>


### [31] [On Quantum Aspects of 1-Form Symmetries II: Bordism, Invertible Phases, and Anomalies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07056)
*Weizhen Jia,Yi-Nan Wang,Yi Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过可逆相和配边（bordism）理论，研究了与U(1) 1-形式对称性相关的量子反常（quantum anomalies），计算了Eilenberg-Mac Lane空间K(Z,3)的有向和旋量配边群至度8，发现了5维和7维理论中新的微扰和整体反常，并讨论了它们的边界实现与物理解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在从可逆相和配边视角系统研究U(1) 1-形式对称性（U(1) 1-form symmetry）相关的量子反常，填补高维反常分类和新型反常现象的理论空白。

Method: 利用Atiyah-Hirzebruch谱序列（Atiyah-Hirzebruch spectral sequence）计算Eilenberg-Mac Lane空间K(Z,3)的有向和旋量配边群至度8，通过几何论证（geometric arguments）解决相关的扩张问题（extension problems），并识别配边不变量（bordism invariants）与几何生成元（geometric generators）。

Result: 在5维理论中发现了一种U(1) 1-形式对称性与时空微分同胚（spacetime diffeomorphisms）之间的新混合微扰反常（mixed perturbative anomaly）；在7维理论中发现了一种内在属于U(1) 1-形式对称性的新的Z₂值离散反常（discrete anomaly）。

Conclusion: 这些反常项具有相应的边界实现（boundary realizations），并获得了新的物理解释，从而深化了对高维1-形式对称性反常结构的理解。

Abstract: We study quantum anomalies associated with $U(1)$ 1-form symmetries from the perspective of invertible phases and bordism. We compute the oriented and spin bordism groups of the Eilenberg-Mac Lane space $K(\mathbb{Z},3)$ up to degree 8 using the Atiyah-Hirzebruch spectral sequence, resolving the relevant extension problems by geometric arguments and identifying both bordism invariants and geometric generators. We then relate these invariants to perturbative and global anomalies, and discuss physical examples and top-down constructions of the corresponding anomaly terms. For 5-dimensional theories, we find a new mixed perturbative anomaly between the $U(1)$ 1-form symmetry and spacetime diffeomorphisms, while for 7-dimensional theories we find a new $\mathbb{Z}_2$-valued discrete anomaly intrinsic to the $U(1)$ 1-form symmetry. We also discuss their boundary realizations and give new physical interpretations of these anomalies.

</details>


### [32] [Wick-connected theories and Lorentz violation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07243)
*Niklas Götzberger,Anamaria Hell*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在场论中实施双Wick转动（double Wick rotation）时，若洛伦兹不变性（Lorentz-invariance）缺失，则原本通过Wick转动相连的理论不再等价。作者聚焦于平坦时空，分析了传播模式（propagating modes）、幺正性（unitarity）与可重整化性（renormalizability）在这些Wick相连理论中的表现，并给出了这些概念失效的条件判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Wick转动是将时间坐标解析延拓到虚时，从而在欧几里得（Euclidean）与洛伦兹（Lorentzian）场论之间建立对应。双Wick转动进一步将某个空间方向重新解释为新的洛伦兹时间，这种操作在缺失洛伦兹不变性的理论中是否仍能保持等价性尚未被系统研究。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 作者采用分析的手法，考虑一般场论中的双Wick转动操作，通过对比Wick相连理论在传播模式、幺正性与可重整化性方面的性质，判定这些概念能否在理论之间忠实地传递。研究在平坦时空背景下进行，并以洛伦兹不变性作为关键判据。

Result: 研究表明，当洛伦兹不变性缺失时，通过双Wick转动相连的理论不再必然等价。具体而言，传播模式的性质、幺正性（unitarity）以及可重整化性（renormalizability）等核心物理概念在Wick相连理论之间可能无法保持一致。论文提供了判断这些概念何时失效的明确判据。

Conclusion: 双Wick转动的有效性依赖于洛伦兹不变性；一旦该对称性被破坏，Wick相连的理论之间可能出现不等价性。这一结论对于非洛伦兹场论（如某些凝聚态系统或有效场论）中的解析延拓操作具有重要的警示意义。

Abstract: We consider double Wick rotation in field theories, which analytically continues the time coordinate, and then reinterprets one of the spatial directions as the new Lorentzian time. We show that if Lorentz-invariance is absent, Wick-connected theories are no longer necessarily equivalent. Focusing on flat spacetime, we study the propagating modes, unitarity and renormalizability of such Wick-connected theories, and provide criteria for when such notions fail to translate.

</details>


### [33] [On the large N convergence of matrix models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07504)
*M. P. Garcia del Moral,P. León,A. Restuccia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，在环面紧化靶空间中，带有中心荷的超膜（supermembrane/M2-brane）模型的哈密顿量本征值，可由其SU(N)正则化矩阵模型在大N极限下半经典近似下精确恢复，二者一一对应且收敛于相同值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 比较超对称矩阵模型（supersymmetric matrix model）与精确连续统描述之间的大N行为，验证正则化方案在大N极限下的有效性。

Method: 针对定义在可微紧环面上的超膜模型（结构群为面积保持微分同胚群（area-preserving diffeomorphisms））及其SU(N)正则化模型，分析约束结构的代数对应关系，并采用半经典近似（semiclassical approximation）计算大N极限下的本征值。

Result: 在大N极限下的半经典近似中，超对称矩阵模型哈密顿量的本征值与带有中心荷的超膜哈密顿量的本征值一一对应且精确收敛。

Conclusion: 中心荷（central charge）在紧化超膜中起到关键作用，允许自上而下的SU(N)正则化，且正则化模型的离散谱性质在大N极限下与连续统模型一致，支持了矩阵模型作为膜理论有效正则化方案的结论。

Abstract: In this paper, the large N behavior of a supersymmetric matrix model is compared with its exact continuum description. We concentrate on the large N limit of a supersymmetric matrix model describing a supermembrane with central charge on a toroidally compactified target space. We analyze, on the one hand, the supermembrane model formulated on a differentiable compact torus without boundary, with structure group given by the area-preserving diffeomorphisms, and, on the other hand, the associated regularized $SU(N)$ model. We emphasize in our analysis the structure of the constraints of the regularized model, which generate the $SU(N)$ algebra and reproduce the area-preserving diffeomorphism algebra in the large N limit, together with the topological information associated with the central charge of the model. We explain the role of the central charge in the compactified supermembrane and how it allows a top-down $SU(N)$ regularization. It is known that the regularized model has discrete spectrum. We prove, in the semiclassical approximation of the models, that in the large N limit the eigenvalues of the Hamiltonian of the supersymmetric matrix model are in one to one correspondence with, and converge exactly to, the eigenvalues of the Hamiltonian of the supermembrane (M2-brane) with central charge. Finally, we discuss some physical consequences of this result.

### [34] [Boundary criticality in the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa model at higher orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07510)
*Oleksandr Diatlyk,Simone Giombi,Zimo Sun*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在Gross-Neveu-Yukawa普适类中，超越领头阶研究了边界临界性。利用双曲空间形式的边界共形场论，在大N下计算了“正常”、“普通”和“特殊”边界普适类自由能的首次次领头修正，并确定了正常固定点处边界费米子维度的1/N阶修正。在d=4-ε的Gross-Neveu-Yukawa理论中，进行了边界自由能的高阶分析，并提取了d=3下边界中心荷的估计。大N与ε展开结果在重叠区域精确一致，为边界普适类的识别提供了非平凡的一致性检验。计算结合了AdS调和分析与边界共形场论技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Gross-Neveu-Yukawa普适类（Gross-Neveu-Yukawa universality class）中边界临界性（boundary criticality）的研究从领头阶推广至次领头阶，从而更精确地理解其边界普适类的性质。

Method: 采用双曲空间形式（hyperbolic space formulation）的边界共形场论（boundary conformal field theory, BCFT），结合AdS调和分析（AdS harmonic analysis）与边界共形场论技术，在大N展开和ε-展开（ε-expansion）下进行系统性计算。

Result: 获得了“正常”、“普通”和“特殊”三种边界普适类（boundary universality classes）自由能的首次次领头阶大N修正，以及正常固定点处边界费米子维度的1/N阶修正。在d=3下给出了边界中心荷（boundary central charge）的高阶估计值。大N与ε展开结果在重叠区域精确一致。

Conclusion: 大N与ε展开结果之间精确的一致性，为边界普适类的识别提供了非平凡的一致性检验（consistency check），表明所采用的计算框架是可靠且自洽的。

Abstract: We extend the study of boundary criticality in the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa universality class beyond leading order. Using the hyperbolic space formulation of boundary conformal field theories, we compute the first subleading corrections at large $N$ to the free energies of the ``normal", ``ordinary" and ``special" boundary universality classes. We also determine the order $1/N$ correction to the dimension of the boundary fermion at the normal fixed point. In the Gross-Neveu-Yukawa theory in $d=4-ε$, we perform a higher-order analysis of the boundary free energy, and use it to extract estimates for the boundary central charge in $d=3$. The large $N$ and $ε$-expansion results are shown to be precisely consistent in overlapping regimes, providing nontrivial consistency checks for the identification of the boundary universality classes. Our calculations rely on a combination of AdS harmonic analysis and boundary conformal field theory techniques.

### [35] [Odd-parity perturbations of trace-quadratic $f(R,T)$ black holes with anisotropic matter: admissible branches, axial ringdown, and a coupled-PINN benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06517)
*Mushtaq Ahmad,M. Farasat Shamir,Adnan Malik,Ahdab K. Althukair*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究迹二次 $f(R,T)=R+\alpha T^2$ 引力中静态黑洞的奇宇称（odd-parity）引力扰动，发现可容许的参数分支位于负径向闭包参数 $w_r$ 区域，并证明在静态可容许背景下奇宇称扇区严格等价于耦合冻结有效各向异性流体的爱因斯坦引力。通过精确 Chebyshev 求解和物理信息神经网络（PINN）计算，发现轴向环影（ringdown）的主要可观测量印来自物质支持分支本身，而非迹耦合 $\alpha$ 的直接变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在修正引力理论中，$f(R,T)$ 引力因其物质-引力耦合而引入额外自由度，但高阶扰动（尤其是奇宇称扇区）的参数空间约束与可观测量之间的联系尚未充分理解。本文旨在系统识别迹二次 $f(R,T)$ 引力中静态黑洞可容许的多参数空间区域，并评估轴向环影在可观测层面的物理特征。

Method: 从未约化轴向（unreduced axial）系统及其主符号入手，识别出支持正则视界、渐近平坦性和双曲型奇宇称演化的参数空间扇区。在静态可容许背景上严格证明奇宇称扇区等价于耦合冻结有效各向异性流体的爱因斯坦引力，进而得到单一规范不变的主方程（master equation）。采用精确 Chebyshev 数值求解方法计算基态轴向 $\ell=2$ 拟正规模（quasinormal mode），并构建耦合物理信息神经网络对未约化两场本征问题进行分析。

Result: 可容许分支位于负 $w_r$ 区间，常用正 $w_r$ 族不满足背景正则性测试，仅作为数值比较分支保留。锚定分支 $(w_r,w_t)=(-0.2,0.15)$ 的质量归一化拟正规模谱与 Schwarzschild 黑洞相差约 $22\%$，但在 $0\le \alpha/M^2\le 0.3$ 范围内未发现统计显著的直接 $\alpha$ 依赖性。闭包层次审计显示锚定族满足零能量条件（null energy condition）、弱能量条件（weak energy condition）和主导能量条件（dominant energy condition）的正诊断组合，修正平衡律分母安全，有效外部质量分数约为 $20\%$。

Conclusion: 在 $f(R,T)=R+\alpha T^2$ 引力中，轴向环影的主要可观测量印来自物质支持分支自身的存在，而非迹耦合 $\alpha$ 的直接变化。常数 $(w_r,w_t)$ 模型应被视为有效各向异性应力（effective anisotropic stress）而非微观物理流体。可容许参数空间被限制在负 $w_r$ 区域，这与常规正 $w_r$ 假设形成鲜明对比。

Abstract: We study odd-parity gravitational perturbations of static black holes in trace-quadratic $f(R,T)=R+αT^2$ gravity supported by an anisotropic effective fluid with constant closure parameters $(w_r,w_t)$. From the unreduced axial system and its principal symbol, we identify the sector of parameter space that supports a regular horizon, asymptotic flatness, and hyperbolic odd-sector evolution. Within this closure the admissible branch lies at negative $w_r$, while the commonly used positive-$w_r$ family fails the background regularity test and is kept only as a numerical comparison branch. On static admissible backgrounds the odd sector is exactly equivalent to Einstein gravity coupled to a frozen effective anisotropic fluid, so the physical axial spectrum is governed by a single gauge-invariant master equation. For the anchored branch $(w_r,w_t)=(-0.2,0.15)$ we compute the fundamental axial $\ell=2$ quasinormal mode with an exact Chebyshev solve. The mass-normalized spectrum differs from Schwarzschild by about $22\%$, whereas no statistically resolved direct $α$-dependence appears within the conservative spectral envelope over $0\le α/M^2\le 0.3$. We also construct a coupled physics-informed neural network for the unreduced two-field eigenproblem and use it to benchmark the inadmissible comparison branch. A closure-level audit of the anchored family shows positive diagnostic combinations associated with the null, weak, and dominant energy conditions, denominator safety in the modified balance law, and an effective exterior mass fraction of about $20\%$, while indicating that the constant-$(w_r,w_t)$ model should be read as an effective anisotropic stress rather than as a microphysical fluid. Within this closure, the main observable imprint in axial ringdown comes from the existence of the matter-supported branch itself, not from direct variation of the trace coupling.

### [36] [GUP-corrected black holes: Thermodynamic properties, evaporation time and shadow constraint from EHT Observations of M87* and Sgr A*](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06548)
*H. Chen,S. -H. Dong,E. Maghsoodi,S. Hassanabadi,J. Křiž,S. Zare,H. Hassanabadi*

Conclusion: GUP修正对Schwarzschild黑洞的热力学和相变产生显著影响，且通过EHT观测数据可有效限制GUP参数，其中Sgr A*的约束效果优于M87*。

Abstract: In this manuscript, we implement the generalized uncertainty principle (GUP) with linear and quadratic moment for Schwarzschild black hole metric in order to study the influence of quantum effect on the thermodynamics and evaporation of black hole. To this end, we first derive the GUP-modified Hawking temperature of a black hole in the semi-classical framework. Due to the existence of the GUP effect, there is a maximum Hawking temperature. We determine the entropy, heat capacity and Helmholtz free energy with heuristic analysis that investigates the particle absorbed by black hole. Furthermore, we also verify that these quantities are modified by the GUP, the influence of quantum effect on the black hole phase transition is discussed in detail. Then, we analyze the black hole evaporation process in the mentioned framework and examine the obtained results by graphical methods and compare them with each other. We likewise explore the behavior of the event horizon radius, photon sphere radius, and shadow silhouette when influenced by the GUP-corrected Schwarzschild black hole (GCSBH) parameters. We intend to establish restrictions for $α$ by utilizing the event horizon telescope (EHT) data for M87* and Sagittarius A* (Sgr A*). Our findings show that Sgr A* provides more robust constraints. As the parameter $β$ grows, the range of constraints for $α$ expands. For Sgr A* one, we find that the shadow radius is close to the observed value at smaller values of $α$.

### [37] [Robustness of the relativistic intermediate-axis instability around dark-matter-dressed rotating black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06557)
*Mohsen Fathi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: DARK-FLIP II 通过受控有效响应模型（effective response model, ERM）验证了在暗物质（dark matter, DM）影响下，环绕旋转黑洞的非轴对称物质元素的中间轴不稳定翻转频率（flip frequency）对 DM 晕轮廓的敏感性，确认该翻转频率可作为受控的 DM 敏感定向时钟（orientation clock）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验 DARK-FLIP I 提出的半解析框架的稳健性，探究当局部环境因暗物质（DM）晕轮廓改变时，中间轴不稳定（intermediate-axis instability, IAI）的翻转频率如何响应。

Method: 采用受控有效响应模型（effective response model, ERM），而非完整的吸积或辐射转移模拟。变化参数包括 DM 归一化量、轮廓标度半径、中间主转动惯量、有效潮汐耦合、初始扰动及初始取向。使用 Einasto 和规则化核尖 Navarro–Frenk–White（cored-NFW）作为主要 DM 模型，Hernquist 作为控制基准。分析手段涵盖一维扫描、二维响应图、轮廓对比图、时域翻转模拟、轮廓时序响应诊断及局部投影发射率代理。

Result: 存在清晰的扰动趋势：包围 DM 归一化量的增加会降低相对于 Kerr 时空的翻转频率，而更延展的 DM 轮廓会削弱局部响应。

Conclusion: DARK-FLIP II 强化了将翻转频率解释为受控的 DM 敏感定向时钟（DM-sensitive orientation clock）的论点。

Abstract: DARK-FLIP I introduced a semi-analytical and Python-based framework for studying a relativistic version of the intermediate-axis instability (IAI) of a coherent non-axisymmetric matter element around rotating black holes dressed by dark matter (DM). In this second paper I test the robustness of that idea. The main question is simple: if the local environment is changed by the DM profile, how does the flip frequency respond? To answer this, I use a controlled effective response model (ERM), not a full accretion or radiative-transfer simulation. The flip frequency is therefore treated as a diagnostic orientation-modulation timescale, not as a direct quasi-periodic oscillation (QPO) model. I vary the DM normalization, profile scale radius, intermediate principal moment of inertia, effective tidal coupling, initial perturbation, and initial orientation. Einasto and regularized cored Navarro--Frenk--White (cored-NFW) profiles are used as the main DM models, while Hernquist is kept as a control benchmark. The analysis includes one-dimensional scans, two-dimensional response maps, profile-contrast maps, time-domain flip simulations, a profile timing-response diagnostic, and a local projected-emissivity proxy. The results show a clear perturbative trend: increasing the enclosed DM normalization decreases the flip frequency relative to Kerr, while more extended profiles weaken the local response. DARK-FLIP II therefore strengthens the interpretation of the flip frequency as a controlled DM-sensitive orientation clock.

</details>

*Adrian Ka-Wai Chung,Kelvin Ka-Ho Lam,Anna Liu,Nicolas Yunes*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种引力波（gravitational-wave）方法，从并合前期的直接波（direct waves）中推断克尔等效黑洞视界面积（Kerr-equivalent horizon area）。将其应用于GW250114事件，发现在峰值振幅前3–4.5M（M为总质量）时段的分析得到的面积与克尔残余黑洞（Kerr remnant）一致，从而首次通过直接波实现黑洞面积测量，并对霍金面积定律（Hawking's area law）进行了近并合阶段的新检验。

Result: 将该方法应用于引力波事件GW250114，发现峰值振幅前3–4.5M时间窗口内的分析所得面积与克尔残余黑洞（Kerr remnant）的面积一致。这是首次通过直接波实现黑洞面积的测量。

Conclusion: 该结果给出了基于直接波的首个黑洞面积测量，并为霍金面积定律（Hawking's area law）提供了一个新的近并合阶段检验手段。

Abstract: Black-hole area is the geometric variable behind horizon thermodynamics. Applied to GW250114, and interpreting the fitted direct-wave frequency and damping rate as horizon quantities, we find that analyses initiated $3$--$4.5M$ before the peak-amplitude time yield an area consistent with the Kerr remnant.
