### [39] [Radial Oscillations of Viscous Stars at Finite Temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06600)
*Amanda Guerrieri,Gabriel S. Rocha,Gabriel S. Denicol,Raissa F. P. Mendes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Israel-Stewart理论与Navier-Stokes理论框架下，研究了包含热扩散和热力学自洽有限温度状态方程的相对论性恒星的径向振荡谱，揭示了热扇区模式的结构及其与无穷耗散流体色散关系的对应，并发现有限几何效应可使热模式从纯阻尼转变为传播行为，为致密星中的相对论第二声提供了有限尺寸实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前对粘性恒星径向振荡的分析尚未完整纳入热扩散这一最后的耗散自由度（dissipative degree of freedom），本文旨在填补这一空白，通过引入热通量（heat flux）和有限温度状态方程（finite-temperature equation of state）来完善Israel-Stewart框架下的恒星振荡理论。

Method: 在Israel-Stewart理论与Navier-Stokes理论中求解相对论性恒星的径向振荡谱，同时引入热扩散和热力学自洽的有限温度状态方程；采用Sommerfeld型微扰（Sommerfeld-type perturbation）形式的冷多方球（cold polytrope）有限温度修正，构建平直时空色散关系（flat-spacetime dispersion relations）的解析ansatz来捕捉离散恒星谱。

Result: 热通量的引入使模式谱中出现独立的热扇区（thermal sector），其结构与无穷耗散流体的色散关系高度一致；在Israel-Stewart理论中，热模式在超过临界泛音数（critical overtone number）时从纯阻尼（purely damped）转变为传播行为（propagating behavior），且有限恒星几何可推动基本热模式进入传播区；热扇区与普通流体振荡谱的耦合在温度参数中为二阶，耦合较弱。

Conclusion: 本文在Israel-Stewart框架内完整了粘性恒星径向振荡分析，纳入了最后一项耗散自由度；研究结果为致密星中相对论第二声（relativistic second sound）的有限尺寸实现提供了理论依据，并表明解析色散关系的离散化方案能有效描述恒星离散谱。

Abstract: We study the radial oscillation spectrum of relativistic stars within Israel-Stewart and Navier-Stokes theories, extending previous analyses to include heat diffusion and a thermodynamically consistent finite-temperature equation of state. The inclusion of heat flux gives rise to a distinct thermal sector in the mode spectrum, whose structure closely mirrors the dispersion relations of an infinite dissipative fluid. Within Israel-Stewart theory, the thermal modes transition from purely damped to propagating behavior above a critical overtone number, providing a finite-size realization of relativistic second sound in compact stars. Remarkably, the finite stellar geometry can push even the fundamental thermal mode into the propagating regime -- a feature with no continuum analogue. For the class of equations of state considered here, where finite-temperature corrections enter as controlled, Sommerfeld-type perturbations of a cold polytrope, the thermal sector couples only weakly to the ordinary fluid oscillation spectrum, with the coupling being of second order in a suitable temperature parameter. We further show that the discrete stellar spectrum is well captured by an analytic ansatz constructed from the flat-spacetime dispersion relations, with the star's finite radius discretizing the continuous mode structure. Our results complete the analysis of radial oscillations of viscous stars by incorporating the last remaining dissipative degree of freedom within the Israel-Stewart framework.

### [40] [Gravitational waveforms from binaries in higher-derivative gravity: a Love story](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07070)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先推导了在含有任意源项时，描述宇称偶（even-parity）和宇称奇（odd-parity）扰动的控制方程（master equations）；然后构建了齐次控制方程解的后闵可夫斯基展开（Post-Minkowskian expansion）；针对圆形双星系统（circular binary system），计算了波形（waveform）的后牛顿展开（Post-Newtonian expansion）以及无穷远处的能量流（energy flux）和角动量流（angular-momentum flux）。

Result: 高阶导数修正项总是出现在5PN（post-Newtonian）阶，并且与描述ℓ=2模（mode）扰动下几何可变形性（deformability）的Love数（Love number）成正比。数值计算（numerical computations）结果与解析结果一致，并将分析扩展到了更高速度情形。

Conclusion: 高阶导数引力对引力波信号的影响在5PN阶开始显现，且与几何的Love数呈普适的比例关系。这一结果为未来通过引力波观测约束高阶引力理论提供了理论依据和可检验的预言。

Abstract: We study the emission of gravitational waves by a test particle orbiting a non-rotating black hole in higher-derivative gravity theories with cubic and quartic contractions of the Riemann tensor. To this aim, we first derive the master equations describing even- and odd-parity perturbations in the presence of an arbitrary source term, and then construct a Post-Minkowskian expansion of the solutions to the homogeneous master equations. Specializing to a circular binary system, we compute the Post-Newtonian expansion of the waveform, as well as the energy and angular-momentum fluxes at infinity. We show that higher-derivative corrections to the waveform and to the fluxes always appear at 5PN order, and are universally proportional to the Love number describing the deformability of the geometry under the $\ell=2$ mode perturbation. These analytical results are validated against numerical computations, which also allow us to extend the analysis to larger velocities.

### [41] [Vanishing of all redshift modes in Schwarzschild ringdown](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07173)
*Adrien Kuntz,Matteo Della Rocca*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 对于史瓦西黑洞，粒子坠入黑洞产生的环down信号中，红移模、视界模和直达波在可观测波形中的振幅均为零；这一抵消源于因果性，并揭示了准正则模式叠加与脉冲贡献之间的精确对消关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明，粒子坠入黑洞产生的环down（ringdown）信号中存在以表面引力（surface gravity）整数倍衰减的贡献，称为红移模（redshift modes）、视界模（horizon modes）和直达波（direct waves）。本文旨在证明这些贡献在可观测波形中振幅为零，并揭示其背后的物理机制。

Method: 基于因果性（causality）论证，证明源积分后的格林函数（source-integrated Green function）在光锥（light cone）上为零，从而直接导致红移模等贡献的振幅为零。进一步通过分析准正则模（quasinormal mode, QNM）过音（overtones）的求和，展示各过音中非零的红移模贡献在求和后精确抵消，而波形中的脉冲贡献（impulsive contribution）恰好充当了实现这一抵消的反项（counterterm）。

Result: 对于史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black holes），红移模、视界模和直达波在可观测波形中的振幅均为零。单个准正则模过音仍携带非零的红移模贡献，但这些贡献在过音求和后精确抵消；脉冲贡献正是执行这一抵消的反项。此外，为准正则模激发系数的标准正则化（regularization）提供了动机——因为发散导致了红移模为零。

Conclusion: 红移模等贡献在可观测波形中完全消失，其根本原因是因果性导致的格林函数在光锥上为零。这一发现不仅澄清了环down信号中各成分的实际角色，也为准正则模激发系数的正则化提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Several studies of black hole ringdown from particles plunging into black holes have identified contributions decaying at integer multiples of the surface gravity, called redshift modes, horizon modes, and direct waves. We show that, for Schwarzschild black holes, every one of these contributions has vanishing amplitude in the observable waveform. The cancellation follows from causality, which forces the source-integrated Green function to vanish on the light cone. Individual quasi-normal mode overtones still carry non-zero redshift-mode contributions, but these cancel exactly once the sum over overtones is performed; the so-called impulsive contribution to the waveform acts precisely as the counterterm enforcing this cancellation. Finally, we provide a motivation to the standard regularization of quasinormal mode excitation coefficients since divergences give rise to vanishing redshift modes.

</details>

Similar to what happens with Killing vectors, the construction works on any background, providing a "physical visualization" of its symmetries. ### [43] [Loss of the Scaling Attractor in Self-Gravitating Domain Wall Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07296)
*Zhen-Min Zeng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文通过将速度依赖单尺度模型（velocity-dependent one-scale model）与弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equation）及辐射能量转移相耦合，研究了畴壁网络（domain-wall networks）的自洽演化。结果表明，一旦将膨胀率提升为动力学自由度，辐射时代的缩放解（scaling solution）便会从稳定吸引子（stable attractor）退化为鞍点（saddle），且物理相空间中不存在稳定不动点。缩放 regime 仅作为瞬态阶段存在，所有轨迹最终都趋向于壁主导（wall-dominated）且运动学受挫（kinematically frustrated）的状态，即壁在共动坐标系中冻结。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有理论认为畴壁网络在固定辐射主导和物质主导背景下会接近相对论性缩放 regime，构成“无受挫猜想”（no-frustration conjecture）的基础。然而，该图像假设缺陷网络在引力上始终是次主导的，未考虑引力反作用（gravitational backreaction）对网络动力学的反馈效应。本文旨在探究自引力条件下畴壁网络的真实演化行为。

Method: 将速度依赖单尺度模型（velocity-dependent one-scale model）与弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equation）及辐射能量传递方程耦合，构建自治动力系统（autonomous system）。该方法使宇宙膨胀历史能够动态演化，而非作为外部固定背景施加。

Result: 解析证明引力反作用会定性改变相空间结构：在固定背景下的辐射时代吸引子解，在膨胀率成为动力学自由度后退化为鞍点。物理相空间中不存在稳定不动点。缩放 regime 仅作为瞬态存在，所有轨迹最终趋于壁主导且运动学受挫状态，壁在共动坐标系中冻结。

Conclusion: 缩放吸引子（scaling attractor）在自引力畴壁网络中无法维持；揭示出壁主导的晚期受挫动力学（frustration dynamics）是自洽演化的一般性结果，否定了无受挫猜想在自引力情形下的适用性。

Abstract: Domain-wall(DW) networks are known to approach a relativistic scaling regime on fixed radiation- and matter-dominated backgrounds, forming the basis of the no-frustration conjecture. However, this picture assumes that the defect network remains gravitationally subdominant. We investigate the self-consistent evolution of DWs by coupling the velocity-dependent one-scale model to the Friedmann equation and radiation energy transfer. The resulting autonomous system allows the cosmic expansion history to evolve dynamically rather than being imposed externally. We demonstrate analytically that gravitational backreaction qualitatively changes the phase-space structure: the radiation-era scaling solution, which is a stable attractor on a fixed background, becomes a saddle once the expansion rate is promoted to a dynamical degree of freedom. Furthermore, we establish that no stable fixed point exists within the physical phase space. Consequently, the scaling regime survives only as a transient stage, and all trajectories are driven toward a wall dominated and kinematically frustrated state in which the walls freeze in comoving coordinates. Our results demonstrate that the scaling attractor is not preserved in self-gravitating DW networks and reveal the generic late-time frustration dynamics of wall domination.

### [44] [Red noise and evolving signals: a complete frequentist approach to supermassive black hole binary searches with pulsar timing array](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07330)
*Xuan Tao,Boris Goncharov,Yiqian Qian,Yan Wang,Soumya D. Mohanty*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对脉冲星测时阵列（PTA）数据中孤立超大型黑洞双星（SMBHB）的引力波搜索问题，提出了一种广义似然比检验（GLRT）及其对应的𝒯统计量。该方法通过半解析最大化脉冲星相位参数的似然函数，再结合粒子群优化（PSO）对剩余参数进行全局优化，有效解决了模型维度随脉冲星数量增长的计算难题，并能处理包含地球项与脉冲星项的信号演化问题。模拟显示，在30颗脉冲星的阵列中，该检测统计量在信噪比20的条件下实现了100%的检测概率与0.06的虚警概率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有频率学派方法（如ℱ统计量）仅限于非演化源，且隐含了圆形分析（circular analysis），可能导致有偏估计。同时，包含引力波源演化时需同时保留地球项与脉冲星项，引入未知的脉冲星距离，导致拟合维度随脉冲星数量线性增长，计算困难显著加剧。

Method: 提出广义似然比检验（GLRT）及𝒯统计量。首先对脉冲星相位参数进行半解析最大化，将似然函数维度大幅降低；随后对剩余参数采用粒子群优化（Particle Swarm Optimization）进行高效全局搜索。

Result: 模拟结果表明：对于啁啾质量ℳ=10^9.2 M⊙、信噪比为20的演化型超大型黑洞双星信号，在包含30颗脉冲星、100 ns均方根白噪声残差及脉冲星特定红噪声的阵列中，该检测统计量在虚警概率0.06条件下实现了100%的检测概率。

Conclusion: 该GLRT框架及𝒯统计量克服了现有方法对非演化源的限制与计算维度过高的问题，为PTA数据中演化型超大型黑洞双星引力波信号的检测提供了高效且无偏的统计推断工具。

Abstract: Searches for gravitational waves (GWs) from isolated supermassive black hole binaries (SMBHBs) in pulsar timing array (PTA) data require simultaneous estimation of signal and noise parameters, so the dimensionality of the fit scales with the number of observed pulsars. This computational difficulty is exacerbated when source evolution from GW emission is included, since retaining both Earth and pulsar terms introduces the unknown pulsar distances. Existing frequentist methods such as the $\mathcal{F}$-statistic, restricted so far to non-evolving sources, effectively, imply a circular analysis, which may lead to biased estimators. We present a Generalized Likelihood Ratio Test (GLRT) and the associated $\mathcal{T}$-statistic that overcomes the aforementioned limitations. The formulation of the GLRT extends earlier work in which the dimensionality of the fitting problem was drastically reduced by semi-analytical maximization of the likelihood over the pulsar phase parameters, followed by efficient global optimization over the remaining parameters using Particle Swarm Optimization. Our simulations demonstrate that for an evolving SMBHB signal with chirp mass $\mathcal{M}=10^{9.2}\,M_\odot$ and signal-to-noise ratio $20$, this detection statistic achieves a $100\%$ detection probability at a false-alarm probability of $0.06$ in a 30-pulsar timing array, which is characterized by a $100~\mathrm{ns}$ root-mean-square white noise residual and pulsar-specific red noise.

### [45] [Stochastic scalar-tensor inflation and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07467)
*Yoann Launay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于有效场论框架，将随机暴胀（stochastic inflation）形式从广义相对论（General Relativity）推广至更广泛的非线性标量-张量理论（scalar-tensor theories），通过规范无关的粗粒化程序（gauge-agnostic coarse-graining procedure）推导随机运动方程，并在Gauss-Bonnet、广义Brans-Dicke、Horndeski等多个理论中给出具体实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子真空涨落在暴胀期间被拉伸至超哈勃尺度并有效经典化，但其非线性和红外微扰失效问题需要随机暴胀范式来处理。然而，这一随机形式仅在广义相对论中得到了自洽构造，尚未被推广至更一般的早期宇宙理论，本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用规范无关的粗粒化程序，将暗能量有效场论（effective field theory of dark energy）的线性方程应用于一大类完全非线性的标量-张量理论。通过识别每种理论在有效场论（EFT）中的相应系数，将其映射至各自的随机运动方程。

Result: 提供了Gauss-Bonnet、广义Brans-Dicke、Horndeski以及braiding理论等具体且多数为首例的随机形式实例。此外，还展示了广义相对论中多场暴胀（multifield inflation）的粗粒化处理，论证了该程序的通用性。

Conclusion: 本文建立的随机框架具有现象学完整性，证明了规范无关粗粒化程序具有广泛适用性，其潜在应用可拓展至暴胀之外的更多宇宙学场景。

Abstract: During cosmological inflation, inhomogeneities arising from quantum vacuum fluctuations are stretched to become super-Hubble and effectively classical. As many scenarios of the origin involve nonlinearities or a breakdown of perturbativity in the infrared, the limitations of quantum field theory can be addressed using a stochastic description of the dynamics, the so-called stochastic inflation paradigm. However, the stochastic formalism was only recently formulated consistently within full General Relativity and has not yet been extended to more general theories of the early universe, which is the subject of this work.
  In order to find the stochastic sources for a wide class of fully nonlinear scalar-tensor theories, we apply our gauge-agnostic coarse-graining procedure to the linear equations of the effective field theory of dark energy. Each theory can then be mapped to its own set of stochastic equations of motion by identifying the corresponding coefficients in the EFT. We illustrate this with a few concrete and, in most cases, unprecedented examples, including Gauss-Bonnet, generalized Brans-Dicke, Horndeski, and braiding theories.
  Finally, we discuss other natural extensions to provide a phenomenologically complete stochastic framework. For example, we showcase the coarse-graining of multifield inflation in full General Relativity and argue for the generality of our procedure and thus its potential applications beyond the realm of inflation.

</details>

### [46] [Distilling first-principles accuracy into compact machine learning potentials for condensed-phase chemistry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06848)
*Sijia Chen,Niamh O'Neill,Benjamin X. Shi,Venkat Kapil*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本研究结合迁移学习（transfer learning）与知识蒸馏（knowledge distillation），将大型教师模型压缩为紧凑的学生模型，使计算成本降低约一个数量级，同时保持第一性原理级别的精度。在冰相、液态水及TiO2/水界面等复杂凝聚相问题中，蒸馏学生模型可靠地重现了教师模型的目标可观测量，并使核量子效应（nuclear quantum effects）的路径积分模拟（path-integral simulations）变得可行，定量解释了实验中的界面反应热力学数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高精度机器学习原子间势能（MLIPs）虽已使第一性原理精度的势能面（potential energy surfaces）在凝聚相化学中越来越易获得，但其推理成本仍限制了获取实验可观测量所需的大规模采样，亟需在不牺牲精度的前提下降低计算成本。

Method: 将迁移学习与知识蒸馏相结合：先通过迁移学习将基础模型（foundation models）应用于目标体系获得大型教师模型（teacher model），再通过知识蒸馏从教师模型训练紧凑的学生模型（student model），在保持高精度的同时将生产模拟计算成本降低约一个数量级。

Result: 在冰Ih的有限温度NPT模拟、液态水（240-370K）的经典与路径积分模拟以及锐钛矿TiO2(101)/水界面的路径积分伞形采样（umbrella sampling）水 dissociation 模拟中，蒸馏学生模型均比相同规模但直接在有限参考数据上训练的模型更可靠地再现教师模型的目标可观测量。液水学生模型（从Δ-learned CCSD(T)质量教师蒸馏）在全部温度范围内准确重现热力学、结构、输运及核量子性质。在TiO2/水界面，蒸馏使路径积分分子动力学（PIMD）伞形采样变得可行，揭示核量子效应使 dissociation 势垒降低约2 kcal/mol，并将分子-解离自由能差修正至与近期固态17O NMR测量定量一致。

Conclusion: 知识蒸馏能够使高精度MLIPs在凝聚相反应热力学与实验连接所需的采样方法中变得实用，尤其适用于界面化学与催化研究中的挑战性凝聚相问题。

Abstract: Accurate machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) have made first-principles-quality potential energy surfaces increasingly accessible for condensed-phase chemistry, but their inference cost can still limit the sampling needed to compute experimentally relevant observables. In this work, we combine transfer learning and knowledge distillation to construct compact "student" models that retain the accuracy of much larger "teacher" models obtained by applying transfer learning to foundation models. The resulting students reduce production simulation cost by roughly an order of magnitude, making high-accuracy sampling practical for challenging condensed-phase problems. We demonstrate this across three problems of increasing sampling complexity: finite-temperature NPT simulations of ice Ih, classical and path-integral simulations of liquid water over 240-370 K, and path-integral umbrella-sampling simulations of water dissociation at the anatase TiO2(101)/water interface. In all cases, the distilled students reproduce the target observables of their teachers more reliably than models of the same size trained directly on the limited reference data. The liquid-water student, distilled from a Δ-learned CCSD(T)-quality teacher, reproduces thermodynamic, structural, transport, and nuclear quantum properties over the full temperature range studied. At the TiO2/water interface, distillation makes PIMD umbrella sampling practical and shows that nuclear quantum effects lower the dissociation barrier by roughly 2 kcal/mol and shift the molecular-dissociated free energy difference into quantitative agreement with recent solid-state 17O NMR measurements. Our work demonstrates how knowledge distillation can make accurate MLIPs practical for the sampling methods needed to connect condensed-phase reaction thermodynamics with experiment, notably for interfacial chemistry and catalysis.

</details>

### [47] [Capturing non-Markovian dynamics in non-equilibrium stochastic systems using flow matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06658)
*Bhargav Sriram Siddani,John B. Bell,Alejandro L. Garcia,Ishan Srivastava*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对粗粒化随机偏微分方程（如正则化Dean-Kawasaki方程）无法准确捕捉非马尔可夫效应主导的短时动力学与高度非高斯分布的低密度区域的问题，本文发展了一种生成式流匹配方法，直接对粒子模拟中的通量概率分布建模，显式整合非马尔可夫与非高斯效应。在非相互作用布朗粒子系统的Kramers首达时间问题上的实验表明，该方法能准确捕捉短时行为，并在数密度统计矩预测上优于马尔可夫基线（正则化DK方程）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粗粒化随机偏微分方程（如正则化Dean-Kawasaki方程）在随机粒子系统水动力学模型中无法准确描述两方面的系统动力学：一是受非马尔可夫效应（non-Markovian effects）主导的短时行为，二是粒子密度低、分布高度非高斯（non-Gaussian）的区间。

Method: 提出一种生成式流匹配（generative flow matching）方法，直接对粒子模拟中的通量（fluxes）概率分布进行建模，在模型中显式地纳入非马尔可夫效应与非高斯效应。

Result: 在非相互作用布朗粒子系统的Kramers首达时间问题（Kramers first passage time problem）上，该方法准确捕捉了短时行为；与作为马尔可夫基线的正则化Dean-Kawasaki方程的解相比，该方法在数密度（number density）的统计矩（statistical moments）预测上表现更好。

Conclusion: 所提出的生成式流匹配方法能够有效地将非马尔可夫和非高斯效应纳入系统建模，在短时动力学和低密度区域的预测精度上优于传统的马尔可夫粗粒化方法。

Abstract: Hydrodynamic models of stochastic particle systems represented by coarse-grained stochastic partial differential equations (SPDE), such as the regularized Dean-Kawasaki (DK) equation, do not accurately capture the short-time system dynamics that is dominated by non-Markovian effects, and low particle density regimes where the distributions are highly non-Gaussian. We develop a generative flow matching method that directly models the probability distribution of fluxes from particle simulations that explicitly incorporates non-Markovian and non-Gaussian effects. As a demonstration, we use this method to simulate the Kramers first passage time problem for a system of non-interacting Brownian particles. We show the model accurately captures the short-time behavior and provides better predictions of the statistical moments of the number density when compared against the solution of the Markovian baseline, regularized DK equation.

</details>

### [48] [Self-organized Floquet band geometry in cavity-driven quantum materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06579)
*Christopher Yang,Gil Refael,Mark S. Rudner,Iliya Esin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出并分析了一种无需外部激光的自组织Floquet工程范式，通过空腔中自生相干场对电子能带进行Floquet修饰，在电驱动的空腔材料系统中产生几何霍尔响应，并自洽求解了非平衡稳态下的周期极限环行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Floquet工程依赖外部激光场，存在功耗大、难以集成、与电子系统耦合弱等局限。本文旨在探索一种利用自生空腔场替代外部激光的替代范式，以实现器件兼容的电子能带动态调控和拓扑响应。

Method: 考虑嵌入空腔的半导体层，耦合外部引线和声学声子（acoustic phonons）浴。通过直流泵浦（dc pumping），利用光-物质耦合（light-matter coupling）在腔内建立相干场。采用自洽方法确定非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady state），并分析系统在阈值以上的时间周期极限环（time-periodic limit cycle）行为。

Result: 研究表明，在阈值以上，耦合系统稳定于一个由空腔品质因子（quality factor）和耗散共同决定振幅的周期极限环。该自生周期场对电子能带进行Floquet修饰，从而改变具有时间反演对称性破缺（broken time-reversal symmetry）材料的反常霍尔响应（anomalous Hall response）。所得到的霍尔电导率（Hall conductivity）可直接通过面内直流输运测量进行探测。

Conclusion: 本工作建立了一条无需外部激光照明的自组织Floquet能带重构与几何输运（geometric transport）路线，揭示了空腔驱动稳态（cavity driven steady states）可作为电控非平衡相（electrically controlled nonequilibrium phases）的平台。

Abstract: Floquet engineering has emerged as a powerful route to dynamically control band structure and topology in quantum materials, but most implementations rely on externally imposed laser fields that are power intensive, difficult to integrate into devices, and weakly coupled to the electronic system. We propose and analyze an alternative paradigm in which a self-generated cavity field Floquet-dresses the electronic bands and produces a geometric Hall response in an electrically driven cavity material system. We consider a semiconductor layer embedded in a cavity and coupled to external leads and a bath of acoustic phonons, where dc pumping leads to the buildup of a coherent intracavity field through light-matter coupling. We determine the resulting nonequilibrium steady state self-consistently and show that, above threshold, the coupled system settles into a stable time-periodic limit cycle with a field amplitude set by the cavity quality factor and dissipation. This emergent periodic field Floquet-dresses the electronic bands and modifies the anomalous Hall response of a material with broken time-reversal symmetry. We demonstrate that the resulting Hall conductivity can be directly probed via in-plane dc transport measurements. Our work establishes a route to self organized Floquet band reconstruction and geometric transport without external laser illumination, highlighting cavity driven steady states as a platform for electrically controlled nonequilibrium phases.

</details>


### [49] [Non-Hermitian Crystalline Braid Topology from Hermitian Projection: A Zero-Mode Resonance Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06626)
*Stefan Đorđević,Vladimir Juričić*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，非厄米（non-Hermitian）晶体辫拓扑（crystalline braid topology）可以仅通过投影（projection）从完全厄米且拓扑平凡的母晶格中涌现，其核心机制是零模共振投影（zero-mode-resonant projection）。当被消除的互补子系统不含零模时，投影在低频极限下平滑并退化为静态Schur补，产生常规SSH型拓扑；当互补子系统存在零模并与保留子系统耦合时，自能出现极点，零频极限奇异，拓扑由有限频率处投影格林函数承载。作者在可精确求解的近邻正方形晶格嵌入一维锯齿膜的模型中验证了该机制，并指出该模型无非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect），拓扑不变量为纯Bloch体量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索能否不从传统的增益、损耗、非对称耦合或显式环境通道出发，而是仅通过从厄米拓扑平凡母体的投影操作来产生非厄米拓扑相。

Method: 提出“零模共振投影”机制：将完全厄米的拓扑平凡母晶格划分为保留子系统和消除互补子系统，分析互补子系统是否含零模两种情形下的投影效应；在可精确求解的正方晶格嵌入一维锯齿膜模型中进行解析演示，结合电路实现验证有限频率处的辫拓扑转变。

Result: 当互补子系统无零模时，投影平滑退化为静态Schur补，产生SSH型拓扑；当互补子系统含零模时，自能出现极点，零频奇异，拓扑由有限频率处投影格林函数承载。在正方晶格-锯齿膜模型中，奇宇称周期扇区存在子晶格不平衡零模，诱导奇异自能，复数谱形成阿贝尔二能带辫，转变仅发生在孤立有限频率处。该模型无趋肤效应，拓扑不变量为纯Bloch体量。

Conclusion: 非厄米辫拓扑可以仅通过投影操作从厄米平凡母体涌现，无需显式非厄米元件；该机制在电路实现中表现为预测驱动频率下的传输零点和导纳特征。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian topological phases are usually engineered through gain, loss, asymmetric couplings, or explicit environmental channels. Here we show that non-Hermitian crystalline braid topology can instead emerge from projection alone, starting from a fully Hermitian and topologically trivial parent lattice. The mechanism is zero-mode-resonant projection. When the eliminated complement is zero-mode free, projection has a smooth low-frequency limit and reduces to a static Schur complement, yielding conventional SSH-type descendants. When a complement zero mode couples to the retained subsystem, the embedding self-energy develops a pole, the zero-frequency limit becomes singular, and topology is carried by the finite-frequency projected Green's function-where frequency is a tunable parameter, the drive frequency in a circuit realization, for instance. We demonstrate this mechanism in an exactly solvable model, a trivial nearest-neighbor square lattice with an embedded one-dimensional zig-zag brane. Odd-parity periodic sectors are resonant: a sublattice-imbalance zero mode generates the singular self-energy, and the complex spectrum forms an abelian two-band braid whose transitions occur only at isolated finite frequencies. Although the internal class is $\text{AI}^†$ featuring only trivial phases, embedding parity induces conjugated pseudo-Hermiticity (CPH), quantizes the complex Berry phase, and identifies it with the braid count. The model is free of the non-Hermitian skin effect, making the invariant a genuine Bloch bulk quantity. In topolectrical realizations, the same finite-frequency braid transitions appear as transmission zeros and admittance features at the predicted drive frequencies.

</details>


### [50] [Descriptor Covariance and Correlation Hierarchy in Moiré Exciton Photoluminescence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06780)
*Katsunori Wakabayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文针对过渡金属硫族化合物异质双层（moiré TMD heterobilayers）中的光致发光谱（photoluminescence spectra）空间组织问题，提出了一种基于描述符（descriptor）的无序过滤（disorder-filter）理论模型。该模型通过分析MoSe₂/WSe₂超光谱成像（hyperspectral mapping）中九个无峰分解谱描述符的微米尺度关联，揭示了多尺度无序地貌（multi-scale disorder landscape）中不同描述符探测不同组分所导致的空间关联长度层级（hierarchy of spatial correlation lengths）。核心结论是关联层级ξ(E_cent) ≥ ξ(E_dom)，该结论源自将主导峰能量分解为平滑背景贡献与短程陷阱切换涨落项。该框架同时解释了描述符间的主要Spearman相关性，包括近乎完美的反相关ρ_S(ΔE_cd, R_HL) ≈ -0.978，并将其归因为具有主导单峰包络谱的稳健谱形关系。该工作提供了一条无需峰分解、不依赖微观谱线指认，即可从超光谱数据中通过描述符协方差结构推断有效无序参数的路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoSe₂/WSe₂异质双层的超光谱成像显示，九个无峰分解谱描述符之间存在微米尺度的空间关联，但缺乏统一的物理框架来解释这些关联的起源与结构。

Method: 提出描述符基的无序过滤理论（descriptor-based disorder-filter picture），将主导峰能量分解为平滑背景贡献与短程陷阱切换涨落项，从而导出关联层级ξ(E_cent) ≥ ξ(E_dom)；通过描述符协方差结构（descriptor covariance structure）分析解释描述符间的Spearman相关性。

Result: 导出核心关联层级ξ(E_cent) ≥ ξ(E_dom)；解释包括ρ_S(ΔE_cd, R_HL) ≈ -0.978在内的描述符间主要Spearman相关性，并将其识别为具有主导单峰包络谱的稳健谱形关系。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种无需峰分解（peak-decomposition-free）且不依赖微观谱线指认的途径，能够通过超光谱数据的描述符协方差结构推断有效无序参数。

Abstract: We develop a minimal theory for the spatial organization of photoluminescence spectra in moiré transition-metal dichalcogenide heterobilayers. Motivated by hyperspectral mapping of MoSe$_2$/WSe$_2$, which reveals micron-scale correlations among nine peak-decomposition-free spectral descriptors, we propose a descriptor-based disorder-filter picture in which different descriptors probe different components of a multi-scale disorder landscape, producing a hierarchy of spatial correlation lengths. The central result is the correlation hierarchy $ξ(E_{\rm cent}) \ge ξ(E_{\rm dom})$, derived from the decomposition of the dominant-peak energy into a smooth background contribution and a short-range trap-switching fluctuation term. The same framework explains the principal inter-descriptor Spearman correlations, including the near-perfect anti-correlation $ρ_{\rm S}(ΔE_{\rm cd}, R_{\rm HL}) \approx -0.978$ as a robust spectral-shape relation for spectra with a dominant unimodal envelope. The framework provides a peak-decomposition-free route to infer effective disorder parameters from hyperspectral data through the descriptor covariance structure, without microscopic line assignment.

</details>


### [51] [Layer-Polarization-Driven Metal-Insulator Transition in multi-band Graphene Moire' Superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06939)
*Harsimran Kaur Mann,Simrandeep Kaur,Harsimran Singh,Yashashwani Garg,Amogh Waghmare,Mohit Kumar Jat,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Manish Jain,Aveek Bid*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了ABA堆叠三层石墨烯（TLG）与hBN形成的莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice），发现通过垂直位移场（displacement field）调控层极化（layer polarization）可驱动电子能带结构重建，实现从多能带（multi-band）到单能带（single-band）的转变以及伴随的金属-绝缘体相变（metal-insulator transition），其机制在于层选择耦合（layer-selective coupling）到莫尔势（moiré potential）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多层石墨烯/六方氮化硼（graphene/hBN）莫尔超晶格中多能带体系的量子相调控机制，特别是利用莫尔势（moiré potential）作为工具来混合无质量与有质量电子能段，并通过垂直位移场（displacement field）实现能带结构（band structure）的有效重建。

Method: 在ABA堆叠三层石墨烯（TLG）与hBN形成的莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）中，施加垂直位移场（displacement field）以调控层极化（layer polarization）；通过量子电容（quantum capacitance）测量探测态密度（density of states）变化，并结合理论计算进行机制验证。

Result: 增加位移场驱动系统从多能带（multi-band）向低能单能带（single-band）演化，并在空穴掺杂的次级狄拉克点（hole-doped secondary Dirac point）处发生金属-绝缘体相变（metal-insulator transition）。量子电容测量直接证实了该狄拉克点处态密度的抑制，与能隙（band gap）开启一致。

Conclusion: 层极化与层选择耦合（layer-selective coupling）在多能带莫尔异质结构（multi-band moiré heterostructures）中为实现能带结构重建（band structure reconstruction）和电子相互作用调控提供了有效途径，可用于工程化拓扑相（topological phases）和关联相（correlated phases）。

Abstract: Graphene/hBN moiré superlattices provide a highly tunable platform for exploring emergent quantum phases in low-dimensional systems. Here, we investigate the moiré superlattice formed between hBN and ABA-stacked trilayer graphene (TLG), an inherently multi-band system. We demonstrate that the moiré potential is not merely a perturbation but a tool to hybridize the distinct massless and massive electronic sectors of TLG. By applying a perpendicular displacement field to tune layer polarization, we drive a fundamental reconstruction of the electronic band structure. Specifically, increasing the displacement field evolves the system from a multi-band regime to an effectively single-band regime at low energies, accompanied by a metal--insulator transition at the hole-doped secondary Dirac point. This transition originates from a redistribution of carriers across graphene layers that selectively enhances their coupling to the extrinsic moiré potential. Quantum capacitance measurements provide direct evidence for the suppression of the density of states at the hole-side secondary Dirac point, consistent with gap opening and the emergence of a displacement-field-tuned band gap. Theoretical calculations reproduce these observations and identify layer-selective coupling to the moiré potential as the underlying mechanism. These results demonstrate electrical control of an emergent insulating phase in a low-dimensional moiré system, and highlight that layer polarization and layer-selective coupling in multi-band moiré heterostructures provide a powerful route for engineering topological and correlated phases through band structure reconstruction and electron interactions.

</details>


### [52] [Spin SWAP operation in double quantum dots at the LaAlO3/SrTiO3 interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06948)
*A. Sierant,J. Czarnecki,B. Szafran,P. Wójcik*

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了LaAlO₃/SrTiO₃界面双量子点中SWAP操作的电子自旋控制，重点关注自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和轨道间耦合（interorbital coupling）对自旋动力学的影响，发现大量子点（dxy轨道主导）与小量子点（dxz/yz轨道贡献）之间存在SWAP保真度的显著差异。

Method: 首先研究单电子自旋动力学，分析自旋-轨道耦合和轨道间耦合的影响；使用基于布洛赫方程（Bloch equations）的半经典计算与全量子力学模拟进行对比验证；随后通过对大量子点与小量子点两个区间的交叉分析，模拟SWAP操作。

Result: 半经典计算与全量子力学模拟结果吻合良好；在大量子点（dxy轨道主导）中，自旋动力学主要受Rashba型自旋-轨道相互作用影响；在小量子点中，高能dxz/yz轨道参与电子结构，导致SWAP保真度显著降低；在大量子点区域观察到自旋-轨道耦合引起的SWAP操作各向异性（anisotropy）。

Conclusion: LaAlO₃/SrTiO₃界面双量子点中的SWAP操作保真度强烈依赖于量子点尺寸和轨道结构，大量子点区域在应用层面更具潜力，但需考虑自旋-轨道耦合所引入的各向异性效应。

Abstract: Progress in the fabrication of nanoscale transition-metal-oxide heterostructures makes these platforms promising candidates for the realization of spin qubits, mainly due to the $d$-character of their electronic structures, which could potentially result in a reduction of hyperfine interactions and spin decoherence. Here, we present a systematic study of spin control within the SWAP operation in double quantum dots embedded in a two-dimensional electron gas at the LaAlO$_3$/SrTiO$_3$ interface. Our analysis starts with a study of single-electron spin dynamics, focusing on the influence of spin-orbit and interorbital coupling on the spin evolution. In this case, our findings are supported by semiclassical calculations based on the Bloch equations, which show good agreement with full quantum mechanical simulations. We then simulate the SWAP operation by analyzing the crossover between two regimes: (i) large quantum dots, where the electronic structure is dominated by the $d_{xy}$ orbitals and the spin dynamics is affected primarily by Rashba-type spin-orbit interaction; and (ii) small quantum dots, where higher-energy orbitals $d_{xz/yz}$ contribute to the electronic structure, leading to a significant reduction in the SWAP fidelity. In the first regime, particularly relevant from the application point of view, we analyze in detail the anisotropy of the SWAP operation induced by the spin-orbit coupling.

### [53] [Light-tunable quantum metric non-linear Hall response in Berry dipole semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06999)

Method: 基于贝利偶极子半金属（Berry dipole semimetals）模型，理论分析光对量子度量（quantum metric）非对角部分的影响，并考察光振幅对非线性霍尔电导（nonlinear Hall conductivity）的调控作用。

Result: 光诱导了量子度量非对角部分的不可调对称性，表现为量子度量偶极子（quantum metric dipole）的不对称性；非线性响应可通过光振幅直接调控，当光振幅超过某一阈值时，非线性霍尔信号的方向发生反转。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of light on quantum metric-mediated intrinsic nonlinear Hall conductivity in Berry dipole semimetals. We discover that light induces a tunable asymmetry in the off-diagonal part of the quantum metric, which is manifested by an asymmetry in the quantum metric dipole. We show that the nonlinear response can be tuned directly by the light amplitude. In particular, we note that the direction of the nonlinear Hall signal changes when the light amplitude is increased beyond a threshold value. Light thus emerges as a promising stimulus to control the quantum geometric response in topological semimetals.

### [54] [Polar and quadratic magneto-optical Kerr effects in nonmagnetic/ferromagnet bilayers for spin-orbit torque measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07395)
*Yukihiro Marui,Masashi Kawaguchi,Kohji Nakamura,Masamitsu Hayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过实验对比发现，在非磁金属/铁磁金属双层体系中，自旋霍尔磁电阻（SMR）对磁光克尔效应（MOKE）信号的贡献远小于其对霍尔电阻的贡献，因此MOKE测量可准确提取自旋力矩效率（spin-torque efficiency），避免了因SMR导致的谐波霍尔电压测量偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋霍尔磁电阻（SMR）在非磁金属（NM）/铁磁金属（FM）双层膜中同时对反常霍尔电阻（anomalous Hall resistance）和平面霍尔电阻（planar Hall resistance）产生贡献，尤其是在NM层具有大自旋霍尔角（spin Hall angle）的体系（如W/CoFeB）中，平面与反常霍尔电阻之比可趋近于1，这严重干扰了利用谐波霍尔电压（harmonic Hall voltage）测量提取自旋力矩效率（spin-torque efficiency）的准确性。因此，需要确认磁光克尔效应（MOKE）测量能否作为替代方案来可靠地表征自旋力矩效率。

Method: 本文分别测量了NM/FM双层膜中的极向（polar）和二次（quadratic）MOKE信号——这两个分量在低频极限下分别对应反常霍尔电阻和平面霍尔电阻——并与霍尔电阻测量结果进行对比，以评估SMR对MOKE响应的贡献程度。

Result: 在NM/FM双层膜中，二次MOKE信号与极向MOKE信号的比值远小于对应的平面霍尔电阻与反常霍尔电阻的比值，表明在可见光范围内SMR对MOKE响应的贡献可忽略不计。因此，从MOKE测量中提取的自旋力矩效率与基于NM层自旋霍尔角预期的结果吻合良好。

Conclusion: 这些结果阐明了MOKE测量能够可靠地确定自旋力矩效率的原因：SMR对MOKE信号贡献极小，从而避免了谐波霍尔电压测量方法中的干扰。

Abstract: Recent studies have revealed that spin Hall magnetoresistance (SMR) contributes to both the anomalous and planar Hall resistances in nonmagnetic metal (NM)/ferromagnetic metal (FM) bilayers. This effect becomes pronounced when the NM layer exhibits a large spin Hall angle, as in W/CoFeB bilayers. In such systems, the ratio of planar to anomalous Hall resistances, normally small in single CoFeB layers, can approach unity. This unusually large ratio complicates the determination of spin-torque efficiency using harmonic Hall voltage measurements. To overcome this limitation, magneto-optical Kerr effect (MOKE) measurements have been proposed as an alternative approach. Here, we investigate the polar and quadratic MOKE components, which correspond to, respectively, the anomalous and planar Hall resistances in the low-frequency limit to clarify whether the MOKE measurements are suitable for characterizing the spin-torque efficiency. We find that the ratio of quadratic to polar MOKE signals in NM/FM bilayers is significantly smaller than the corresponding Hall resistance ratio, indicating that SMR contributes negligibly to the MOKE response in the visible range. Consequently, the spin-torque efficiency extracted from MOKE measurements agree well with those expected from the spin Hall angle of the NM layer. These results clarify the reason why MOKE measurements provide reliable determination of the spin-torque efficiency.

### [55] [Charge density waves and enhanced superconductivity in the electron-hole gas: a plausible, simple, physically intuitive model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06649)
*Carl A Kukkonen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过一个简单的两参数模型（密度 r_s 和质量比 M/m）研究了电子-空穴气（electron-hole gas）——一种由等量电子和带正电费米子（空穴）组成的中性简并等离子体。基于两个未经证明的简化假设，计算了所有质量比和密度下的相图、不稳定性和有效相互作用。关键新物理在于移动空穴提供的额外屏蔽效应，当函数 Delta 在 q=0 或有限 q 处为零时，电荷密度波、大 T^2 电阻率和吸引性电子-电子相互作用同时增强；粗略估计超导转变温度可达约 275 K（M/m=9）。作者未声明该模型适用于任何具体材料，旨在引发对假设的审视和相关计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索电子-空穴气这一双载流子（two-carrier）体系的基本物理性质，特别是移动空穴提供的额外屏蔽效应对相图、不稳定性及有效相互作用的影响。模型旨在以极简方式捕捉关键物理，并激发对相关假设和未知局域场因子（local field factors）的理论研究。

Method: 采用一个物理动机明确的两参数模型，参数为密度 r_s 和质量比 M/m。做出两个简化假设：（1）电子-空穴关联能（correlation energy）近似与密度无关，不影响压强和体模量；（2）电子-空穴对局域场因子的贡献为零，因此可直接使用已知的电子气局域场因子。基于此，推导出所有有效相互作用和响应函数分母中的单一函数 Delta，通过分析其零点来研究不稳定性。

Result: 当 Delta 在 q=0（压缩率不稳定性，compressibility instability）和有限 q 处为零时，三种现象同时增强：电荷密度波（charge density waves，当 M/m ≥ 4.97 时出现）、由电子-空穴散射产生的大 T^2 电阻率，以及纯电子版本类 BCS 电子-声子耦合的吸引性电子-电子相互作用。粗略估计超导转变温度可达约 275 K（M/m=9）。

Conclusion: 作者未声称该模型适用于任何具体材料，其目的在于促发对模型假设的严格审视、对未知局域场因子的计算，以及探究这一极简双载流子框架是否能够映射到真实物理系统。

Abstract: A neutral degenerate plasma of equal numbers of electrons and positively charged fermions (holes) -- the electron-hole gas -- is studied using a simple, physically motivated two-parameter model (density r_s and mass ratio M/m). Two simplifying assumptions are made but not proven: the electron-hole correlation energy is approximately independent of density and does not affect the pressure or bulk modulus, and the electron-hole contribution to the local field factors is zero, allowing use of the known electron-gas local field factors. With these assumptions the phase diagram, instabilities, and effective interactions can be calculated for all mass ratios and densities using simple formulae, reproducible on a laptop. The key new physics is the additional screening provided by the mobile holes. A single function Delta appears in the denominator of all effective interactions and response functions. Near the zeros of Delta at q = 0 (compressibility instability) and at finite q, three phenomena are simultaneously enhanced: charge density waves (for M/m >= 4.97), a large T^2 electrical resistivity from electron-hole scattering, and an attractive electron-electron interaction that is the purely electronic analog of BCS electron-phonon coupling. Crudely estimated superconducting transition temperatures approach room temperature, reaching approximately 275 K at M/m = 9. No claim is made that this model applies to any specific material. The aim is to provoke scrutiny of the assumptions, calculation of the unknown local field factors, and investigation of whether this minimal two-carrier framework maps onto real systems.

### [56] [Magnetic Field Walls in Flat-band Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06791)
*Guodong Jiang,Aaron Dunbrack,Tero Heikkilä,Päivi Törmä*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文预测在平带（flat bands）超导体中，施加外磁场时会出现一种具有磁通壁（walls of magnetic flux）的超导相；该相源于平带中任意动量凝聚体无单粒子能量惩罚，导致超导自由能在低温下成为矢势的负周期函数；通过最小晶格周期自由能模型，研究了壁相的扭结（kink）和呼吸子（breather）两种孤子模，并讨论了壁与涡旋（vortices）的竞争，结果表明平带有助于在大磁场中维持超导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不同种类超导体具有截然不同的磁性行为（如阿布里科索夫涡旋（Abrikosov vortices）或交替的正常-超导畴），但平带系统中在磁场下是否会出现新型超导相尚不清楚；本文旨在探索平带中超导体在外磁场下的稳定相行为及其物理机制。

Method: 采用最小晶格周期自由能模型对壁相进行描述，通过自由能的负周期函数推导壁相的存在条件；利用孤子理论分析壁相的两种孤子模——扭结（kink）和呼吸子（breather），并比较壁相与涡旋相的竞争。

Result: 预测了一种由磁通壁构成的超导相，该相在平带中稳定存在；扭结孤子决定下临界场（lower critical field），呼吸子孤子决定高场行为；平带中壁与涡旋之间存在竞争。

Conclusion: 平带有助于在大磁场下维持超导性，为高场超导材料的设计提供了新的理论方向。

Abstract: Superconductors of different types have distinct magnetic properties; for example, they can form Abrikosov vortices or alternating normal-superconducting domains. We predict that, in flat bands, a superconducting phase exhibiting walls of magnetic flux is stable in an applied magnetic field. This phase relies on the lack of a single particle energy penalty for forming condensates of any momentum in flat bands and, consequently, their superconducting free energy being a negative and periodic function of the vector potential at low temperatures. Using a minimal lattice-periodic model of free energy, we study two types of soliton modes of the wall phase: the kink and breather solitons. They determine the lower critical field and the high-field behavior of the wall phase, respectively. The competition between the walls and vortices in flat bands is also discussed. Our results suggest that flat bands help sustain superconductivity in the presence of large magnetic fields.

### [57] [Multiband superconductivity in the kagome-lattice superconductor Re2Zr](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07184)
*Gabriel Kuderowicz,Bartlomiej Wiendlocha*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，系统研究了六角笼目晶格（kagome-lattice）化合物 Re₂Zr 的电子结构、晶格动力学、电子-声子耦合及超导性质。结果表明，该材料的超导能标可以在常规的声子介导框架下被定量重现，超导态表现出显著的多带和各向异性能隙结构，但实验提出的时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal symmetry breaking）的起源仍是一个开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对六角笼目晶格化合物 Re₂Zr 近期被提出存在时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal symmetry breaking）和非常规配对（unconventional pairing）的实验背景，检验其超导性是否能在常规的声子介导（phonon-mediated）框架下得到解释。

Method: 采用基于超导密度泛函理论（density functional theory for superconductors, SCDFT）的全第一性原理（fully ab initio）计算，对 Re₂Zr 的电子结构、晶格动力学、电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）以及超导性质进行从头算研究。

Result: 电子结构由七种二维和三维费米面（Fermi surface sheets）构成，导致多带超导（multiband superconductivity）和多个重叠超导能隙；自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）在费米能级（E_F）附近诱导出范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularity）；电子-声子耦合强度中等（λ≈0.88）；超导能隙计算显示显著的各向异性和宽分布；自旋涨落（spin fluctuations）引入额外退配对效应（depairing effects），将临界温度从 7.7 K 压低至 6.4 K，与实验值 6.65 K 高度吻合。

Conclusion: Re₂Zr 的超导能标可在常规声子介导框架下被定量重现，超导态具有明显的多带和各向异性能隙结构；但实验所提示的时间反演对称性破缺的起源仍是一个未解决的问题。

Abstract: We present a first-principles investigation of the electronic structure, lattice dynamics, electron-phonon coupling, and superconducting properties of the hexagonal kagome-lattice compound Re$_2$Zr, in which time-reversal symmetry breaking and unconventional pairing have recently been proposed. We examine whether superconductivity in Re$_2$Zr can be explained within a conventional phonon-mediated framework by performing fully ab initio calculations within the density functional theory for superconductors. The electronic structure is characterized by a mixture of seven two- and three-dimensional Fermi surface sheets, giving rise to multiband superconductivity with many overlapping superconducting gaps. A spin-orbit-induced van Hove singularity is identified in the density of states near $E_F$. The electron-phonon interaction is moderately strong, with a coupling constant $λ\simeq 0.88$. Superconducting gap calculations reveal significant anisotropy and a broad distribution of gap values across different Fermi surface sheets. Spin fluctuations introduce additional depairing effects and reduce the critical temperature from 7.7 K to 6.4 K, in excellent agreement with the experimental value of 6.65 K. Taken together, our results show that the superconducting energy scale in Re$_2$Zr can be quantitatively reproduced within a conventional phonon-mediated framework, while the resulting state exhibits pronounced multiband and anisotropic gap structure. The origin of the experimentally suggested time-reversal symmetry breaking, however, remains an open question.

TL;DR: 该论文研究发现，在非常规超导体4Hb-TaS₂中，通过Se/S替代引入的淬灭无序（quenched disorder）可以驱动Mott绝缘层中的载流子退局域化，从而形成新的费米面（Fermi surface）并诱导出体超导电性，而干净样品中则不存在超导。这表明Mott态的脆弱性是超导的关键驱动因素之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The unconventional superconductor 4Hb-TaS$_2$ is a natural heterostructure that can be broadly understood as interleaving Mott-like and metallic layers. We study the properties of this material as a function of quenched disorder in the form of Se/S substitution and find that while disordered samples show bulk superconductivity, clean samples do not. We show that a disorder-driven delocalization of carriers in the Mott-like ($1T$-) layer forms a new Fermi surface that is absent in the cleanest samples. This suggests that one of the primary drivers for superconductivity is the fragility of the Mott state, whose delocalization brings to life a sea of strongly correlated electrons.

### [59] [A variational formulation of the adjoint Kutta condition in potential flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06937)
*Carlos Lozano,Jorge Ponsin*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该论文提出了二维亚临界势流中连续伴随库塔条件（continuous adjoint Kutta condition）的变分公式化（variational formulation），重点讨论了库塔条件（Kutta condition）与尾流（wake）的作用。研究表明，伴随库塔条件可通过在尾缘（trailing edge）处施加惩罚项（penalty term）来实现，对应的拉格朗日乘子（Lagrange multiplier）由拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）对环量（circulation）的驻定性（stationarity）决定，且无需处理尾流。论文还简要讨论了这些结果对伴随一致性（adjoint consistency）的部分启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有连续伴随方法在处理库塔条件与尾流时存在理论不清晰或数值实现复杂的问题，亟需建立严格的变分框架来厘清伴随库塔条件的施加方式及其与尾流的关系。

Method: 采用变分公式化（variational formulation）方法，将伴随库塔条件转化为尾缘处的惩罚项，并通过拉格朗日量对环量的驻定性确定相应的拉格朗日乘子。

Result: 伴随库塔条件可以通过在尾缘处添加惩罚项来施加，对应的拉格朗日乘子由拉格朗日量对环量的驻定性唯一确定，且无需显式建模尾流。

Conclusion: 尾流处理对于伴随库塔条件的施加并非必需，这一发现对改善伴随一致性（adjoint consistency）具有潜在的理论意义，并为相关数值方法的设计提供了更简洁的框架。

Abstract: We give a variational formulation of the continuous adjoint Kutta condition for two-dimensional subcritical potential flow, with emphasis on the Kutta condition and the role of the wake. We show that the adjoint Kutta condition can be imposed by a penalty term evaluated at the trailing edge, with the corresponding Lagrange multiplier determined by stationarity of the Lagrangian with respect to circulation, and that a wake treatment is not required. Some of the implications of these results for adjoint consistency are also briefly discussed.

</details>


### [60] [Functional Renormalization for Elastic Burgulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06496)
*Johannes Conrad,Martin Oberlack*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文利用 Martin-Siggia-Rose 路径积分形式（path-integral formalism）对弹性湍流（elastic turbulence）和弹惯性湍流（elasto-inertial turbulence）进行建模，并发展了一种系统化的源扩展对称算法（source-extended symmetry algorithm），直接从欧拉-拉格朗日方程（Euler-Lagrange equations）推导 Ward 恒等式（Ward identities）。这些恒等式提供了非微扰约束（nonperturbative constraints）和构建封闭方案（closure schemes）的原则性基础。作为弹性湍流的降维简化模型，本文提出了一个扩展的 Burgers 方程（extended Burgers equation），该方程保留了额外应力与速度梯度之间的特征耦合，同时保持足够简单以进行首次受控计算。特别地，获得了一组扩展的 Ward 恒等式，其强烈约束了可容许的封闭形式，并揭示了固定点附近的标度行为（scaling behaviour）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弹性湍流和弹惯性湍流是复杂流体动力学中的重要现象，但缺乏系统化的非微扰理论工具来约束和指导封闭方案（closure schemes）的构建。现有方法难以直接从运动方程出发获得严格的恒等约束关系。

Method: 采用 Martin-Siggia-Rose 路径积分形式（path-integral formalism）对弹性湍流和弹惯性湍流进行形式化表述，并发展了一种系统化的源扩展对称算法（source-extended symmetry algorithm），直接从欧拉-拉格朗日方程（Euler-Lagrange equations）推导 Ward 恒等式。此外，提出一个扩展的 Burgers 方程（extended Burgers equation）作为弹性湍流的降维简化模型。

Result: 获得了扩展的 Ward 恒等式（Ward identities），这些恒等式为非微扰约束（nonperturbative constraints）提供了严格的数学基础，并强烈限制了可容许的封闭形式（closures）。扩展的 Burgers 方程能够保留额外应力与速度梯度之间的特征耦合特性。

Conclusion: 所提出的路径积分框架和 Ward 恒等式为弹性湍流和弹惯性湍流的封闭方案构建提供了原则性基础，并有助于理解固定点（fixed point）附近的标度行为（scaling behaviour）。

Abstract: We formulate elastic and elasto-inertial turbulence in the Martin-Siggia-Rose path-integral formalism and develop a systematic source-extended symmetry algorithm to derive Ward identities directly from the Euler-Lagrange equations. These identities provide nonperturbative constraints and a principled foundation for constructing closure schemes. As a dimensionally reduced model for elastic turbulence, we propose an extended Burgers equation that preserves the characteristic coupling between the extra stress and velocity gradient, while remaining simple enough for first controlled calculations. In particular, we obtain an extended set of Ward identities that strongly constrains admissible closures and provides insight into the scaling behaviour near the fixed point.

</details>


### [61] [Fluctuation-induced and quantum effects in nanofluidic transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06693)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点将流体动力学壁面视为无特征的边界对象，但纳米尺度实验表明液体流动对壁面内部电子自由度敏感。本文旨在系统梳理相关实验证据并呈现定量理解的理论进展。

Method: 通过综述实验证据，采用液体-固体界面的量子描述来揭示电子动力学对经典流体输运的影响；引入涨落诱导的量子摩擦概念，并将液-电耦合现象整合为水电输运矩阵（hydro-electronic transport matrix），给出输运系数的解析公式。

Result: 建立了水电输运系数的解析公式，可实现实际场景下的定量估算；指出耦合液-电输运对水-能源关系（water-energy nexus）的潜在影响。

Conclusion: 液体-固体界面中的涨落诱导与量子效应代表了流体动力学与凝聚态物理学之间的新兴交叉领域，对理论与实验而言均是一片大部分未被探索的疆域。

Abstract: The hydrodynamic wall has traditionally been considered a featureless object, whose only role is to provide a boundary for fluid flow. Yet, there is now ample evidence that at nanometer scales, liquid flows are sensitive to the wall's internal -- in particular, electronic -- degrees of freedom. Here, after reviewing the experimental evidence for nanoscale liquid-electron couplings, we present the theoretical advances that have allowed for their quantitative understanding. We discuss how a quantum description of the liquid-solid interface reveals the influence of electron dynamics on classical fluid transport, in the form of the fluctuation-induced quantum friction effect. Quantum friction is at the root of liquid-electron coupled transport phenomena, that may be combined into a hydro-electronic transport matrix. We present analytical formulas for the hydro-electronic transport coefficients, that allow for their quantitative estimation in practical cases; we further outline the potential consequences of coupled liquid-electron transport for the water-energy nexus. Fluctuation-induced and quantum effects at liquid-solid interfaces represent an emerging interface between fluid dynamics and condensed-matter physics, and a largely uncharted territory for both theory and experiment.

### [62] [A homodyne detection scheme for all-optical photon-photon scattering experiments using 2D detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07460)
*Timo Pohle,Leonard Doyle,Paul Ihde,Felix Karbstein,Jörg Schreiber,Matt Zepf*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出一种平衡零拍测量方案（balanced homodyne measurement scheme），通过将信号与短参考脉冲干涉实现时间门控，有效抑制光子-光子散射（photon-photon scattering）实验中的低频背景噪声，将有效背景降低3-4个数量级，并在模拟数据上实现了相比传统光子计数方法超过100倍的测量时间缩短。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在光学波段利用拍瓦级飞秒激光测量光子-光子散射时，大束斑导致背景噪声在到达时间上弥散至100皮秒量级，而信号仅存在于飞秒尺度。传统方法受限于低信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio），亟需一种能利用信号与背景在时间尺度上的差异来有效压制背景的测量方案。

Method: 采用平衡零拍测量方案，将信号与一段短参考脉冲进行干涉，使测量有效门控（gated）至脉冲持续时间，仅对时间重合的光成分敏感；通过增大参考脉冲能量可提升被测幅值而不改变本征信噪比，从而压制外部噪声源；同时采用二维探测器（two-dimensional detectors）提升灵敏度并实现自参考单脉冲测量；最后引入基于最大似然估计（maximum-likelihood estimation）的评估流程。

Result: 该方案将有效背景降低约3-4个数量级；在模拟数据上，相比传统光子计数方法（photon-counting methods），在现实条件下实现了超过100倍的测量时间缩减。

Conclusion: 所提出的平衡零拍测量方案能够显著抑制光子-光子散射实验中的背景噪声，大幅提升测量效率，结合二维探测器和最大似然估计方法具有良好的鲁棒性和实用性能，有望推动光学波段光子-光子散射实验的可行性。

Abstract: Low signal-to-noise ratios are a common problem in experiments attempting to measure photon-photon scattering. In the optical regime, where petawatt lasers with femtosecond pulse durations are used, the large beam sizes cause the major contribution of the background to be spread over up to 100 ps in arrival time, whereas the signal is confined to the femtosecond scale. We present a balanced homodyne measurement scheme, which exploits this property to suppress the background. By interfering the signal with a short reference pulse, the measurement becomes effectively gated to the pulse duration and is therefore only sensitive to the co-timed part of the light, reducing the effective background by 3-4 orders of magnitude. Additionally, increasing the reference pulse energy increases the amplitude of the measured quantity without changing the intrinsic signal-to-noise ratio. Using this property, other external noise sources can be made negligible by boosting the measured quantity above the noise floor. Using two-dimensional detectors further enhances the scheme by improving sensitivity and enabling self-referenced single-pulse measurements. In addition, an evaluation procedure based on maximum-likelihood estimation is presented and demonstrated. The robustness and performance of this scheme are demonstrated on simulated data, where a more than 100-fold reduction of measurement time compared to conventional photon-counting methods under realistic conditions is found.

### [63] [The massless sine-Gordon model with logarithmic correlations in arbitrary dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06657)
*Sami Vihko*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了任意维度 d ≥ 1 下具有对数相关性的 sine-Gordon 模型，通过连续统中的重整化方法（不使用边界条件）非微扰地构造了该场论，证明了配分函数的可重整性，并给出了电荷与梯度关联函数的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对数相关的高斯场在统计力学（statistical mechanics）与量子场论中具有重要地位，但 sine-Gordon 模型在高维度和无边界条件下的严格构造仍存在空白。本文旨在不依赖边界条件的情况下，证明该模型配分函数的可重整性（renormalizability），并建立非微扰（non-perturbative）的有效性范围。

Method: 采用连续统（continuum）中的直接分析：通过尺度分解（scale decomposition）实施重整化（renormalization），并利用 Brydges 与 Kennedy 提出的迭代 Mayer 展开（iterated Mayer expansion）控制重整化势（renormalized potential），从而构造配分函数。

Result: 证明配分函数是可重整的；结果对所有 z ∈ ℝ 非微扰成立。当 d=1 时，有效范围覆盖全子临界区间 β ∈ (0, 4π)；当 d ≥ 2 时，有效范围为 β ∈ (0, (d+1)2π)。构造了场及其电荷关联函数（charge correlation functions）和梯度关联函数（gradient correlation functions），且无需施加边界条件。

Conclusion: 本文为高维 sine-Gordon 模型提供了无边界条件下的严格非微扰构造框架，并明确了 β 的有效范围对维度 d 的依赖关系。这一工作拓展了经典二维 sine-Gordon 模型的重整化理论到任意维度。

Abstract: In this article, we study the sine-Gordon model with logarithmic correlations in arbitrary dimension $d \ge 1$. The model is defined as a Euclidean field theory whose interaction term in the classical action is \[ S_{\mathrm{int}}(\varphi) := 2z \int_Λ \cos(\sqrtβ\,\varphi)\,\dx, \] where $\varphi$ is a logarithmically correlated Gaussian field on a compact domain $Λ\subset \mathbb{R}^d$ that coincides with the Gaussian free field when $d=2$, and where $z \in \mathbb{R}$ and $β>0$. We treat both the massive and massless cases, with the main emphasis on the massless regime. We construct the field without imposing boundary conditions, together with its charge and gradient correlation functions, and we show that the partition function is renormalizable. The results are non-perturbative, holding for all $z \in \mathbb{R}$. If $d=1$, our results are valid for the full subcritical range $β\in (0,4π)$ and if $d\geq 2$, the results are valid for $β\in (0,(d+1)2π)$. Our analysis is carried out directly in the continuum: we perform renormalization via a scale decomposition and control the partition function by controlling the renormalized potential that arises in this procedure, using the iterated Mayer expansion of Brydges and Kennedy~\cite{BrKe87a}.

</details>


### [64] [Unified Framework for Functional Theories of Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06676)
*Chih-Chun Wang,Julia Liebert,Markus Penz,Christian Schilling*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建并研究了一个统一框架，将密度泛函理论（density-functional theory）及其变体推广到有限维希尔伯特空间（finite-dimensional Hilbert spaces）上的量子系统。该框架通过广义可观测量的期望值定义约化变量（reduced variables），并引入“scope”概念作为建立泛函理论所必需的最小结构，使得通用泛函的凸性、可微性、可表示性（representability）以及Hohenberg-Kohn型唯一性定理得以统一证明。特别地，李代数（Lie-algebra）可观测量结构将变分框架与辛几何（symplectic geometry）联系起来，使得结构性结果能够一次性证明并应用于多种有限维泛函理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体量子问题（many-body quantum problem）的复杂性极高，密度泛函理论及其变体通过约化变量描述基态（ground states）来降低这一复杂性。然而，现有理论缺乏一个统一的数学框架来系统性地处理不同泛函理论中的共性结构问题。

Method: 提出“scope”概念作为泛函理论的最小结构，包含广义可观测量（basic observables）的选择和哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）的固定部分。在此结构上定义通用泛函（universal functionals），并利用纯化构造（purification construction）将系综泛函（ensemble functionals）与纯态变体（pure-state variant）联系起来。特别地，引入李代数可观测量结构，将变分框架与辛几何关联。

Result: 建立了通用泛函的凸性（convexity）和可微性（differentiability）性质；解决了可表示性问题；证明了Hohenberg-Kohn型唯一性定理（Hohenberg-Kohn-type uniqueness result）；通过纯化构造统一了系综与纯态泛函；在李代数可观测量结构下建立了与辛几何的联系。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个系统性的数学表述，使得结构性结果能够被一次性证明并广泛适用于多种有限维泛函理论，从而实现了对密度泛函理论及其变体的统一数学处理。

Abstract: We introduce and study a unified framework for density-functional theory and its variants for quantum systems on finite-dimensional Hilbert spaces. These theories seek to reduce the complexity inherent in the many-body quantum problem by describing ground states through reduced variables. The central ingredients of our unified framework are a generalized choice of basic observables, whose expectation values define precisely those reduced variables, and a fixed part of the Hamiltonian characterizing the class of quantum systems under consideration. It is this minimal structure, which we call the scope of a functional theory, that is necessary and sufficient for the formulation of a functional theory. In particular, it allows one to define the universal functionals, establish their convexity and differentiability properties, address representability questions, and prove a Hohenberg-Kohn-type uniqueness result. A purification construction also relates ensemble and weighted-ensemble functionals to the pure-state variant. Particular emphasis is placed on functional theories with Lie-algebra observable structures, connecting the variational framework to symplectic geometry. The result of this work is a systematic mathematical formulation in which structural results can be proved once and applied across a broad class of finite-dimensional functional theories.

</details>


### [65] [Rational Heun operators on $q$-linear grids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06863)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用构造性定义方法：从算子应具有将有理函数 $[n/n]$ 映射到 $[n+1/n+1]$ 的上升作用这一要求出发，定义二阶 q-差分算子 $W_q$，其极点在 q-线性网格上。进一步，通过分析极点结构、有理函数类型和给定基的保持条件，刻画经典子类。

Result: 获得了定义在 q-线性网格上的有理 Heun 算子 $W_q$，发现其与 Ruijsenaars-van Diejen-Takemura Hamiltonians 的一个家族相关；同时，识别出一类称为“经典”的算子子类，该类算子能够改变极点结构，同时保持有理函数类型和指定基。

Conclusion: 有理 Heun 算子 $W_q$ 的提出及其与 Ruijsenaars-van Diejen-Takemura Hamiltonians 的联系，为 q-正交多项式（$q$-orthogonal polynomials）和可积系统理论提供了新的工具；经典子类的刻画进一步丰富了这类算子的结构分类。

Abstract: Rational Heun operators on the $q-$linear grid are presented. They are second-order $q-$difference operators $W_q$ constructively defined from the requirement that they have a raising action on rational functions of type $[n/n]$, namely $W_q: [n/n] \rightarrow [n+1/n+1]$, with poles on $q-$linear grids. It will be observed that these operators are related to one family of the Ruijsenaars-van Diejen-Takemura Hamiltonians. A distinguished subclass of $W_q$ called classical which shifts the pole structure while preserving the rational function type and a prescribed basis is also characterized.

### [66] [A survey on rigorous results for the dynamics of periodic FPU chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07018)
*Dario Bambusi,Andrea Carati,Alberto Maiocchi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了费米-帕斯塔-乌拉姆（FPU）系统动力学的若干解析结果，通过其与户田（Toda）系统的近似关系，分析了从有限粒子体系到热力学极限下的稳定性、连续极限行为及热化时间下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FPU系统是统计力学（statistical mechanics）和混沌理论中的经典模型，其长时间的动力学行为尚未完全理解。本文旨在通过利用FPU哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）与Toda哈密顿量的近似关系，从解析角度揭示FPU系统的稳定性及热化（thermalization）过程。

Method: 首先，针对有限粒子情形，基于Toda系统的作用-角变量（action-angle variables）推导FPU系统的稳定性性质，并研究$N\to\infty$极限。其次，考察Toda链的连续极限（continuous limit），展示其可由一对Korteweg-de Vries（KdV）方程描述。接着，直接研究插值FPU系统的函数的动力学，证明其哈密顿结构与KdV层级（KdV hierarchy）前三个哈密顿量的函数密切相关。最后，在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下分析时间自相关函数（time autocorrelation functions）的衰减行为。

Result: 在有限粒子系统及连续极限下，FPU系统与Toda及KdV方程之间存在紧密联系，其动力学具有哈密顿结构（Hamiltonian structure）。在热力学极限下，构造的某些可观测量的时间自相关函数衰减缓慢，从而给出了系统热化时间的下界（lower bounds）。

Conclusion: FPU系统的动力学可通过与可积系统（Toda及KdV层级）的近似关系获得深刻理解；热化时间下界的建立表明系统在热力学极限下可能存在异常缓慢的热化过程。

Abstract: In this paper we review some analytic results on the dynamics of the FPU system. In the first part of the paper, having in mind that the FPU Hamiltonian and the Toda Hamiltonian are close each other, we present some results on the action angle variables of the Toda system and deduce some stability properties for the dynamics of the FPU system. We first focus on the case of finitely many particles and then we study the limit $N\to\infty$. We present also some results on the continous limit of the Toda chain showing that it is well described by a couple of KdV equations. Then we study directly the dynamics of the function interpolating the FPU system and show that the dynamics is Hamiltonian and that the Hamiltonian is very close to a function of the first three Hamiltonians of the KdV hierarchy. In the second part of the paper we present some results valid in the thermodynamic limit, according to which the time autocorrelation functions of some suitably constructed observables decay slowly implying lower bounds on the thermalization times of the system.

</details>


### [67] [Einstein-Kropina Metrics and Their Application in Finsler Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07121)
*Sjors Heefer,Fidel F. Villaseñor,Andrea Fuster*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文将Kropina度量的Einstein条件从正定情形推广到任意符号，构造了新的正定和首个Lorentzian符号的Einstein-Kropina度量示例，并分类了所有满足Finsler引力真空方程（含宇宙学常数）的Einstein-Kropina解。发现所有解均为Berwald型、Ricci平坦，且宇宙学常数必须为零，呈现出显著的刚性现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Kropina度量的Einstein条件从正定（positive definite）情形推广到任意符号，并探索Finsler引力（Finsler gravity）真空方程下的Einstein-Kropina解的分类问题。

Method: 通过推广Zhang、Shen等人在正定情形下的Einstein条件到一般符号，基于Finsler引力真空方程（含宇宙学常数Λ），在任意维度下对Einstein-Kropina度量的解进行分类分析。

Result: 构造了新的正定Einstein-Kropina度量以及首个Lorentzian符号的示例。在维度4及以下，仅存在平凡解（Minkowski或Euclidean空间）；在维度5及以上，度量a为直线与Ricci平坦度量的乘积，向量场b为第一个因子上的唯一单位向量。所有解均为Berwald型、Ricci平坦，且宇宙学常数Λ必须为零。

Conclusion: Einstein-Kropina度量在Finsler引力Λ-真空方程下表现出极强的刚性：所有非平凡解仅出现在维度5及以上，且必须满足Berwald条件、Ricci平坦以及宇宙学常数为零。

Abstract: We generalize the Einstein condition for Kropina metrics obtained in the positive definite setting by Zhang, Shen and others to all signatures. As examples of Einstein-Kropina metrics $L=L_{a,b}$, we construct new explicit positive definite ones and the first ones with Lorentzian signature. Next, we classify all Einstein-Kropina solutions to the vacuum equation of Finsler gravity by Pfeifer and Wohlfarth, in arbitrary dimension and including a possible cosmological constant $Λ$. For the Lorentzian and positive definite cases, the local picture is as follows. In dimension 4 or lower, only the trivial solution exists: a Minkowski or Euclidean space, essentially. In dimension 5 and higher, the solutions are those $L_{a,b}$ for which the metric $a$ is a product of the real line with a Ricci-flat metric (Lorentzian or Riemannian) and the vector field $b$ is the unique unit vector on the first factor. As a very surprising rigidity phenomenon, all Einstein-Kropina solutions to the $Λ$-vacuum equation are Berwald and Ricci-flat, and the cosmological constant necessarily vanishes.

</details>


### [68] [Information theoretic measures of isotropic Dunkl oscillator in spherical coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07228)
*Akash Halder,Amlan K. Roy,Debraj Nath*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本研究在Dunkl-Schrödinger框架下对各向同性谐振子势进行了信息论分析，导出了多种量子信息度量及其相对度量与散度，并引入了一种新的因子分解方法计算Shannon熵。结果表明，当Dunkl参数消失时，该结果与非Dunkl情形完全一致，且反射算符与Dunkl参数对上述度量有显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在Dunkl-Schrödinger框架下，对各向同性谐振子势（isotropic harmonic oscillator potential）进行信息论分析，推导并考察多种量子信息度量（quantum information measures）及其相对度量与散度在反射算符（reflection operators）和Dunkl参数影响下的行为。

Method: 采用球坐标系下的Dunkl-Schrödinger框架，从精确解析本征解出发，推导Shannon熵、Rényi信息、Tsallis熵等量子信息度量及其相对度量（relative Shannon、relative Rényi、relative Tsallis），并计算相应的散度（Jensen-Shannon、Jensen-Rényi、Jensen-Tsallis）。为获取Shannon熵，引入了一种基于加权Lebesgue测度（weighted Lebesgue measure）的因子分解方法（factorization method）。

Result: Dunkl情形下的结果在Dunkl参数（Dunkl parameters）为零时与非Dunkl情形完全一致。反射算符与Dunkl参数对上述信息度量有显著影响，该影响通过图形形式进行了展示。

Conclusion: 研究表明，Dunkl-Schrödinger框架下的信息论方法能够有效刻画量子系统的信息结构，反射算符和Dunkl参数是调控信息度量的关键因素。

Abstract: An information theoretic analysis is done for the isotropic harmonic oscillator potential within the Dunkl-Schrödinger framework in spherical coordinates. Starting from the exact analytical eigensolution, various quantum information measures such as Shannon entropy, Rényi information, Tsallis entropy are derived. Besides, their relative measures like relative Shannon, relative Rényi, relative Tsallis as well as corresponding divergences (Jensen-Shannon, Jensen-Rényi, Jensen-Tsallis) are also obtained. In order to get Shannon entropy, a novel factorization method is introduced. This is facilitated through the use of well-known weighted Lebesgue measure. The results from the Dunkl case agree exactly with the non-Dunkl scenario, when Dunkl parameters vanish. The reflection operators and Dunkl parameters considerably influence the above measures. These are portrayed in graphical forms.

</details>

### [69] [The limit shape and emergence of the Discrete Gaussian level lines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06612)
*Joseph Chen,Eyal Lubetzky*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了(2+1)维离散高斯模型（Discrete Gaussian model）在低温、硬地板和零边界条件下顶层等高线的全局极限形状及其临界转变窗口，发现顶层等高线依Hausdorff距离收敛到确定的Wulff形状，并识别了宏观等高线出现的尖锐相变窗口，结果推广至$|\nabla φ|^p$模型族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前工作已证明(2+1)维离散高斯模型（ZGFF）在低温下表面形成近乎充满整个方盒的台地（plateau），且顶层等高线（top level lines）在盒子四边附近经重标度后收敛到Ferrari–Spohn扩散的乘积。但顶层等高线的全局极限形状，以及台地高度从H跃迁到H+1的临界窗口（critical window）仍未解决。

Method: 通过分析顶层等高线的Hausdorff距离收敛性，建立其全局极限形状，并利用单调性分析宏观等高线出现概率随系统尺寸L的变化，识别临界窗口宽度。

Result: (1) 对每个固定的n，第n层等高线依Hausdorff距离收敛到确定形状$\mathscr{L}_n$，在盒子四角附近以$N_n=L^{1-o(1)}$尺度呈现Wulff形状。(2) 宏观h等高线出现概率在L增长时单调递增（误差$o(1)$），并在宽度$\leq L^{1/2+o(1)}$的临界窗口内从接近0突变为接近1，且一旦出现即几乎占据整个盒子，Wulff和Ferrari–Spohn标度极限均适用。

Conclusion: 该工作完整刻画了(2+1)维离散高斯模型顶层等高线的全局极限与临界转变，并将结论推广至所有$p>1$的$(2+1)$维$|\nabla φ|^p$模型（ZGFF对应$p=2$）。

Abstract: Consider the $(2+1)$D Discrete Gaussian model (ZGFF) on an $L\times L$ box with a hard floor at height zero and zero boundary conditions, at low temperature. The second author, Martinelli and Sly (2016) showed that the surface has a plateau, filling nearly the full square, at height either $H$ or $H+1$ for an explicit function $H(L)$. In a companion paper, we studied the local laws of the top level lines near the four sides of the box, and showed that after rescaling each by $(L^{2/3-o(1)},L^{1/3-o(1)})$, they converge to a product of Ferrari--Spohn diffusions. Two key features of the top level lines remained unaddressed: their global limit shape, and the critical window marking the transition from a top plateau at height $H$ to one at height $H+1$. These features are intrinsically linked: deriving the global limit of the top level line is needed for determining whether it is preferable to be at height $H$ or $H+1$ near criticality.
  This work completes this picture as follows. First, we obtain the global limit of the top level lines: for every fixed $n$, the $n$-th from-the-top level line converges in Hausdorff distance to a deterministic shape $\mathscr{L}_n$ that features the Wulff shape at scale $N_n=L^{1-o(1)}$ near the four corners of the box. Second, we identify, for every $h$, the point of emergence of a macroscopic $h$ level line: the probability of this event is monotone increasing in $L$ (up to a $o(1)$ error), and undergoes a sharp transition from near $0$ to near $1$ in a critical window of width $\leq L^{1/2+o(1)}$ around a side length $L=L_c^{(h)}$. This transition is discontinuous in that, once a macroscopic level $h$ emerges, it immediately occupies nearly all the box, and the above global and local scaling limits (Wulff, Ferrari--Spohn) hold for it. The new results extend to the $(2+1)$D $|\nablaφ|^p$-models (ZGFF is the case $p=2$) for every fixed $p> 1$.

</details>

### [70] [Amplitude-dependent quantum hydrodynamics from a \(\coth\)-Madelung ansatz](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06561)
*C. Dedes*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于双曲型相位-振幅耦合的非线性Madelung变换推广形式，该构造赋予流体力学描述以内在几何结构，导致连续性方程和量子力项修正，并在超导电动力学中产生对空间密度梯度敏感的伦敦方程修正项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于标准极分解的Madelung变换在描述量子系统的耗散波动、复群速度（complex group velocity）以及振幅敏感输运（amplitude-sensitive transport）等现象时存在局限，亟需一种具有内在几何结构的推广形式。

Method: 采用形如 Ψ= R e^{iθ coth R} 的双曲型相位-振幅耦合（hyperbolic phase–amplitude coupling）替换传统极分解，其中R为实振幅场，θ为由薛定谔方程控制的辅助相位坐标，从而在振幅与相位之间建立奇异的双曲关系。

Result: 该构造导出的速度场包含密度梯度贡献，产生广义连续性方程（generalized continuity equations）和修正的量子力（quantum force）项；在超导电动力学框架下，伦敦方程（London equations）获得额外修正项，使迈斯纳响应（Meissner response）对空间密度梯度敏感。

Conclusion: 该非线性推广框架为理解量子系统中的耗散动力学、振幅敏感输运以及超导体中密度梯度依赖的电磁响应提供了新的几何化理论工具。

Abstract: We investigate a nonlinear extension of the Madelung transformation based on a hyperbolic phase--amplitude coupling of the form \[ Ψ= R e^{\imathθ\coth R}, \] where \(R\) is a real amplitude field and \(θ\) is an auxiliary phase coordinate governed by Schrödinger's equation. In contrast to the conventional polar decomposition, this construction imposes a singular hyperbolic relation between amplitude and phase, thereby endowing the Bohmian or hydrodynamic description with an intrinsically geometric structure. We show that the associated velocity field acquires a density-gradient contribution, producing generalized continuity equations and modified quantum force terms. When interpreted as a complex macroscopic order parameter, this generalized phase structure leads to modified superconducting electrodynamics; in particular, the London equations acquire additional contributions that render the Meissner response sensitive to spatial density gradients. The proposed framework is motivated by broader developments involving complex group velocities, dissipative wave propagation, and amplitude-sensitive transport in quantum systems.

</details>


### [71] [Computational Superiority of Non-Markovian Kerr Feedback in Continuous-Variable Quantum Reservoir Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06689)
*Daniel Soh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文证明，基于高斯光学（Gaussian optics）的连续变量量子储备池计算机（continuous-variable quantum reservoir computers, QRCs）受限于其线性本质，无法在储备池内部实现输入信号的跨时间非线性乘积。论文提出在时间延迟反馈回路（time-delayed feedback loop）中引入单一克尔元件（Kerr element），利用其强度依赖的相位（intensity-dependent phase）实现真正的非线性乘法，并结合损耗（loss）使每次回环产生不同的非线性指纹（fingerprint），从而在无需额外线性模式（linear modes）的情况下，将一个非线性模式的跨时间非线性秩（cross-time nonlinear rank）提升至与反馈深度（feedback depth）D相等，而N个线性模式的秩上限仅为2N。实验表明，在集成平台上D可达30至230，一个非线性模式可替代多达约100个线性模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性光学系统只能对光进行延迟、混合和叠加，无法实现乘法运算（multiplication），而乘法是非线性的本质要求。连续变量量子储备池计算（QRCs）若仅依赖高斯光学，则无法在储备池内部形成不同历史时刻输入的真实乘积，只能通过在读出层（readout）中分别存储每个历史输入后再相乘，这迫使测量高阶统计量（high-order measurement）呈指数级困难。因此，需要引入非线性机制以突破这一硬件性能瓶颈。

Method: 在时间延迟反馈回路中引入单个克尔元件，利用克尔效应（Kerr effect）使相位依赖于强度，从而在介质内部实现真正的乘法。反馈机制使光反复经过该非线性元件，每经过一次回环，一个模式便与其自身历史混合一次，将时间维度转化为空间维度：D次通过一个非线性模式可替代D个并行的线性模式。论文通过开放式系统模拟（open-system simulation）验证了激活过程，并在非线性信道均衡（nonlinear channel equalization）任务中确认了性能分离。

Result: 定理3与推论2证明：一个N模高斯储备池（Gaussian reservoir）的跨时间非线性秩（cross-time nonlinear rank）上限为2N，这是硬件天花板（hardware ceiling）；而一个单一克尔模式的跨时间非线性秩可达到其反馈深度D，且无需消耗额外模式。对每一个N，一个克尔模式能计算任何N模线性储备池无法完成的运算。在集成平台上，D可达30至230，因此一个非线性模式可替代多达约100个线性模式，代价是测量时间（measurement time）的增加。

Conclusion: 损耗在本方案中扮演了反直觉的关键角色：每次回环使光强衰减，导致每次通过时非线性相位不同，从而使每次回波（echo）拥有独特的指纹；若没有损耗，各次通过将产生冗余。这表明，通过精心利用损耗与非线性反馈的结合，可以指数级扩展量子储备池的计算能力，为实际量子计算硬件设计提供了新方向。

Abstract: A linear optical medium can delay, mix, and superpose light, but never make two pulses multiply: multiplication is nonlinear, and a linear system has no such operation. This roots a sharp limit on continuous-variable quantum reservoir computers (QRCs) built from Gaussian optics. Within the reservoir they cannot form genuine products of the input at different past times, the cross-time nonlinear correlations many temporal computations require; they can only fake them by storing each past input separately and multiplying in the readout, forcing an exponentially harder high-order measurement. We show that a single Kerr (intensity-dependent phase) element in a time-delayed feedback loop removes this limit. The Kerr effect makes phase depend on intensity, a true multiplication inside the medium; feedback makes the light revisit that element repeatedly, so one mode mixes its own history against itself once per round-trip. Feedback turns time into space: D passes through one nonlinear mode replace D parallel linear modes. We prove an unbounded resource separation (Theorem 3, Corollary 2): an N-mode Gaussian reservoir reaches cross-time nonlinear rank at most 2N, a hardware ceiling, while a single Kerr mode reaches rank equal to its feedback depth D, costing no extra modes. For every N, one Kerr mode performs a computation no N-mode linear reservoir can. Loss is the counterintuitive ingredient: each round-trip dims the light, so the nonlinear phase differs pass to pass, giving every echo its own fingerprint; without loss the passes would be redundant. We confirm activation on an exact open-system simulation and ground the separation in nonlinear channel equalization. Achievable D is 30 to 230 on integrated platforms, so one nonlinear mode replaces up to about 100 linear ones, at the price of measurement time.

</details>


### [72] [Quantum correlations and coherence in a two-qubit anisotropic $XY$ under magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07051)
*Ahmed Jellal,Pablo Díaz,David Laroze*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了均匀磁场下各向异性海森堡XY模型中热量子关联（纠缠、局域量子不确定度、Bell-CHSH非定域性）与相干性的调控机制。研究发现，磁各向异性、耦合各向异性、DM相互作用、温度和磁场等参数可有效调节量子资源的退化层次：非定域性最先消失，其次纠缠和一般量子关联，而相干性最为鲁棒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子信息与凝聚态物理交叉领域，各向异性海森堡模型是描述真实自旋系统的关键模型。本文旨在系统量化磁各向异性、耦合各向异性、DM相互作用、温度和磁场等参数如何调控热量子关联与相干性，从而为设计鲁棒的自旋基量子技术提供理论指导。

Method: 采用 concurrence $C$、局域量子不确定度（local quantum uncertainty, LQU）、Bell-CHSH 非定域性（Bell-Clauser-Horne-Shimony-Holt nonlocality）$\mathbb{B}$ 以及相干性（coherence）$C_l$ 作为量化指标，在均匀磁场 $B$ 下对各向异性海森堡 $XY$ 模型中的热量子资源进行系统分析。

Result: 低温下纠缠最大，但 $\delta_m=0$ 时出现纠缠猝死（sudden death），随 $\delta_m$ 增大变为平滑衰减。LQU 显示更强的各向异性抑制量子关联；$\mathbb{B}$ 在临界磁场 $B_c$ 处出现非单调峰值。Bell-CHSH 非定域性违反（$\mathbb{B}>2$）在 $B_c$ 以下存在，但热噪声（$T\geq 1$）可将其压制。相干性 $C_l$ 对热涨落最为鲁棒，高 $\delta_m$ 可抑制突变量子相变。DM 相互作用对纠缠生成至关重要，且 $D$ 与各向异性协同增强关联鲁棒性。量子资源热退化的层次为：非定域性先消失，其次纠缠，然后一般量子关联，相干性保持最久。

Conclusion: 研究证明，通过各向异性和外场参数可实现量子资源的可调控制，各向异性起到稳定纠缠和抑制突变量子相变的作用。所揭示的量子资源热退化层次为设计抗噪声的自旋基量子技术提供了重要参考。

Abstract: We study thermal quantum correlations and coherence in Heisenberg $XY$ model with anisotropic interactions under a uniform magnetic field $ B $. Using concurrence $C$, local quantum uncertainty (LQU), Bell-Clauser-Horne-Shimony-Holt (CHSH) nonlocality $ \mathbb{B}$, and coherence $C_l$ as quantifiers, we analyze how magnetic anisotropy $ δ_m $, coupling anisotropy $ δ_c $, Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya (DM) interaction $ D $, temperature $ T $, and magnetic field $ B $ modulate quantum resources. At low temperatures and relevant magnetic fields, the entanglement is maximized, but exhibits sudden death for $ δ_m = 0 $, which turns into a smooth decay as $ δ_m $ increases, highlighting its stabilizing role. LQU shows that stronger anisotropy suppresses quantum correlations, while $ \mathbb{B} $ induces a non-monotonic response peaking at a critical field $ B_c $. Bell-CHSH nonlocality violations ($ \mathbb{B} > 2 $) persist below $ B_c $, but thermal noise ($ T \geq 1 $) suppresses them. Coherence $ C_l $ is most robust to thermal fluctuations, especially for high \( δ_m \), which also dampens abrupt quantum phase transitions. The DM interaction is essential for entanglement generation, with $ D $ and anisotropy synergistically enhancing correlation resilience. We identify a hierarchy of thermal degradation: nonlocality ($ \mathbb{B} $) vanishes first, followed by entanglement ($ C $), then general quantum correlations (LQU), while coherence $ C_l $ persists the longest. These results demonstrate tunable control of quantum resources via anisotropy and external parameters, providing insights for the design of robust spin-based quantum technologies.

</details>


### [73] [Fun with Graph States: Nonlocal Bell Pairs and the Arf Invariant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06582)
*Bartlomiej Czech,Yichen Feng,Xianlai Wu,Minjun Xie*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现图态（graph states）的内积与部分振幅的幅值由图在F₂上的邻接矩阵（adjacency matrix）的秩决定，相位由其二次精细化的Arf不变量（Arf invariant）决定，并由此提出一种非局域张量分解，将图态分解为贝尔对（Bell pairs）与未纠缠辅助态的乘积，同时发展了一种用于计算图态中量子比特置换期望值的专门技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图态是量子信息中常用的量子态类，但对其内积与部分振幅的代数结构缺乏深入理解，尤其是在幅值与相位的数学刻画方面。本文旨在揭示这些量在图论与代数拓扑语言中的简洁表达，并探索其对于理解测量基量子计算（Measurement-Based Quantum Computation）中量子优势的潜在意义。

Method: 基于图论方法，本文通过分析图在二元域F₂上的邻接矩阵的秩来确定图态内积与部分振幅的幅值，并引入二次精细化的Arf不变量（Arf invariant）来刻画相位。此外，提出一种非局域张量分解（nonlocal tensor factorization），将图态表示为贝尔对与未纠缠辅助态的乘积，并开发了计算图态中量子比特置换期望值的专门技术。

Result: 图态内积与部分振幅的幅值由邻接矩阵在F₂上的秩决定，相位由Arf不变量决定。在此基础上，所有图态均可通过非局域张量分解表示为贝尔对与未纠缠辅助态的乘积。此外，建立了计算图态中量子比特置换期望值的专门技术，可用于多不变量（multi-invariants）的计算。

Conclusion: 这些发现为测量基量子计算中的量子优势提供了理论基础，并表明图态可以借助代数拓扑（algebraic topology）的语言进行更直观的刻画。非局域张量分解与置换期望值计算技术为图态的结构分析和应用提供了新的工具。

Abstract: We study inner products and partial amplitudes of graph states--a commonly employed class of quantum states, which are specified by graphs. We find that the magnitudes of these quantities are simply related to the rank of the adjacency matrix of the graph over F_2 while the phase is determined by the Arf invariant of its quadratic refinement. These facts motivate a nonlocal tensor factorization of the Hilbert space, with respect to which all graph states are products of Bell pairs with unentangled ancillae. These results may illuminate the quantum advantage in the framework of Measurement-Based Quantum Computation and suggest that graph states can be usefully visualized in the language of algebraic topology. In addition, we develop a specialized technique for computing expectation values of qubit-wise permutations in graph states, which is useful for calculating multi-invariants.

</details>


### [74] [Quantum-stabilized patterns in a vector Hopfield network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06597)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子效应对霍普菲尔德网络（Hopfield network）中存储模式稳定性和检索性能的影响，寻找超越经典联想记忆模型的新机制。

Method: 构建量子向量霍普菲尔德网络，利用自旋算符的非对易性引入内在量子动力学；推导该网络及其经典对应版本的状态方程（equations of state）与相图（phase diagrams）。

Result: 量子涨落出乎意料地稳定了存储模式；临界检索温度和目标模式重叠均高于经典网络；这种增强效应随模式负载（pattern loading）增加而增长，直至网络容量（network capacity）。

Conclusion: 量子涨落对模式存储的增强机制可类比为量子序-由-无序，该发现为构建量子增强的联想记忆提供了新途径。

Abstract: We introduce the quantum vector Hopfield network, in which patterns are formed by orientations of quantum vector spins; quantum dynamics arise intrinsically from the non-commutativity of the spin operators. We derive the equations of state and the phase diagrams for this network as well as its classical counterpart. We find that quantum fluctuations, surprisingly, stabilize the stored patterns. Both the critical retrieval temperature and the target pattern overlap are enhanced relative to the classical network. Additionally, we find that this enhancement grows with pattern loading up to network capacity. We interpret this effect as an analog of quantum order-by-disorder, a mechanism by which quantum fluctuations promote the formation of ordered phases. These findings offer a new route to quantum-enhanced associative memory.

### [75] [Sensing ac fields with quantum many-body scars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06611)
