<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体疤痕展现出弱遍历性破缺（weak ergodicity breaking）和长寿命相干动力学，但其在量子度量学（quantum metrology）中的潜力尚未被充分探索。本文旨在利用QFI研究MBS在弱交流场振幅估计中的度量学性能。

Method: 基于PXP模型，分析了不同探针算符（probe operator）诱导的连通性（connectivity）对传感性能的影响；通过频率扫描（frequency scanning）和有限尺寸分析（finite-size analysis）表征QFI随粒子数的标度行为；并发展出单塔近似（single-tower approximation）推导QFI的解析表达式。

Result: 驱动频率匹配疤痕间隔（scar gap）整数倍时，疤痕塔的近似均匀能级间距触发集体共振过程，使QFI在长时间窗口内呈二次时间增长；交错磁化（staggered magnetization）相比均匀磁化（homogeneous magnetization）能带来更优的QFI随系统尺寸增长行为。

Conclusion: 研究结果建立了如何利用结构化非遍历动力学（structured non-ergodic dynamics）增强量子传感协议（quantum sensing protocols）的可行性，并提供了可解析描述的框架。

Abstract: Quantum many-body scars (MBS) exhibit weak ergodicity breaking and long-lived coherent dynamics within an otherwise thermal spectrum. We investigate their metrological properties using the quantum Fisher information (QFI), focusing on estimating the amplitude of a weak AC field in the PXP model. We show that the approximately uniform energy spacing of the scar tower enables collective resonant processes when the driving frequency matches integer multiples of the scar gap, resulting in a quadratic-in-time growth of the QFI over an extended time window. We analyze how the connectivity induced by different probe operators shapes sensing performance and demonstrate that staggered magnetization leads to a more favorable growth of the QFI with system size than homogeneous magnetization. Through frequency scanning and finite-size analysis, we characterize the scaling of the QFI with the number of particles. Finally, we develop a single-tower approximation under resonant driving, deriving a compact analytical expression that captures the time dependence and system-size scaling of the QFI. Our results establish how to leverage structured non-ergodic dynamics in quantum sensing protocols.

### [76] [Higher-order Symmetric Quantum Mpemba Effect in Fragmented Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06653)
*Sreemayee Aditya,Sara Murciano,Xhek Turkeshi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过张量网络、哈密顿量模拟和可解耗散模型，发现强希尔伯特空间碎片化不会阻止量子Mpemba效应，而是将其重塑为冻结碎片记忆与活性碎片弛豫两个阶段，并揭示了高次对称性下的高阶量子Mpemba效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子Mpemba效应（quantum Mpemba effect）在强希尔伯特空间碎片化（Hilbert-space fragmentation）背景下是否仍然存在尚未明确。本文旨在解答这一问题，探究当守恒律将希尔伯特空间分裂为指数多个互不连通的Krylov扇区（Krylov sectors）时，该效应是否仍能存活。

Method: 采用电荷与偶极子同时守恒的电路和哈密顿量作为强希尔伯特空间碎片化的典型设定；利用副本张量网络（replica tensor-network）形式处理电荷与偶极子守恒门，计算至L=128的退火Rényi-2纠缠不对称性（annealed Rényi-2 entanglement asymmetry），并结合哈密顿量模拟与一个精确可解的耗散模型进行分析。

Result: 发现了高阶对称性量子Mpemba效应（higher-order symmetric quantum Mpemba effect）：电荷不对称性和偶极子不对称性分别在参数不同的时间尺度上呈现Mpemba式交叉。将态分解为冻结扇区（frozen sectors）和活性扇区（active sectors）后发现，冻结碎片保留有限不对称性阻碍完全恢复，而活性碎片则主导弛豫过程从而产生交叉现象。

Conclusion: 希尔伯特空间碎片化并不排除量子Mpemba效应，而是将其重塑为冻结记忆与活性碎片弛豫两个组分，为高矩对称性（higher-moment symmetries）下的Mpemba现象学提供了理论框架。

Abstract: A quantum system can restore a broken symmetry faster the more strongly it initially breaks it, an anomaly known as the quantum Mpemba effect. Whether this effect survives once conservation laws fragment the Hilbert space into exponentially many disconnected Krylov sectors has remained open. We address this question for circuits and Hamiltonians with simultaneous charge and dipole conservation, the paradigmatic setting for strong Hilbert-space fragmentation. Combining a replica tensor-network formulation for charge and dipole-conserving gates, which reaches the annealed Rényi-2 entanglement asymmetry up to $L=128$, with Hamiltonian simulations and an exactly solvable dissipative model, we uncover a higher-order symmetric quantum Mpemba effect: the charge and dipole asymmetries each display Mpemba-like crossings on parametrically distinct timescales. Resolving the state into frozen and active Krylov sectors reveals the mechanism: frozen fragments retain a finite asymmetry that obstructs full restoration, while active fragments host the relaxation responsible for the crossings. Fragmentation thus does not preclude the quantum Mpemba effect but reshapes it into frozen memory and active-fragment relaxation, providing a framework for the Mpemba phenomenology of higher-moment symmetries.

### [77] [Scalable Quantum Algorithms for Gutzwiller Projection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06919)

Method: 将任意BCS态的电路构造与振幅放大投影（AAGP, amplitude amplification for Gutzwiller projection）程序相结合，构建了可扩展的量子算法。AAGP利用振幅放大技术替代基于测量的后选择（measurement-based postselection），实现投影查询次数的二次缩减。

Conclusion: AAGP成为量子模拟中投影BCS态的一种实用化输入态制备协议，其资源缩放的大幅改善为强关联晶格模型的量子模拟扫清了关键障碍。

Abstract: Quantum simulation requires highly accurate input states. Gutzwiller-projected Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer (BCS) states provide physically motivated input states for solving strongly correlated lattice models, but their preparation on a quantum computer is hindered by the non-trivial nature of the Gutzwiller projection. We construct scalable quantum algorithms for this task by combining a circuit construction for arbitrary BCS states with the amplitude amplification for Gutzwiller projection (AAGP) procedure. AAGP yields a quadratic reduction in the number of projection queries compared with measurement-based postselection and leads to substantially improved fault-tolerant resource scaling. For projected BCS states optimized for the square-lattice $t$-$J$ model, we find that the projected-state weight decreases exponentially with system size, but the quadratic improvement is still large enough at physically relevant finite sizes to make a decisive practical difference. In particular, for a 100-site benchmark, AAGP reduces the required number of projection queries by about seven orders of magnitude. These results establish AAGP as an enabling input-state preparation protocol for projected BCS states in quantum simulation.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准连续时间量子退火（Continuous-time Quantum Annealing, QA）依赖线性调度，遇到小光谱间隙（small spectral gaps）瓶颈时退火时间呈指数增长，严重影响绝热性（adiabaticity）和基态制备效率。

Method: 采用dressed-CRAB方法优化平滑连续时间退火调度，结合动力学数字化表示（digitized representation of the dynamics）高效计算梯度，并在受挫伊辛环这一具有指数级小瓶颈能隙的模型上实施量子控制。

Result: 优化后的调度通过强非绝热机制（strongly nonadiabatic mechanism）绕过瓶颈，所需退火时间随系统大小线性增长而非指数增长；最低阶变分抵消绝热修正（variational counter-diabatic correction）在允许调度优化后未带来额外改进。

Abstract: Continuous-time Quantum Annealing (QA) is a strategy for preparing the ground state of nontrivial many-body systems. In its standard form, the dynamics is generated by a time-dependent interpolation between a simple driving Hamiltonian and the target problem Hamiltonian, usually implemented through a linear schedule. This approach faces the crucial bottleneck of small spectral gaps, which may require exponentially long annealing times to ensure adiabaticity. Here, we show how to implement quantum control over the annealing schedule in a frustrated Ising ring, one of the simplest models exhibiting an exponentially small bottleneck gap. By optimizing smooth continuous-time annealing schedules with a dressed-CRAB approach, and using a digitized representation of the dynamics to efficiently evaluate gradients, we construct protocols that strongly outperform standard fixed schedules. The optimized dynamics bypasses the bottleneck through a strongly nonadiabatic mechanism, leading to efficient ground-state preparation despite the exponentially small minimum gap. In particular, the annealing time required to reach a fixed residual-energy threshold is found to grow linearly with system size rather than exponentially. We further examine a lowest-order variational counter-diabatic correction and find that, once schedule optimization is allowed, it does not lead to any improvement.

### [79] [Long-range interactions assisted shortcuts to adiabaticity and battery charging in open quantum critical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07221)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以具有长程耦合的Kitaev链（Kitaev chain）为例，对比短程相互作用情形，分析长程相互作用下STA控制的相互作用强度随距离的代数衰减特性；并针对耗散环境下的量子电池充电提出一种改进的STA技术。

Conclusion: 长程相互作用是量子控制中的有价值资源，对量子技术具有直接的应用意义。

Abstract: In this work we show that long-range interactions can be significantly beneficial for implementing shortcuts to adiabaticity (STA) in many-body open quantum critical systems driven out of equilibrium, as well as for charging quantum batteries in the presence of dissipation. In sharp contrast to short range interactions where passage through criticality may demand STA control with non-zero interactions between infinitely distant spins, using the example of a Kitaev chain with long-range couplings, we find that the corresponding control may involve involve interaction strength with decays algebraically with distance. In case of non-unitary control, the advantage of long-range interactions manifest through reduction in the cost of STA. We further propose a modified STA technique aimed at charging a quantum battery in the presence of dissipation, in which case long-range interactions may enhance the resultant ergotropy. Our results establish long-range interactions as a valuable resource for quantum control, with direct implications for quantum technologies.

Abstract: The characterization of the quantum critical properties of genuine non-Hermitian many-body systems remains ambiguous as neither the state considered nor the definition of expectation values is unique. In this work, we investigate the quantum critical properties of two models of non-Hermitian XY spin chains with magnetic field. Using exact solutions, we systematically investigate the parameter dependence of the energy, the magnetization as well as the long-distance asymptotic behavior of static correlation functions. We compute expectation values within the standard formalism of quantum mechanics as well as within biorthogonal quantum mechanics and take two different states which one might reasonably consider to be the analog of the ground state of a Hermitian model. The critical properties, including such fundamental characteristics as the phase diagram, depend on both the formalism used as well as the state considered. We provide arguments in favor of the use of standard quantum mechanics. Which state to be taken in computations, depends on the (hypothetical) experimental preparation of the system.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Ising machines are a promising approach to solve combinatorial optimization problems. They map these problems onto the Ising model and search for low-energy configurations. However, navigating the rugged energy landscapes of these systems remains difficult. To improve this navigation, classical adiabatic annealing has been proposed in the literature as a heuristic optimization method for classical Ising machines. Using this technique, the Hamiltonian of the Ising machine is gradually transformed from an easily solvable Hamiltonian to the target Hamiltonian. However, its purported effectiveness is primarily motivated by an analogy to quantum adiabatic annealing, and systematic benchmarking has remained limited.
  In this work, we analyze the classical adiabatic annealing technique using continuation methods. Motivated by insights from this analysis, we propose an optimized annealing strategy we refer to as hybrid classical adiabatic annealing. We benchmark our proposed strategy using MaxCut instances with up to 800 spins and problems with external fields, for which it achieves a marginal improvement for a limited set of problems. We conclude that, although theoretically motivated and occasionally beneficial, the hybrid strategy does not offer a sufficient practical advantage over simpler, existing techniques.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阻尼自旋动力学（damped spin dynamics）对理解磁性材料至关重要，但量子修正对吉尔伯特阻尼机制的明确信号（signature）仍难以捉摸，因此需要寻找区分量子与经典吉尔伯特自旋阻尼的方法。

Method: 基于铁电衬底上的磁性二聚体体系，采用第一性原理（ab initio）计算表明极化反转（polarization reversal）可在铁磁（ferromagnetic）与反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）交换耦合之间切换；提出以磁化强度为基础的诊断方法，将磁化迹线（magnetization traces）与纠缠动力学（entanglement dynamics）关联；利用材料参数化的量子朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特（quantum Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert）模拟分析磁化动力学特征。

Result: 铁电衬底的极化反转可切换二聚体间的交换耦合类型；所提出的磁化诊断方法能够实现二聚体纠缠的铁电开关（on/off）控制；量子LLG模拟表明磁化动力学的特征原则上可用于推断量子吉尔伯特自旋阻尼的存在。

Conclusion: 该最小化、非易失性（non-volatile）的平台将第一性原理建模与实验可观测物理量相连接，为磁性自旋网络中电压控制的量子纠缠提供了起点。

Abstract: While damped spin dynamics is important for the understanding of magnetic materials, clear signatures of \emph{quantum corrections} to the Gilbert damping mechanism remain elusive. We propose a route to distinguish quantum and classical Gilbert spin damping using ferroelectric control of a magnetic dimer. Ab initio calculations for dimers on ferroelectric substrates show that polarization reversal switches the inter-spin exchange between ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic regimes. We formulate a magnetization-based diagnostic that relates magnetization traces to entanglement dynamics, which enables ferroelectrical on/off control of dimer entanglement. Material-informed quantum Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert simulations illustrate how the signature of magnetization dynamics can, in principle, be used to infer the existence of quantum Gilbert spin damping. This minimal and non-volatile platform connects first-principles modeling to experimentally accessible observables and provides a starting point for voltage-controlled quantum entanglement in magnetic spin networks.

</details>


### [83] [Driving Exchange Interaction in Spin Qubits with Quasi-Zero Pulses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07472)
*Julian D. Teske,Remy L. Delva,Shobhan Kulshreshtha,Yuval Baum,Florian Luthi,Fahd A. Mohiyaddin,Rostyslav Savytskyy,Thomas Watson,Pranav S. Mundada*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对自旋量子比特（spin qubits）中由交换相互作用（exchange interactions）引起的脉冲失真问题，提出了一种准零脉冲（quasi-zero pulses）设计方案，在减少可调参数数量的同时，实现了与完整滤波方法相当的门保真度（gate fidelities），并在Intel Tunnel Falls六量子点器件上进行了实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高保真量子门（high-fidelity quantum gates）的实现需要精确控制量子点中电子间的交换相互作用，但脉冲失真（pulse distortions）会限制控制精度。虽然线性动态失真可通过卷积控制信号来补偿，但这需要校准大量参数，增加了复杂度。

Method: 将净零脉冲（net-zero pulse）设计推广为准零脉冲（quasi-zero pulses），允许时间积分（time integral）为正但更小；系统性地开发了交换-唯一量子比特（exchange-only qubits）的完整门集（complete gate sets），并在仿真和实验中研究了脉冲持续时间、保真度与可调参数数量之间的权衡。

Result: 在Intel Tunnel Falls六量子点器件上进行的基准测试表明，优化后的门脉冲实现了与完整滤波方法（full filtering approach）相似的保真度，且脉冲持续时间相同，但需要的调优参数更少。

Conclusion: 这种复杂度的降低为快速且易于自动化的校准方案（calibration schemes）开辟了道路，使其能够兼容大规模商用量子器件。

Abstract: The implementation of high-fidelity quantum gates for spin qubits requires accurate control of exchange interactions between electrons confined in quantum dots, but pulse distortions can limit this control accuracy. Although linear-dynamical distortions can be compensated for by appropriately convolving the control signal, determining the necessary convolution requires detailed knowledge of the distortion's transfer function, and therefore the calibration of numerous parameters. Alternatively, control pulses can be designed to have a net-zero time integral canceling out linear-dynamical pulse distortions. We generalize net-zero pulse designs to quasi-zero pulses allowing net-positive but reduced time integrals. Using these pulse designs, we systematically develop complete gate sets for exchange-only qubits, and study the resulting tradeoffs between pulse duration, fidelity, and the required number of tunable parameters, both in simulation and experiment. We benchmark the optimized gate pulses on Intel's Tunnel Falls six-dot device and show they achieve fidelities similar to those obtained with a full filtering approach, with identical pulse durations and fewer tuning parameters. This reduction in complexity opens the door to fast and easily automated calibration schemes compatible with large-scale commercial quantum devices.

</details>

### [84] [Impact of capacity volatility and input substitutability on supply chain resilience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06874)
*Jaeseok Hur,Juha Jang,Meesoon Ha,Hawoong Jeong*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究基于Feld-Barthelemy框架，分析了产能波动性（capacity volatility）和投入可替代性（input substitutability）对随机供应链（stochastic supply chains）关键需求（critical demands）的影响，发现降低产能波动性和供应链结构多样化与传统库存扩张同等重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 供应链由于顺序生产依赖（sequential production dependencies）而固有地易受随机冲击（stochastic shocks）的影响；现有研究对产能波动性和投入可替代性如何共同决定关键需求缺乏系统分析。

Method: 采用截断正态分布（truncated normal distribution）建模产能，并引入改进的列昂惕夫型生产函数（modified Leontief-type production function），在Feld-Barthelemy框架下分析供应链中产能波动性与投入替代性的作用。

Result: 长供应链中降低产能波动性通常比提高平均产能更有效；投入可替代性能有效分散随机冲击；供应商多样化即使在最大容量固定的情况下也会因网络拓扑效应（network topology）提高关键需求。

Conclusion: 缓解产能波动性和结构性多样化供应路线对供应链韧性（supply chain resilience）的贡献与传统库存扩张同等关键。

Abstract: Supply chains are intrinsically vulnerable to stochastic shocks due to their sequential production dependencies. Building on the Feld-Barthelemy framework, we investigate how capacity volatility and input substitutability determine critical demands in stochastic supply chains. By modeling production capacity with a truncated normal distribution, we show that in long supply chains, reducing capacity volatility is often more effective than increasing average capacity, emphasizing the need for firm-level synchronization. Furthermore, introducing a modified Leontief-type production function reveals that input substitutability effectively disperses stochastic shocks. Supplier diversification inherently raises critical demands, even under fixed maximum capacities, by introducing the effect of network topology that independently enhances the resilience of physical stock. Our findings demonstrate that mitigating capacity volatility and structurally diversifying supply routes are just as crucial to supply chain resilience as traditional inventory expansion.

</details>


### [85] [A Machine-Learning Based Approach to the Evaluation of the Critical Scaling Behavior of Anisotropic Spin Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06925)
*Alina A. Chubarova,Ivan A. Mamonov,Marina V. Mamonova,Mikhail I. Bogachev,Pavel V. Prudnikov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于机器学习（ML）的方法，通过卷积神经网络（CNN）模型从蒙特卡罗模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）获得的相关矩阵中识别各向异性自旋系统的临界点。该方法能够快速估算临界温度，且结果与参考蒙特卡罗模拟高度一致，计算成本约为经典热力学方法的十分之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确描述相变（phase transition）并评估临界系统参数，对于理解多种材料的性质至关重要。现有基于蒙特卡罗模拟等经典热力学方法的计算成本较高，亟需更高效的替代方案。

Method: 从蒙特卡罗模拟得到的相关矩阵（correlation matrices）中训练卷积神经网络（convolutional neural network, CNN）模型；随后利用预训练模型作为快速估算器，通过多种互补方式从CNN推理中提取临界温度（critical temperature），以提高分析的鲁棒性（robustness）。

Result: 基于机器学习的估算结果与参考蒙特卡罗模拟结果高度一致；计算成本相比经典热力学方法降低约10倍。

Conclusion: 所提出的机器学习方法能够在显著降低计算开销的同时，准确识别各向异性自旋系统的临界点，为相变分析提供了一种高效且鲁棒的替代方案。

Abstract: Computational models adequately representing phase transitions and evaluating the critical system parameters are essential for the understanding of the properties of a wide range of materials. Here we propose a machine learning (ML)-based approach to the identification of the critical point in anisotropic spin systems. Our approach implies training of a convolutional neural network (CNN) model from the correlation matrices obtained by Monte Carlo simulations. Next, the pretrained model is employed as a fast estimator of the critical temperature, which can be extracted in several complementary ways from the CNN model inference, this way improving the robustness of the analysis. The ML-based estimates obtained in this study are in very good agreement with the reference Monte Carlo simulation results, while computational costs are about 10x lower compared to the classical thermodynamic approach.

</details>


### [86] [Fate of the Ising universality class under nonreciprocal interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06981)
*M. Akritidis,A. Garcés,A. Vasilopoulos,M. Carosi,D. Levis,N. G. Fytas*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟和动态重整化群分析，研究具有非互易视觉锥相互作用的二维伊辛模型（two-dimensional Ising model）的临界行为，发现其渐近临界指数与平衡态伊辛普适类一致，但无量纲量（如Binder累积量）出现各向异性非平衡修正，且非互易扰动在Wilson-Fisher固定点下是无关的，仅引起临界温度的有限移动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究显式破坏互易性（reciprocity）和细致平衡（detailed balance）的非互易视觉锥相互作用对二维伊辛模型临界行为的影响，检验该类非互易相互作用是否改变临界普适类。

Method: 采用大规模蒙特卡洛模拟和动态重整化群（dynamic renormalization-group）分析，在广泛的非互易耦合强度 λ 范围内研究二维伊辛模型的临界行为。

Result: 渐近临界指数与平衡态伊辛普适类（equilibrium Ising universality class）完全一致；Binder累积量（Binder cumulant）和关联长度比（correlation-length ratio）等无量纲量呈现各向异性非平衡修正并系统偏离平衡伊辛值；重整化群流显示非互易扰动在Wilson-Fisher固定点下是无关的，而临界温度发生正比于 λ² 的有限移动。

Conclusion: 二维伊辛临界性对此类定向相互作用表现出显著的鲁棒性（robustness）。

Abstract: We study the critical behavior of a two-dimensional Ising model with nonreciprocal vision-cone interactions, which explicitly violate reciprocity and detailed balance. Extensive Monte Carlo simulations and dynamic renormalization-group analysis show that the asymptotic critical exponents remain fully consistent with the equilibrium Ising universality class over a broad range of nonreciprocal coupling strengths $λ$. In contrast, dimensionless quantities such as the Binder cumulant and the correlation-length ratio display pronounced anisotropic nonequilibrium corrections and systematically deviate from their equilibrium Ising values. The renormalization-group flow further demonstrates that the nonreciprocal perturbation is irrelevant at the Wilson-Fisher fixed point while generating a finite shift of the critical temperature proportional to $λ^2$. Our results demonstrate the remarkable robustness of two-dimensional Ising criticality against this class of directional interactions.

</details>


### [87] [Phase lag enhances synchronization in coupled oscillators with inertia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07002)
*Sudo Yi,Cook Hyun Kim,Heetae Kim,B. Kahng*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了带惯性项的Kuramoto二阶模型中，通过施加对称破缺相位滞后（phase lag）来改善因多同步簇涌现而降低的全局同步性。结果表明，该相位滞后能够引导主簇沿特定路径与高阶簇合并，从而提升全局同步，并揭示了惯性振子系统中有控相位滞后增强同步的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二阶Kuramoto模型（second-order Kuramoto model）因惯性项的存在表现出与一阶模型不同的动力学行为，其核心差异在于多同步簇（multiple synchronized clusters）的涌现导致全局同步性降低。本文旨在探讨如何通过施加外部扰动（external perturbation）（如对称破缺相位滞后）来改善这种降低的同步性。

Method: 针对处于稳态的系统，向一组振子（oscillator）子集施加对称破缺（symmetry-breaking）的相位滞后（phase lag）扰动，观察系统全局同步行为的变化。

Result: 相位滞后能够引导主簇（primary cluster）沿特定路径运动，使其与更高阶的簇（higher-order cluster）合并，从而增强全局同步性（global synchronization）。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了一种通过有控相位滞后（controlled phase lag）改善惯性振子系统中夹带（entrainment）现象的机制，对惯性振子网络（inertial oscillator network）的同步控制具有潜在意义。

Abstract: The second-order Kuramoto model with inertia exhibits different dynamical behaviors than the first-order KM without inertia. A central difference is its lower synchronization due to the emergence of multiple synchronized clusters with different frequencies. We aim to investigate how such lowered synchronization can be improved by applying external perturbations to the system in a steady state, for example, a symmetry-breaking phase lag to a subset of oscillators. We find that this phase lag steers the primary cluster along a specific path and enables it to merge with higher-order clusters, thereby enhancing global synchronization. Our results reveal a mechanism by which controlled phase lag can improve entrainment in inertial oscillator systems, with possible implications for synchronization control in inertial oscillator networks.

</details>


### [88] [Asymmetry dynamics and nonequilibrium symmetry-breaking phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07188)
*Liv Hammer,Colin Rylands,Federico Carollo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了开放量子多体系统中对称性破缺情形下的不对称性动力学，发现了在该系统中特有的量子姆潘巴效应（quantum Mpemba effect），并将其扩展到对称性破缺相变框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有关于量子姆潘巴效应的工作主要集中于闭系统（closed systems），其特征为热平衡化和哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）对称性。本文旨在将量子姆潘巴效应的研究拓展至开放量子多体系统（open quantum many-body systems），并探索其中对称性破缺所引发的独特动力学行为。

Method: 通过分析具有对称性破缺的开放量子多体系统中的不对称性动力学，在对称相中研究不对称性的非单调演化，在破缺相中分析系统增大或减小不对称性能力之间的不平衡。

Result: 在对称相中，证明了量子姆潘巴效应的存在，该效应直接源于不对称性的非单调演化。在对称性破缺相中，分析了系统在增大与减小不对称性能力之间的不平衡。

Conclusion: 研究结果将量子姆潘巴效应的概念扩展至呈现对称性破缺相变（symmetry-breaking phase transitions）的开放量子多体系统，并确立了该系统作为观察和控制反常弛豫现象（anomalous relaxation phenomena）的平台。

Abstract: In classical settings, the Mpemba effect occurs when a hotter system cools faster than an initially colder one. In quantum systems, this effect can be reinterpreted exploiting the concept of symmetries, with the asymmetry of a subsystem playing the role of temperature. A quantum Mpemba effect arises when a more asymmetric state restores the symmetry faster than a less asymmetric one. Previous work mainly focuses on closed systems characterized by thermal equilibration and Hamiltonian symmetries. In this paper, we analyze the dynamics of asymmetry in an open quantum many-body system featuring symmetry breaking and uncover dynamical behavior that appears to be unique to these settings. In the symmetric phase, we demonstrate the existence of a quantum Mpemba effect, which emerges as a direct consequence of a non-monotonic evolution of the asymmetry. In the broken-symmetry phase, we analyze the imbalance between the system's ability to increase or to decrease its asymmetry. Our results extend the notion of quantum Mpemba effects to open quantum many-body systems exhibiting symmetry-breaking phase transitions and establish them as a platform for observing and controlling anomalous relaxation phenomena.

</details>


### [89] [Oscillatory-nonnormal decomposition of dissipation in Ornstein-Uhlenbeck processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07263)
*Ryuna Nagayama,Artemy Kolchinsky,Sosuke Ito*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究将Ornstein-Uhlenbeck过程稳态熵产生率分解为振荡贡献与非正态（nonnormality）贡献两部分，并分别建立了对应的基本权衡关系：振荡贡献导致耗散-相干权衡，其约束比已有猜想或推导的结果严格两倍；非正态贡献则体现了熵产生与弛豫加速之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究中，噪声诱导振荡系统的熵产生与相干性之间的权衡关系（dissipation-coherence trade-off）已被探讨，但Ornstein-Uhlenbeck过程中熵产生的不同物理来源尚未被系统分解，且已有权衡边界的严格性有待进一步澄清。

Method: 对Ornstein-Uhlenbeck过程的稳态熵产生率（steady-state entropy production rate）进行解析分解，将其划分为与振荡行为（oscillatory behavior）相关的部分和与非正态性（nonnormality）相关的部分。通过一个简单的珠-弹簧模型（bead-spring model）演示了该分解方法。

Result: 发现了两个不同的基本权衡关系：（1）振荡贡献对应的耗散-相干权衡，约束每个振荡周期内的熵产生不超过一个相关时间内的振荡次数，且该约束比此前其他系统中猜想或推导的结果严格两倍；（2）非正态贡献对应的熵产生与弛豫加速（acceleration of relaxation）之间的权衡。

Conclusion: Ornstein-Uhlenbeck过程的稳态熵产生可分解为两个具有不同物理意义的贡献，各自对应独立的权衡关系，这为理解非平衡系统中的耗散、振荡与非正态性之间的基本联系提供了更精细的理论框架。

Abstract: We provide a decomposition of the steady-state entropy production rate associated with an Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process into two contributions: one associated with oscillatory behavior and one associated with nonnormality. We also show that each contribution is associated with a different fundamental trade-off. The oscillatory contribution leads to the dissipation-coherence trade-off for noise-induced oscillations, which bounds the entropy production per oscillatory period by the number of oscillations within one correlation time. Notably, the trade-off is twice as strict as those conjectured or derived for other systems. The nonnormal contribution leads to a trade-off between entropy production and acceleration of relaxation. We also demonstrate the decomposition using a simple bead-spring model.

</details>


### [90] [Modelling time-irreversible avalanches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07268)
*Andrea Baldassarri,Andrea Puglisi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对雪崩（avalanche）形状中观察到的时间反演对称性破缺现象，提出了一种非平衡（non-equilibrium）ABBM模型，该模型与布朗回转器（Brownian Gyrator）及速率-状态（rate-and-state）模型相关。该模型能够复现颗粒摩擦实验中的现象，并将实验中易测量的不对称性指标与动力学熵产生率（entropy production rate）联系起来，为非平衡动力学中时间反演对称性的理论研究提供了系统性框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管在磁材料、地震等多种系统中均观测到雪崩形状的不对称性，这反映了非平衡动力学（non-equilibrium dynamics）的特征，但目前缺乏对这一特征的理论控制与系统性研究。

Method: 本文提出了“噼啪噪声”（crackling-noise）现象中ABBM模型的非平衡扩展。该模型与随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）中描述热各向异性（thermal anisotropy）的布朗回转器密切相关，同时可置于速率-状态模型的框架下进行理解。

Result: 该模型成功复现了颗粒摩擦（granular friction）实验中的观测现象。研究将一种实验易测的雪崩形状不对称性度量与动力学熵产生率建立了定量关联。

Conclusion: 该非平衡ABBM模型为雪崩形状中时间反演对称性（time reversal symmetry）破缺的研究提供了系统的理论工具，并通过不对称性与熵产生率的关联，建立了一个连接实验观测与非平衡热力学核心量的理论桥梁。

Abstract: We investigate the problem of the time reversal symmetry of fluctuations, as witnessed by the average shape of avalanches. This quantity has been measured in a variety of systems, ranging from magnetic materials to earthquakes. Although an asymmetric shape is often observed, which is a signature of a non-equilibrium dynamics, there is no general theoretical control of this feature. In this paper, we propose a non equilibrium extension of a paradigmatic model for ``crackling-noise'', the so called ABBM model. Our model is strictly related to the Brownian Gyrator, which has been previously introduced in stochastic thermodynamics as the simplest model for thermal anisotropy, but it can also be framed in the context of rate-and-state models. It reproduces the phenomenology observed in experiments on granular friction, and allows for a systematic theoretical study of the asymmetry. We manage to correlate a measure of asymmetry, that can be easily computed in experiments, with the entropy production rates of the dynamics.

</details>


### [91] [Topologically Enforced Lifshitz Multicriticality in One Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07380)
*Kuang-Hung Chou,Xue-Jia Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在一维手性对称费米子系统中发现了一类由拓扑驱动的新型Lifshitz多临界点（multicritical point），其形成仅依赖于相邻临界线拓扑性质的变化，而非传统的临界指数变化；该多临界点具有稳健的拓扑简并，但伴随Li-Haldane体边对应关系的破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑相变（topological phase transition）已揭示拓扑可拓展量子相变（quantum phase transition）的普适类，但拓扑可区分量子临界线之间的多临界性（multicriticality）尚未被充分探索。

Method: 在一维手性对称费米子系统中系统性地构造并研究了由拓扑强制形成的Lifshitz多临界点（topologically enforced Lifshitz multicritical point），通过分析相邻临界线拓扑性质的变化来驱动多临界行为。

Result: 该多临界点展现出稳健的拓扑简并（robust topological degeneracy），但出现了Li-Haldane体边对应关系（bulk-boundary correspondence）的意外破坏。

Conclusion: 发现了超越传统临界指数变化机制的多临界点新类型，并通过简单物理图像解释了体边对应关系的破坏现象。

Abstract: Recent advances have revealed that topology can further enrich the universality classes of quantum phase transitions, thereby extending beyond the traditional paradigms of statistical and condensed matter physics. However, multicriticality between topologically distinct quantum critical lines remains insufficiently explored. In this Letter, we systematically construct and investigate a novel class of topologically enforced Lifshitz multicritical points in one dimensional chiral symmetric fermionic systems. Such multicriticality is driven solely by changes in the topology of neighboring critical lines, beyond previously recognized multicritical points that are typically induced by changes in critical exponents. More importantly, the topologically enforced multicriticality identified here can host robust topological degeneracies while surprisingly exhibiting a breakdown of the Li Haldane bulk boundary correspondence-a phenomenon we elucidate through a simple physical picture.

</details>


### [92] [Fermion sign problem and the structure of Lee-Yang zeros. II. Finite temperature results for a model system without interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07415)
*Ran-Chen He,Jia-Xi Zeng,Shu Yang,Cong Wang,Qi-Jun Ye,Xin-Zheng Li*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用可精确求解的一维无相互作用的环上粒子模型，分析李-杨零点（Lee-Yang zeros）随温度演化的轨迹，揭示低温下零点靠近ξ=-1导致解析延拓失效的机制，并提出一种先高温后低温拟合的新策略以获取低温费米子（fermionic）性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前序工作[He et al. Phys. Rev. E 113, 24115 (2026)]分析了0 K下ξ的李-杨零点（Lee-Yang zero）之后，理解这些零点如何随温度（temperature, T）演化是重要但复杂的课题，因此需要发展一个可解析求解的模型来系统研究这一问题。

Method: 采用一维无相互作用的环上粒子模型（noninteracting one-dimensional particle-on-a-ring model），该模型可解析求解；通过计算配分函数（partition function）的解析结构，追踪李-杨零点随温度的轨迹；并提出一种新的拟合策略：先利用符号问题自由（sign-problem-free）的ξ∈[0,1]数据解析延拓至ξ=-1以获得可靠的高温费米子性质，再通过对ξ无关的剩余项φ(β)=Z_F进行温度拟合，将信息推广至低温区域。

Result: 零点轨迹显示：T=0时源于ξ=-1的零点在低温下仍保持在-1附近，主导符号因子（sign factor）并强烈约束沿实ξ轴的解析延拓；这解释了直接外推和基于轮廓拟合（contour-based fitting）等隐式方案在低温下失败、而在高温下合理的原因。基于配分函数的多项式结构提出的新策略可有效获取低温费米子性质。

Conclusion: 为诊断解析延拓（analytic continuation）的有效性提供了可精确求解的基准模型（benchmark），并为处理更具现实意义的相互作用费米子系统（interacting fermionic systems）提供了一条可行的路径。

Abstract: Beyond the analysis of the Lee-Yang (LY) zero of $ξ$ at $0$ K presented by our previous work [He et. al. Phys. Rev. E 113, 24115 (2026)], it is important but intricate to understand how these zeros evolve with temperature ($T$). Here, we use an analytically solvable noninteracting one-dimensional particle-on-a-ring model to address this. We determine the trajectories of these zeros and analyze how their evolution with $T$ reshapes the analytic structure of the partition function. In particular, the zero originating from $ξ=-1$ at $T=0$ remains close to $-1$ at low $T$, where it governs the sign factor and strongly constrains continuation along the real $ξ$ axis. This explains why both direct extrapolation and implicit schemes such as contour-based fitting can fail in the low-$T$ regime, even at high fitting order, while becoming reasonable again once the relevant zeros move away at higher $T$s. Furthermore, based on the polynomial structure of the partition function, we propose a new fitting strategy for low-$T$ fermionic properties. The key is to first obtain reliable high-$T$ fermionic properties by continuing sign-problem-free data in $ξ\in[0,1]$ to $ξ=-1$, and then extend this information toward lower $T$ through $T$-fitting of the $ξ$-independent remainder $φ(β)=Z_{\text{F}}$. These results provide a solvable benchmark for diagnosing the validity of analytic continuation and suggest a possible route toward treating more realistic interacting fermionic systems.

</details>

### [93] [Structural gradients and strain partitioning across the mouse Achilles tendon enthesis revealed by in situ X-ray scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06504)
*Isabella Silva Barreto,Moritz L. Stammer,Moritz P. K. Frewein,Claire Camy,Juraj Todt,Michael Meindlhumer,Jozef Keckes,Stefano Checchia,Sandrine Roffino,Martine Pithioux,Tilman A. Grünewald*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过同步辐射小角/广角X射线散射（SAXS/WAXS）结合原位拉伸实验，系统绘制了小鼠跟腱止点（enthesis）中胶原纤维、分子及羟基磷灰石矿物颗粒在纳米至分子尺度的变形响应图谱。结果揭示止点处的载荷传递具有空间异质性和层级依赖性：组织应变20%时，纳米纤维应变约1-2%，胶原分子约0.5%，羟基磷灰石晶体约0.05%，遵循约1:0.1:0.01:0.001的比例。这一分级附着机制通过区域特异性载荷分担和层级应变分配来缓解应力集中并维持肌腱-骨骼过渡区的力学完整性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 肌腱止点（enthesis）是肌腱插入骨骼的部位，尽管两种组织在材料属性上存在巨大不匹配，却表现出极高的力学耐久性，这源于多层级长度尺度上的成分、结构与组织梯度。然而，尽管已有大量关于止点结构与力学的研究，其局部变形机制仍不清楚。

Method: 研究采用同步辐射扫描小角/广角X射线散射（synchrotron scanning small- and wide-angle X-ray scattering），结合小鼠跟腱止点的原位拉伸测试（in situ tensile testing），对胶原纤维（collagen fibrils）和分子（molecules）以及羟基磷灰石（hydroxyapatite）矿物颗粒和晶体的力学响应进行广泛的空间映射。

Result: 在软组织和矿化组织中均观察到纳米至分子尺度的结构梯度，且越靠近界面的区域，变形响应越强、越迅速。应变随层级逐级递减：组织应变20%时，纳米纤维应变约1-2%，胶原分子约0.5%，羟基磷灰石晶体约0.05%，比例约为1:0.1:0.01:0.001。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，止点的载荷传递（load transfer）既具有空间异质性（spatially heterogeneous），又具有层级依赖性（hierarchy-dependent）。这表明分级附着（graded attachment）通过区域特异性载荷分担（region-specific load sharing）和层级应变分配（hierarchical strain partitioning）来适应变形，与非胶原基质（non-collagenous matrix）内的耗散贡献一致，从而缓解应力集中并维持肌腱-骨骼过渡区的力学完整性。

Abstract: The enthesis is the insertion site of tendon into bone and exhibits a high mechanical durability despite the large mismatch in material properties between the two tissues. This durability stems from gradients in composition, structure and organization on multiple hierarchical length scales. Despite extensive research on enthesis structure and mechanics, the local deformation mechanisms are poorly understood. Synchrotron scanning small- and wide-angle X-ray scattering was combined with in situ tensile testing of the mouse Achilles tendon enthesis to extensively map the mechanical response of the collagen fibrils and molecules as well as the hydroxyapatite mineral particles and crystals. Gradients in nano- and molecular scale structure and a stronger and more immediate deformation response towards the interface compared to further away were observed in both the soft and mineralized tissue. The strain decreased progressively across hierarchical levels; with an applied tissue strain of 20% the nanoscale fibrils were strained by ~1-2%, the collagen molecules by ~0.5% and the hydroxyapatite crystals by ~0.05%, thus following an approximate ratio of 1 : 0.1 : 0.01 : 0.001. These results show that load transfer across the enthesis is both spatially heterogeneous and hierarchy-dependent. This indicates that the graded attachment accommodates deformation through region-specific load sharing and hierarchical strain partitioning, consistent with a contribution from dissipation within the non-collagenous matrix. In doing so, the enthesis can mitigate stress concentrations and maintain mechanical integrity across the tendon-to-bone transition.

Method: 本文采用综述性回顾（review）方法，基于Barbiellini四十余年的科学生涯轨迹，从早期ADONE和LEP（DELPHI）的正负电子对撞机实验，到AGILE、Fermi和PAMELA等空间任务，系统梳理高能天体物理作为探测器驱动科学的发展历程。

Result: Barbiellini在硅径迹探测器、量热法和数据分析方面做出了个人贡献，并在国际协作中展现出领导力。他的工作深刻影响了γ射线天文学、宇宙射线物理和反物质研究等关键领域，在高能宇宙观测领域留下了不可磨灭的印记（indelible mark）。

Conclusion: Barbiellini的跨学科方法在概念层面产生了重要影响（conceptual impact），未来高能宇宙观测的前进道路建立在他所奠定的基础之上（built on the foundations he helped lay）。

Abstract: The development of modern high-energy astrophysics has been deeply intertwined with advances in particle detector technology. Guido Barbiellini Amidei (1943-2024) played a pivotal role in bridging experimental particle physics and astrophysical observation. His scientific career spanned over four decades, from early electron-positron collider experiments at ADONE and LEP (DELPHI) to space based missions such as AGILE, Fermi, and PAMELA. This memorial paper reviews the evolution of high-energy astrophysics as a detector-driven science, highlighting key domains where Barbiellini left an indelible mark: gamma-ray astronomy, cosmic-ray physics, and antimatter studies. We discuss his personal contributions to silicon tracking, calorimetry, data analysis, and his leadership in international collaborations. The conceptual impact of his interdisciplinary approach is examined, and future perspectives in the observation of the high-energy universe are outlined, recognizing that the path forward is built on the foundations he helped lay

### [95] [Circular Raman responses from angular-momentum inequivalence in CoSi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06909)

Method: 采用螺旋度分辨拉曼光谱（helicity-resolved Raman spectroscopy）对手性晶体CoSi进行实验测量，并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）来重现两种效应并阐明其对称性起源。

Result: 发现ROA与频率分裂分别源于不同的对称性通道：ROA对应轴向多极对称性（axial multipolar symmetry），而频率分裂源于结构手性（structural chirality）。

Conclusion: 携带相反晶格角动量的声子态的不等价性是圆偏振拉曼响应的统一原理，螺旋度分辨拉曼光谱可关联拓扑材料中手性声子的角动量结构。

Abstract: Circularly polarized Raman scattering in solids exhibits distinct phenomena such as Raman optical activity (ROA) and chiral-phonon-induced frequency splitting, whose relationship has remained unclear. Here we show that these seemingly different responses can be understood within a common framework based on the inequivalence of phonon states carrying opposite crystal angular momenta. Using helicity-resolved Raman spectroscopy of the chiral crystal CoSi, we find that ROA and frequency splitting arise from different symmetry channels, namely axial multipolar symmetry and structural chirality, respectively. First-principles calculations reproduce both effects and clarify their symmetry origins. These results establish angular-momentum inequivalence as a unifying principle of circular Raman responses and link helicity-resolved Raman spectroscopy to the angular-momentum structure of chiral phonons in topological materials.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在混合迷宫分形（mixed labyrinth fractals）基础上引入随机化机制，建立一个更灵活的框架来研究分形拓扑、弧维度（arc dimensions）和最短路径性质。

Method: 通过在每个迭代层级以固定选择概率随机选取迷宫模式来生成结构；提出近似路径矩阵替代大量迭代模拟。

Result: 各向同性（isotropy）从自相似分形扩展到随机混合类；发现了最短路径维度随混合概率呈现线性、非线性单调趋势以及具有最大值的转变行为；近似路径矩阵能够可靠地复现统计结果。

Conclusion: 模式属性在决定分形结构与动力学中具有关键作用，研究结果对扩散、信号处理和天线设计等物理系统具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: In this paper, the class of randomised mixed labyrinth fractals is introduced. It is a class of finitely ramified Sierpinski carpets that generalize mixed labyrinth fractals. The structures are generated by randomly selected labyrinth patterns with fixed selection probabilities at each iteration level, offering a flexible framework to study fractal topology, arc dimensions, and shortest path properties. Here, the focus lies on analysing how the randomised mixing of patterns - specifically their shape, symmetry, and path geometry - effects arc dimensions, path lengths, and isotropy restoration. The study reveals that isotropy, previously shown for self-similar fractals, extends to the randomised mixed class. Various scaling behaviours of shortest path dimensions with respect to the mixing probability are identified, including linear and nonlinear monotonic trends, as well as transitions with maxima. The approximated path matrix is proposed as an efficient alternative to extensive iterative simulations, reliably reproducing statistical results. The findings highlight the relevance of pattern properties in determining fractal structures and dynamics and suggest applications in physical systems such as diffusion, signal processing, and antenna design.

### [97] [Persistent currents in signed directed networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06716)
*Davide Cipollini,Guido Caldarelli*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过将符号有向网络（signed directed network）中的带符号磁拉普拉斯算子（signed magnetic Laplacian）解释为有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian），建立了网络理论与量子相干（quantum coherence）之间的映射关系，从而将持久电流（persistent current）的概念从环形和格子系统推广到任意拓扑结构，并利用网络循环空间（cycle space）对规范不变通量（gauge-invariant flux）进行自然定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者希望利用网络理论（network theory）来描述物理系统中的量子相干性，并将持久电流这一原本局限于简单几何结构（如环和格子）的概念推广到任意拓扑网络上，从而为量子技术领域的相关问题提供一种实用的处理方式。

Method: 将符号有向网络中的带符号磁拉普拉斯算子视为有效哈密顿量，将相关边相位（edge phase）解释为离散规范场（discrete gauge field）；在正则系综（canonical ensemble）框架下，将持久电流定义为对规范不变通量变化的热力学响应，并在网络的循环空间上对该通量进行自然定义。

Result: 持久电流被约束在无散子空间（divergence-free subspace）中，并可分解为独立循环上的贡献。该方法成功构建了一个再现霍夫施塔特蝴蝶谱（Hofstadter butterfly spectrum）的符号有向网络，验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: 该映射不仅为量子技术中涉及的量子相干性问题提供了一种实用处理手段，还为图论中拉普拉斯算子（Laplacian operator）的重要性提供了物理诠释，将其与物理系统中的紧束缚哈密顿量（tight-binding Hamiltonian）联系起来。

Abstract: Network theory can be fruitfully used to describe quantum coherence in physical systems. To that purpose we introduce persistent currents in signed directed networks by interpreting the signed magnetic Laplacian as an effective Hamiltonian and the associated edge phases as a discrete gauge field. In a canonical ensemble, persistent currents arise as thermodynamic responses to variations of gauge-invariant fluxes. We show that these fluxes are naturally defined on the cycle space of the network, and that the resulting currents are constrained to the divergence-free subspace and decompose onto independent cycles. This formulation provides a direct generalization of persistent currents from rings and lattices to arbitrary topologies. Detection of persistent currents provides a signature of the quantum phase coherence supported by the network, and a direct signature of the geometry of its cycle space. Such a mapping, not only allows a practical way to deal with quantum coherence for a variety of situations in the field of quantum technologies, but it also allows a physical interpretation of the importance of the Laplacian operator in graph theory, linking its role to the one of Hamiltonian (i.e. a tight-binding one) in physical systems. To test the power of the method, we construct a signed directed network that reproduces the Hofstadter butterfly spectrum.

</details>

TL;DR: 通过大规模蒙特卡洛模拟，研究三维自旋玻璃的低温激发，发现基态能量和链接重叠的零温外推与已有结果一致；激发分形维数最佳拟合支持复制对称性破缺（RSB）理论，同时验证了Parisi-Toulouse温度标度与重叠等价假说。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用大规模蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation），在最大尺寸$L=18$的格点上进行研究，通过外推至零温（zero temperature）获得基态性质。

Result: 能量与链接重叠（link overlap）的零温外推与先前基态研究结果吻合；激发分形维数（fractal dimension）的最佳拟合支持复制对称性破缺（Replica-Symmetry Breaking, RSB）理论；重叠概率分布$P(q)$满足Parisi-Toulouse温度标度（Parisi-Toulouse temperature scaling）；数据还提供了对重叠等价假说（overlap-equivalence hypothesis）的有力验证。

Conclusion: 研究结果明确支持复制对称性破缺（RSB）理论对三维自旋玻璃低能激发的描述，并验证了Parisi-Toulouse标度与重叠等价假说的正确性。

Abstract: We study the low-energy excitations of the three dimensional spin glass through a large-scale Monte Carlo simulation on lattices up to $L=18$. We find smooth extrapolations down to zero temperature, which, in the case of the energy and of the link overlap, can be directly -- and favourably -- compared with previous investigations featuring ground states (i.e., at zero temperature). The best fit for the fractal dimension of the excitations is provided by Replica-Symmetry Breaking theory, but we also consider the alternative TNT description. The $P(q)$ is found to verify the Parisi-Toulouse temperature scaling. Our data provides a spectacular confirmation of the overlap-equivalence hypothesis.

### [99] [Theory of learning of high-dimensional controlled non-linear dynamical systems (I): models and methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07247)
*Pierfrancesco Urbani*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类基于理论基础的模型，用于研究通过在线随机梯度下降训练的神经常微分方程，并利用动态平均场理论在高维极限下求解其训练动力学和学习曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经常微分方程（neural ODEs）在连接连续时间动力系统建模与离散深度学习范式方面具有重要价值，但其训练动力学的理论理解尚不充分。作者旨在为这类模型建立一个严格的理论分析框架。

Method: 提出一类理论可解的神经ODE模型，训练采用在线随机梯度下降（online stochastic gradient descent）；利用动态平均场理论（dynamical mean field theory）在高维极限（high-dimensional limit）下求解其训练动力学。

Result: 推导出神经ODE模型在高维极限下的训练动力学方程和相应的学习曲线（learning curves）。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解神经ODE的训练与泛化特性提供了严格的理论基础，并可推广至多层神经网络、自回归模型、生成模型及递归神经网络等多种场景。

Abstract: Neural ordinary differential equations (neural ODEs) have rapidly gained prominence as a powerful and unifying framework for conceptualizing artificial neural networks, elegantly connecting the continuous-time modeling of dynamical systems with the discrete, data-driven paradigm of modern deep learning. Beyond their practical advantages they offer fresh theoretical insights into the training and generalization properties of neural networks. The distinctive feature of this framework is its dual dynamical nature: inference dynamics, which govern the ODE evolution during forward computation, and training dynamics, which control the optimization of model parameters. This makes neural ODEs a particularly well-suited theoretical framework for studying a large variety of settings such as multi-layer neural networks (ResNets for example), autoregressive models (with next-token generation dynamics), generative models, and recurrent neural networks in theoretical neuroscience. In this work, we introduce a theoretically grounded class of models for studying neural ODEs trained via online stochastic gradient descent. We solve the training dynamics of these models via dynamical mean field theory and derive learning curves in the high-dimensional limit.

</details>


### [100] [Topological Anderson insulators and reentrant topological transitions in a quasiperiodic long-range Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07274)
*Fang-Ming Meng,Qi-Bo Zeng*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维长程Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型在准周期无序下的拓扑性质，发现系统会出现具有不同绕数的拓扑安德森绝缘体（TAI）相、多重可重入拓扑相变，以及阶梯状拓扑安德森转变现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究长程跳跃和准周期无序的相互作用如何影响一维Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型的拓扑相图，特别是无序诱导的拓扑相和重入相变现象。

Method: 构建包含第三近邻跳跃（third-nearest-neighbor hopping）和准周期无序（quasiperiodic disorder）的一维长程Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型，分析其在干净极限下的绕数（winding number）相图，并通过引入准周期无序研究拓扑相变。

Result: 准周期无序显著改变相图并诱导系列拓扑相变；出现具有不同绕数的拓扑安德森绝缘体（TAI）相，且在强无序区能隙近乎闭合时仍可存续；发现多重可重入拓扑相变（reentrant topological phase transitions）；观察到阶梯状拓扑安德森转变（staircase-like topological Anderson transitions）。

Conclusion: 长程跳跃与准周期无序的相互作用可产生丰富的无序诱导拓扑相和重入拓扑转变现象。

Abstract: We study a one-dimensional long-range Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model with third-nearest-neighbor hopping and subject to quasiperiodic disorder. In the clean limit, the model hosts phases characterized by winding numbers $W=-1,0,1$ and $2$. The introduction of quasiperiodic disorder profoundly modifies the phase diagram and induces a series of topological phase transitions. Owing to the competition between topological dimerization and localization, topological Anderson insulating (TAI) phases with different winding numbers emerge and can persist even when the spectral gap becomes nearly closed in the strong-disorder regime. In addition, we uncover multiple reentrant topological phase transitions induced by varying either the quasiperiodic disorder strength or the hopping amplitudes. Remarkably, the system exhibits staircase-like topological Anderson transitions, where the real-space winding number evolves through successive quantized steps with increasing disorder strength. Our results demonstrate that the interplay between long-range hopping and quasiperiodic disorder generates a rich landscape of disorder-induced topological phases and reentrant topological transition phenomena.

### [101] [Element-Specific Solute Trapping and Grain Structure Evolution during Laser Powder Bed Fusion of Multicomponent Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06568)
*Xinxin Yao,James Hanagan,Md Shafiqur Rahman Jame,Mallikharjun Marrey,Mohsen Taheri Andani,Raymundo Arróyave,Veera Sundararaghavan,Lei Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过CALPHAD辅助的高斯过程回归（Gaussian Process Regression, GPR）相场（Phase-Field, PF）方法，揭示了激光粉末床熔融（laser powder bed fusion, LPBF）中元素特异性溶质捕获（solute trapping）如何主导SS316L多元合金的成核行为与晶粒结构演化，并定量分解了各元素对过冷度（undercooling）的贡献及其非平衡敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在LPBF快速凝固条件下，溶质捕获呈现出元素特异性，改变了多元合金的非平衡分配、成分过冷（constitutional undercooling）和晶粒选择行为，但其中具体的微观机制尚不清晰。因此，需要定量描述非平衡多元热力学与晶粒演化，以阐明这一过程。

Method: 采用CALPHAD辅助的高斯过程回归（GPR）辅助相场（PF）方法，对SS316L在多种LPBF凝固条件下的非平衡多元热力学与晶粒演化进行定量描述。预测的晶粒形态与尺寸转变通过电子背散射衍射（EBSD）测量进行验证。

Result: 增加凝固速率驱动了从溶质扩散控制的成核向溶质捕获控制的晶粒生长的成分依赖性转变；溶质捕获强化了非平衡溶质再分布，抑制了等轴晶的形成。定量分解表明C、Cr和Mo对总过冷度贡献占主导，而S和P等低分配系数元素的过冷贡献被强烈抑制。

Conclusion: 元素特异性溶质捕获主导了多元合金在LPBF中的晶粒选择行为，为非平衡凝固条件下的合金设计提供了机理基础。

Abstract: Under the rapid solidification conditions of laser powder bed fusion (LPBF), solute trapping manifests in an element-specific manner, altering nonequilibrium partitioning, constitutional undercooling, and grain selection behavior in multicomponent alloys. Here, we elucidate the mechanisms by which element-specific solute trapping governs nucleation behavior and grain structure evolution during LPBF demonstrated on a SS316L. This requires quantitative description of nonequilibrium multicomponent thermodynamics and grain evolution across broad LPBF solidification conditions, which is achieved through a CALPHAD-informed Gaussian Process Regression (GPR)-assisted Phase-Field (PF) approach. The predicted transitions in grain morphology and grain size are validated against EBSD measurements under multiple LPBF processing conditions. Results demonstrate that increasing solidification rate drives a composition-dependent transition from solute diffusion-controlled nucleation to solute trapping-controlled grain growth, where nonequilibrium solute redistribution intensified by solute trapping suppresses equiaxed grain formation despite high cooling rates. Quantitative decomposition of multicomponent undercooling further reveals distinct element-specific sensitivities to solute trapping, where C, Cr, and Mo remain dominant contributors to the overall undercooling, while the undercooling contribution of low-partitioning elements such as S and P are strongly suppressed relative to their equilibrium values under rapid solidification conditions. These results reveal how element-specific solute trapping governs grain selection in multicomponent alloys, providing a mechanistic basis for alloy design under nonequilibrium solidification conditions.

</details>


### [102] [Temperature-Induced Crossover of Coherent Phonon Mechanisms in Chiral 2D Perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06616)
*Katherine A Koch,Matthew P Hautzinger,Matthew C Beard,Ajay Ram Srimath Kandada*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过相位分辨共振脉冲受激拉曼散射，揭示了二维金属卤化物钙钛矿中激发态结构重构随温度演化的机制，发现温度会导致从场驱动的受激拉曼散射（ISRS）到布居驱动的相干声子位移激发（DECP）的交叉，展现了通过温度主动调控柔性二维框架中激子-晶格相互作用的新策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子激发与晶格自由度之间的耦合从根本上决定了杂化钙钛矿的光电功能，但激发态势能面（potential energy surface, PES）随温度的结构演化性质尚不清楚。

Method: 选择具有异常大的温度依赖性键角方差的手性钙钛矿框架以最大化结构顺应性，并采用相位分辨共振脉冲受激拉曼散射（phase-resolved resonant impulsive stimulated Raman scattering）测量相干声子动力学，解析激子-晶格缀饰（exciton-lattice dressing）的实时结构路径。

Result: 观察到温度诱导的从场驱动的受激拉曼散射（Impulsive Stimulated Raman Scattering, ISRS）到布居驱动的相干声子位移激发（Displacive Excitation of Coherent Phonons, DECP）的交叉。低温下动量驱动的ISRS路径占主导，而热能的增加使晶格软化并增强坐标驱动的移位路径，使激子能够采样激发态势能面中更陡峭、高度非简谐的区域。

Conclusion: 温度能够主动调控柔性二维框架的激发态结构坐标，为在手性光电子学中调节激子-晶格相互作用提供了实用策略。

Abstract: The coupling between electronic excitations and lattice degrees of freedom fundamentally dictates the optoelectronic functionality of hybrid perovskites. While the potential energy surfaces (PESs) of the electronic excited states are typically considered static, albeit modulated by thermal disorder, the exact nature of their structural evolution with temperature remains elusive. Here, we demonstrate that the excited-state structural reconfiguration in two-dimensional metal-halide perovskites is explicitly temperature-evolving, governed by lattice compliance. We select a chiral perovskite framework with an exceptionally large, temperature-dependent bond angle variance to maximize the structural compliance. Through phase-resolved resonant impulsive stimulated Raman scattering, we measure the coherent phonon dynamics and resolve the real-time structural pathways of exciton-lattice dressing. We observe a temperature-induced crossover from field-driven Impulsive Stimulated Raman Scattering (ISRS) to population-driven Displacive Excitation of Coherent Phonons (DECP). While momentum-driven ISRS pathways dominate at low temperatures, increasing thermal energy softens the lattice and enhances coordinate-driven displacive pathways, allowing excitons to sample steeper, highly anharmonic regions of the excited-state PES. Our results show that temperature can actively modulate the excited-state structural coordinates of flexible 2D frameworks, offering a practical strategy to tune exciton-lattice interactions in chiral optoelectronics.

</details>


### [103] [Matching Terahertz and Hall Mobilities as a Hallmark of Intrinsic Charge Transport in Metal-Halide Perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06623)
*Dmitry R. Maslennikov,Ben P. Carwithen,Vladimir V. Bruevich,Yichao Cai,Davide Nodari,Navendu Mondal,Xijia Zheng,Beier Hu,Nicola Gasparini,Jarvist M. Frost,Vitaly Podzorov,Artem A. Bakulin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究在软晶格钙钛矿外延单晶CsPbBr₃中证实了本征电荷输运（intrinsic charge transport）机制可在毫米尺度上成立，通过光学泵浦-太赫兹探针（OPTP）与霍尔效应（Hall-effect）联合测量获得一致的迁移率，表明无缺陷输运在软晶格材料中是可以实现的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软晶格材料（如金属卤化物钙钛矿）中的载流子输运在不同长度尺度上通常被认为高度不均匀，受本征热电子无序与非本征静态无序的共同影响，导致不同电学和光学测量技术报告的载流子迁移率（carrier mobility）存在显著分歧，从而引发一个关键问题：真正的本征电荷输运机制能否在这些材料的宏观单晶中扩展。

Method: 采用外延生长（epitaxial）的CsPbBr₃单晶作为模型系统，搭建了一个专用器件平台，可在同一单晶样品上同时进行霍尔效应测量和光学泵浦-太赫兹探针（OPTP）测量，从而直接比较宏观稳态输运与超快局域输运行为。

Result: 在室温下两种测量技术获得了一致的迁移率约30 cm²V⁻¹s⁻¹，这是CsPbBr₃有可靠记录的最高值之一；两种技术均显示出类能带（band-like）的空穴迁移率温度依赖关系，且功率指数（power exponent）相似。

Conclusion: 在毫米尺度的软晶格钙钛矿中可实现无缺陷电荷输运，局域超快与宏观稳态响应由相同的本征输运机制主导；该工作建立了一种可用于新兴半导体中本征迁移率基准测试的可靠方法。

Abstract: Charge-carrier transport in soft-lattice materials, including metal-halide perovskites, is often perceived to be highly heterogeneous across different length scales, and influenced by both the intrinsic (dynamic) thermal electronic disorder and extrinsic (static) disorder due to crystal defects, impurities, grain boundaries, and surface states. As a consequence, the reported carrier mobilities obtained by different electrical and optical measurement techniques frequently disagree, raising a critical question: can a truly intrinsic charge transport regime (that is, a regime not dominated by static disorder) extend across macroscopic single crystals of these materials? Here, we demonstrate such a regime in an exemplary metal-halide perovskite system, epitaxial CsPbBr$_{3}$ single crystals, where the local mobility obtained via optical pump-terahertz probe (OPTP) spectroscopy quantitatively agrees with the macroscopic transport mobility across a broad range of experimental conditions. Using a dedicated device platform that enables concurrent Hall-effect and OPTP measurements on the same single-crystalline sample, we obtain consistent room-temperature mobilities of ~ 30 cm$^{2}$V$^{-1}$s$^{-1}$, among the highest reliably reported for CsPbBr$_{3}$. Both techniques reveal band-like temperature dependence of the hole mobility with similar power exponents, confirming that the same intrinsic transport mechanism governs the ultrafast/local and steady-state/macroscopic responses. These results show that defect-free charge transport is achievable in soft-lattice perovskites on millimetre length scales and establish a robust methodology for benchmarking intrinsic mobility in emerging semiconductors.

</details>


### [104] [Symmetry-Protected Phonon Topology and Low Lattice Thermal Conductivity in Square-Octagonal Chalcogenides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06680)
*Nair Surabhi Suresh,Mondal Chiranjith,Alam Aftab,Singh Nirpendra*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算与声子玻尔兹曼输运理论，揭示了四方-八边形硫属化物单层（MoS2和SnS）中声子带拓扑特征与热输运的关联：对称性保护的节线（nodal lines）及其交叉产生的四重狄拉克点（fourfold Dirac points）增强了声子群速度，而近乎平坦的节线则强烈抑制群速度；拓扑能带交叉附近的声子软化和非简谐散射增强显著降低了晶格热导率，室温下so-SnS和so-MoS2的κ_l值分别降至4.0 W/mK和18.7 W/mK，相较六方相分别降低超过两倍和八倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非常规晶格几何为实现对称性保护拓扑声子态（symmetry-protected topological phonon states）提供了有效平台，这些拓扑声子态可强烈影响晶格热输运。本文旨在探索拓扑声子能带特征与二维材料热输运之间的直接联系。

Method: 结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与声子玻尔兹曼输运理论（phonon Boltzmann transport theory），对四方-八边形（square-octagonal, so）硫属化物单层MoS2和SnS进行对称性分析和热输运计算。

Result: 对称性分析揭示了非平庸声子带拓扑（nontrivial phonon band topology）以对称性保护节线的形式存在。不同对称性本征值的节线交叉产生四重狄拉克点，增强声子群速度（group velocity, vg）；而近乎平坦的节线则强烈抑制vg。拓扑能带交叉附近的声子软化和非简谐散射增强显著降低了晶格热导率（κ_l）。室温下so-SnS的κ_l为4.0 W/mK，so-MoS2为18.7 W/mK，相较六方相分别降低两倍和八倍以上。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了二维材料中声子带拓扑（phonon band topology）与热输运之间的直接关联，表明晶格对称性和拓扑能带工程（topological band engineering）是调控热学性质的有效途径，并为设计可控热流的拓扑声子学和热电（thermoelectric）器件提供了启示。

Abstract: Unconventional lattice geometries provide an effective platform for realizing symmetry-protected topological phonon states that can strongly influence lattice heat transport. In this work, we explore the relationship between topological phonon band features and thermal transport in square--octagonal (so) chalcogenide monolayers, namely MoS2 and SnS, by combining first-principles calculations with phonon Boltzmann transport theory. Symmetry analysis reveals the presence of nontrivial phonon band topology in the form of symmetry-protected nodal lines. Crossings between nodal lines carrying different symmetry eigenvalues produce fourfold Dirac points that enhance the phonon group velocity (vg), whereas nearly flat nodal lines lead to strong suppression of vg. The coexistence of these features, together with substantial phonon softening and enhanced anharmonic scattering around the topological band crossings, markedly suppresses the lattice thermal conductivity ($κ_l$). As a result, room-temperature $κ_l$ values of 4.0 W/mK for so-SnS and 18.7 W/mK for so-MoS2 are obtained, representing reductions by more than a factor of two and eight, respectively, relative to their hexagonal phases. Our results uncover a direct connection between phonon band topology and heat transport in two-dimensional materials, highlighting lattice symmetry and topological band engineering as promising routes for tailoring thermal properties. These findings further suggest opportunities for designing topological phononic and thermoelectric devices with controllable heat flow.

</details>


### [105] [Engineering magnetic anisotropy and ferromagnetism in topological Kagome metal GdV6Sn6 via Nd substitution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06734)
*Santosh Karki Chhetri,M. M. Sharma,Jian Wang,Dinesh Upreti,Gokul Acharya,Md Rafique Un Nabi,Jin Hu*

TL;DR: 本研究报道了Kagome金属(NdxGd1-x)V6Sn6的结构、电学和磁学性质。通过用较轻的Nd原子替代Gd位，可将GdV6Sn6的复杂磁基态调控为类铁磁态，并引入磁各向异性（c轴成为易轴）。输运测量表明磁性与电子属性存在强耦合，所有组分均在低磁场下呈现负磁阻，端元化合物在高磁场下出现四重各向异性分量。这些发现突显了稀土元素替换在调控非磁性Kagome层化合物磁各向异性与磁输运行为中的作用，对自旋电子学和拓扑应用具有潜在意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome金属RM6X6体系为探索磁性与电子现象提供了丰富平台，且其性质可通过稀土元素与过渡金属的组合进行调控。本研究旨在通过稀土元素替换（Nd替代Gd），系统调控GdV6Sn6的复杂磁基态和磁各向异性，并揭示磁性与电子输运之间的耦合关系。

Method: 合成了Kagome金属(NdxGd1-x)V6Sn6系列样品，系统表征了其结构、电学和磁学性质。通过改变Nd/Gd比例实现稀土替换，测量了不同组分下的磁化强度、电阻率和磁电阻等物理量。

Result: Nd替代Gd将GdV6Sn6的复杂磁基态转变为类铁磁态，并使原本各向同性的磁化强度呈现各向异性，c轴成为易轴。所有组分在低磁场下均观察到负磁阻现象，说明磁性与电子输运存在强耦合；此外，端元化合物在高磁场下出现四重各向异性分量。

Conclusion: 稀土元素替换是调控RM6X6体系磁各向异性和磁输运行为的有效手段，这些发现对自旋电子学和拓扑材料应用具有潜在意义。

Abstract: Kagome metals with the formula RM6X6 (R = rare-earth, M = 3d transition metal, and X = Sn/Ge) provide a rich platform for exploring magnetic and electronic phenomena, with tunable properties enabled by the combination of rare-earth elements and transition metals. In this study, we report the structural, electrical and magnetic properties of Kagome metal (NdxGd1-x)V6Sn6. We demonstrate that substituting lighter Nd atoms at the Gd site tunes the complex magnetic ground state of GdV6Sn6 into a ferromagnetic-like one. Moreover, the isotropic magnetization of GdV6Sn6 becomes anisotropic, with the c-axis emerging as the easy axis. Transport measurements reveal a strong coupling between magnetism and electronic properties, with negative magnetoresistance observed at low magnetic fields in all compositions. In addition, a fourfold anisotropy component tends to emerge in end compounds at higher magnetic fields. These findings highlight the role of rare-earth substitution in tuning magnetic anisotropy and magneto-transport behaviour in RM6X6 compounds, featuring a non-magnetic Kagome layer, with potential implications for spintronic and topological applications.

</details>


### [106] [Reactivity-Informed Machine Learning for Performance Prediction and Design Space Exploration of Alkali-Activated Slag](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06765)
*Qiyao He,Zhanzhao Li,Kai Gong*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究构建了迄今最大的碱激发矿渣（AAS）文献数据集（>3100条强度记录），通过多种机器学习（ML）算法对比发现，结合矿渣化学组成、细度、养护条件及试件几何参数可显著提升抗压强度预测性能。引入的平均金属氧化物解离能（AMODE）作为前驱体反应活性的物理可解释描述符，在保持预测精度的同时简化了输入维度。模型解释揭示了Na₂O掺量与硅模数的非单调效应、高含水率及大试件尺寸下的强度下降等物理一致趋势。统计约束下的设计空间探索绘制了强度、碳排放与成本之间的权衡图谱，识别出在相似成本下碳排放显著低于普通硅酸盐水泥（OPC）的高强度区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在胶凝材料（cementitious materials）领域，尤其是前驱体与激发剂化学性质多变的碱激发材料（alkali-activated materials）中，建立配合比设计、原材料性质、养护条件与性能之间的定量关系一直是一个长期挑战。

Method: 首先从文献中整理出包含3100余条抗压强度记录、155种化学组成不同的粒化高炉矿渣（GGBS）及24个属性的最大型碱激发矿渣（AAS）数据集。随后，在逐步丰富的特征场景下对多种机器学习（ML）算法进行基准对比，并引入平均金属氧化物解离能（AMODE）作为前驱体反应活性的物理可解释描述符。

Result: 整合矿渣组成、细度、养护条件及试件几何参数可提升预测性能。AMODE作为紧凑替代描述符可获得与显式氧化物组成相当的预测性能。模型解释揭示了Na₂O掺量与硅模数的非单调效应、高含水率与大试件尺寸下的强度降低趋势，以及AMODE比单一氧化物含量更连贯地表示的耦合氧化物效应。设计空间探索揭示了反应活性依赖的强度—碳排放—成本权衡。

Conclusion: 本工作展示了反应活性信息驱动的机器学习（reactivity-informed ML）能从异质性AAS数据中提取具有物理意义的趋势，并指导依赖原材料来源的胶凝材料设计。公开共享的数据集将支持水泥与混凝土研究的后续进展。

Abstract: Establishing quantitative relationships among mix design, raw material properties, curing conditions, and performance remains a long-standing challenge in cementitious materials, particularly for alkali-activated materials with variable precursor and activator chemistry. Here, we curated the largest literature-derived alkali-activated slag (AAS) dataset to date, comprising over 3100 compressive strength records, 155 chemically distinct ground granulated blast-furnace slags (GGBSs), and 24 attributes incorporating precursor chemistry, fineness, and reactivity. Multiple machine learning (ML) algorithms were benchmarked across progressively enriched feature scenarios, demonstrating that integrating GGBS compositions, fineness, curing conditions, and specimen geometry improves predictive performance. The average metal oxide dissociation energy (AMODE), a physically interpretable representation of precursor reactivity, provides a compact alternative descriptor to explicit oxide compositions while enabling comparable predictive performance. Model interpretation revealed physically consistent trends from heterogeneous data, including non-monotonic effects of Na2O dosage and silicate modulus, reduced predicted strength at higher water content and larger specimen size, and coupled oxide-level effects more coherently represented by AMODE than by individual oxide contents. Statistically constrained design space exploration reveals reactivity-dependent trade-offs among strength, embodied CO2 emissions, and cost. The design maps identify high-strength regions with substantially lower CO2 emissions than OPC-based references at similar cost. Overall, this work demonstrates how reactivity-informed ML can extract physically meaningful trends from heterogeneous AAS data and guide source-dependent binder design. The curated dataset is publicly accessible to support advances in cement and concrete research.

### [107] [Atomic-scale phase-field modeling for 2D ferroelectrics including non-Gaussian fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06771)
*Kairi Masuda,Yu Kumagai*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过引入非高斯涨落推广了原子尺度相场模型，使其能处理更复杂非均匀体系（如表面），并将其应用于单层SnTe，成功再现铁电-顺电相变，并通过原子级熵分解揭示了Sn原子对高温熵的更大贡献是相变驱动力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有原子尺度相场模型（atomic-scale phase-field modeling）主要假设原子振动遵循高斯概率分布（Gaussian probability distribution），这限制了其在表面等复杂非均匀体系中的适用性。本文旨在克服这一局限，推广该方法以处理非高斯涨落（non-Gaussian fluctuations）。

Method: 将自由能泛函（free-energy functional）扩展至包含非高斯涨落项，从而推广原子尺度相场框架；在NVT系综（NVT ensemble）中对单层SnTe进行模拟，并与分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟结果进行对比验证。

Result: 预测的平衡极化（equilibrium polarization）与分子动力学模拟结果吻合更好；成功再现了铁电-顺电相变（ferroelectric-to-paraelectric phase transition）；通过对熵进行逐原子分解，获得了原子级别分辨的局域熵（atomically resolved maps of local entropy）图像，发现高温下Sn原子对熵的贡献大于Te原子，这是相变的驱动因素。

Conclusion: 该工作拓宽了相场方法（phase-field approach）在更广泛原子体系中的适用性，并为基于高分辨率热力学（high-resolution thermodynamics）的原子级相变理论指明了方向。

Abstract: Atomic-scale phase-field modeling extends the phase-field framework down to the level of individual atoms by treating the probability density of atomic vibrations as a field variable and constructing a corresponding free-energy functional from this atomic field together with interatomic potentials. In this way, the framework has the potential to visualize local thermodynamic states with atomic-level resolution, just as conventional phase-field modeling has served as a computational microscope for free energy, stress, and related quantities at mesoscopic scales. However, existing formulations mainly assume Gaussian probability distributions for atomic vibrations, which limits their applicability to more complex and heterogeneous systems such as surfaces. In this work, we generalize the atomic-scale phase-field methodology by extending the free-energy functional to include non-Gaussian fluctuations. We apply this approach to monolayer SnTe in the NVT ensemble and show that the predicted equilibrium polarization is in better agreement with molecular dynamics simulations and that the ferroelectric-to-paraelectric phase transition is successfully reproduced. Furthermore, by decomposing the entropy on a per-atom basis, we visualize atomically resolved maps of local entropy and find that Sn atoms contribute more strongly to the entropy than Te atoms at high temperature, which is a driving factor of the ferroelectric-to-paraelectric phase transition. These results broaden the applicability of phase-field approaches to a wider range of atomic systems and suggest a route toward an atom-resolved theory of phase transitions based on high-resolution thermodynamics.

### [108] [Characterization of Nonlinear Dynamics in Semiconductors in Frequency Domain using Modulated Photoexcitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06952)
*Attia Awan,Rong Tang,Zhou Kang,Khadga Jung Karki*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体中载流子动力学（carrier dynamics）因自由载流子、激子等多种激发物种共存及其与陷阱和声子的相互作用而异常复杂。传统时间分辨方法虽然被广泛使用，但其响应往往呈非指数形式，导致解释存在歧义（ambiguity），亟需一种能够清晰解析非线性动力学参数的新方法。

Method: 提出一种频域方法：利用一对相位调制光束激发半导体样品（以CdSe为测试系统），对总光致发光信号进行频域分析，从中提取自由载流子和激子的不同类型复合速率等动力学参数。

Result: 通过频域分析相位调制光束诱导的总光致发光中的频率分量，能够有效评估自由载流子和激子的各类复合速率参数。以CdSe为测试系统的实验验证了该方法的可行性。

Conclusion: 所提出的频域方法可作为一种简单的诊断工具，用于表征与半导体器件功能密切相关的超快过程（ultrafast processes），其优势在于避免了传统时间分辨方法中非指数响应带来的解释歧义。

Abstract: Carrier dynamics in semiconductors is inherently complex owing to the coexistence of different excited species, such as free carriers and excitons, and their interactions among themselves and with traps and phonons. It is usual to use time-resolved responses to identify the processes that contribute to the dynamics. However, the responses often are non-exponential, leading to ambiguity in the interpretation. Here, we propose a frequency domain method to characterize nonlinear dynamics in semiconductors using CdSe as the test system. We show that by analyzing the frequency components in the total photoluminescence induced by a pair of phase-modulated beams, the parameters, such as rates of different types of recombination of free carriers and excitons, can be evaluated. The method can be used as a simple diagnostic tool to characterize ultrafast processes that are relevant to the functionality of semiconductor devices.

### [109] [Electric-field induced trends of exchange interactions in transition-metal trilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06980)
*Moinak Ghosh,Stefan Heinze,Souvik Paul*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用密度泛函理论，系统研究了外加电场对无支撑过渡金属三层膜中Heisenberg成对交换相互作用及超越Heisenberg的多自旋高阶交换相互作用的影响，发现交换常数在电场下呈线性变化但基态不变，且变化幅度与4d覆盖层相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究外加电场如何调制过渡金属超薄多层膜中的Heisenberg成对交换相互作用（pairwise exchange interaction）及超越Heisenberg的多自旋高阶交换相互作用（multi-spin higher-order exchange interactions），以探索电场调控磁性的微观机制。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）进行计算；体系为Fe层夹于4d（Ru, Rh, Pd）和5d（Ir）过渡金属层之间的无支撑三层膜，并考虑fcc与hcp两种堆叠方式。通过计算有/无外加电场（±1.0 V/Å）下的自旋螺旋（spin spiral）能量色散，并拟合提取交换常数；基于多Q态（multi-Q states，如uudd态和3Q态）的总能量计算高阶交换常数。

Result: 外加电场下能量色散定性不变，磁基态（magnetic ground state）不发生改变。成对交换常数在电场约±0.6 V/Å范围内呈线性依赖，符号不变；最近邻交换常数变化为百分之几，更远邻常数变化可达数十个百分点。高阶交换常数在弱电场下也近似线性变化，变化幅度达百分之十。电场引起的交换相互作用变化与Fe局域态密度（local density of states, LDOS）在费米能级（Fermi level）处的自旋依赖变化相关。

Conclusion: 外加电场可通过自旋依赖的静电屏蔽效应（spin-dependent screening）调制Fe层的局域电子结构，进而线性地影响成对交换常数和高阶交换常数，但对磁基态不产生定性改变；该电场响应敏感依赖于4d覆盖层的材料种类。

Abstract: Using density functional theory, we have performed a systematic study of the Heisenberg pairwise exchange interaction and the beyond Heisenberg multi-spin higher-order exchange interactions in unsupported transition-metal trilayers in the presence of external electric fields. The systems consist of a hexagonal atomic Fe layer sandwiched between 4$d$ (Ru, Rh, and Pd) and 5$d$ (Ir) transition-metal layers. Both fcc and hcp stacking of the 4$d$ overlayer has been taken into account. To scan a large part of the magnetic phase space, we have calculated the energy dispersion of spin spirals without and with applied electric fields up to $\pm 1.0$ V/Å. We find that the energy dispersion remains qualitatively the same upon applying the electric fields and the magnetic ground state remains unchanged. The exchange constants obtained by fitting the energy dispersions exhibit a linear dependence on the electric field up to values of about $\pm 0.6$ V/Å. The sign of the calculated pairwise and higher-order exchange constants remain unchanged with electric-field, however, their field induced variation is sensitive to the 4$d$ overlayer. The changes are on the order of a few percent for the nearest-neighbor exchange constant and up to a few ten percent for beyond nearest-neighbor constants. The higher-order exchange constants are calculated based on the total energies of multi-$Q$ states, such as the $uudd$ and the 3$Q$ state. Similar to the pairwise exchange constants, we find a nearly linear field dependence of the higher order constants at small electric fields and variations of up to ten percent. We study the spin-dependent screening of the electric field for the three trilayers and relate the modifications of the pairwise and higher-order exchange interactions to the electric field induced changes of the spin-dependent Fe local density of states and its variation at the Fermi level.

Abstract: Graphdiynes constitute an emerging class of two-dimensional sp-sp2 carbon allotropes with tunable electronic properties not accessible by graphene. Although flawless monolayer growth of graphdiyne networks has been attempted by means of on-surface synthesis protocols, the experimental realization of fully covalent and structurally ordered graphdiyne networks remains challenging due to the persistence of metalated intermediates and reaction byproducts, limiting the structural self-organization required for long-range covalent order. Here, we demonstrate that adding minute amounts of Fe atoms on the surface during the growth can exceptionally improve the synthesis of a covalent 2D graphdiyne monolayer framework on Au(111). By means of low-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy, combined with density functional theory, we unveil the atomic-scale surface dynamics of the reaction. We demonstrate the crucial role of Fe atoms that bond with Br by-products, thereby forming Fe-Br species that promote the removal of Au adatoms and drive the conversion from a metalated network to a purely covalent framework upon mild annealing conditions. Moreover, we show the covalent graphdiyne network to be structurally and electronically decoupled from the underlying metallic substrate, revealing a finite bandgap of about 1.6 eV defined by the position of p_z frontier orbitals. These results establish a viable route for the atomically precise on-surface synthesis of all-carbon graphdiynes, and open the way to semiconducting 2D carbon materials complementing graphene.

### [111] [Unravelling the Role of Stacking Disorder on the Optoelectronic Properties of Zn3P2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07042)
*Francesco Salutari,Nico Kawashima,Aidas Urbonavicius,Helena Rabelo Freitas,Raphael Lemerle,Thomas Hagger,Kimberly A. Dick,Anna Fontcuberta i Morral,Simon Escobar Steinvall,Maria Chiara Spadaro,Silvana Botti,Jordi Arbiol*

TL;DR: 该研究发现Zn3P2薄膜中存在一类此前未报道的平面缺陷（planar faults），其位移矢量位于(001)晶面内；通过赝立方描述建立了平面缺陷与旋转畴（rotated domains）之间的对应关系，揭示两者均源于Zn子晶格中空位位点的灵活排序。第一性原理计算显示该类缺陷的形成能极低（2.5 mJ m-2），且不引入中隙电子态或显著扰动局域静电势，表明其在电子学上是良性的；缺陷间接降低器件性能的机制可能是作为光学活性点缺陷（optically active point defects）的优先偏析位点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用（扫描）透射电子显微镜（(scanning) transmission electron microscopy）识别缺陷结构；通过赝立方描述（pseudo-cubic description）建立平面缺陷与旋转畴之间的对应关系；利用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算缺陷形成能及电子结构影响。

Result: 发现一类位移矢量位于(001)晶面内的平面缺陷；平面缺陷与旋转畴均源于Zn子晶格中空位位点（vacant sites）的灵活排序（flexible ordering）；平面缺陷形成能极低（2.5 mJ m-2）；该类缺陷不引入中隙电子态（mid-gap electronic states）且不显著扰动局域静电势（local electrostatic potential）。

Conclusion: Zn3P2中的平面缺陷在电子学上是良性的（electronically benign），不直接损害器件性能；但其可能通过作为光学活性点缺陷的优先偏析位点（preferential segregation sites），间接降低器件性能。

Abstract: Zinc phosphide (Zn3P2) is a promising photovoltaic absorber for thin-film and flexible solar cells due to its earth-abundant composition and favourable optoelectronic properties. Recent advances in epitaxy have enabled the growth of high-quality Zn3P2 thin films despite the challenges posed by its incompatible lattice parameter and thermal expansion coefficient. However, Zn3P2 remains prone to intrinsic extended defects, such as rotated domains, that can limit device performance. Here, using (scanning) transmission electron microscopy, we identify a previously unreported class of extended defects that appear as planar faults described by displacement vectors lying in the (001) plane. Within a pseudo-cubic description of Zn3P2, we establish a direct correspondence between planar faults and rotated domains, showing that both arise from the flexible ordering of vacant sites in the Zn sublattice. First-principles calculations reveal an extremely low planar-defect formation energy of 2.5 mJ m-2, demonstrating that these defects form at essentially negligible energetic cost, in excellent agreement with their high experimentally observed occurrence. Additional density functional theory (DFT) calculations show that intrinsic planar defects neither introduce mid-gap electronic states nor significantly perturb the local electrostatic potential, indicating that they are electronically benign. Instead, we propose that planar defects indirectly degrade device performance by acting as preferential segregation sites for optically active point defects.
